# Wiki Index

The catalog of all pages in this wiki. Each entry: a wikilink to the page and a one-line summary. The LLM reads this first when answering queries to identify candidate pages.

Keep summaries tight â€” one line each. The index is engineered to be cheap to read; a fat index defeats its purpose.

When this file exceeds ~300 lines or the wiki passes ~150 pages, shard into `wiki/indexes/<type>.md` and replace this file with a directory of shards. See the `scaling-playbook.md` reference in the `llm-wiki` skill for the migration procedure.

---

- [[rna-dotbracket-001-evidence]] â€” evidence artifact for test unit RNA-DOTBRACKET-001 (Dot-Bracket / extended WUSS notation â€” **parse & validate** a structure string; the notation/representation layer of the RNA secondary-structure family): `RnaSecondaryStructure.ParseDotBracket` (structure string â†’ base pairs) + `ValidateDotBracket` (well-formedness). Algorithm: **one balanced-bracket stack per family** (shared stack would mis-pair `([)]`); a closer must match a same-family opener. Oracles â€” parse `((((....))))`â†’(0,11),(1,10),(2,9),(3,8), `([)]`â†’`(`:(0,2)+`[`:(1,3), `<<<<[[[[....>>>>]]]]` / `((((AAAA....))))aaaa`â†’two 4-bp crossing helices; validate `(((...)))`/`(([[]]))`/`([)]`â†’**true**, `(((...)` / `...)` / `)(` / `(]`â†’**false**. Two API-contract assumptions (malformed input â†’ best-effort parse dropping unmatched closers, gate with `ValidateDotBracket`; empty/null â†’ valid pair-free). No contradictions. New concept [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]].
- [[rna-energy-001-evidence]] â€” evidence artifact for test unit RNA-ENERGY-001 (**Free Energy Calculation**; the thermodynamic/energy layer of the RNA secondary-structure family): `RnaSecondaryStructure.CalculateStackingEnergy`/`CalculateStemEnergy`/`CalculateHairpinLoopEnergy`/`CalculateMinimumFreeEnergy`, the **Turner 2004 nearest-neighbor** free-energy terms summed into a fold's خ”Gآ° at 37 آ°C. Model `خ”Gآ°total = init + خ£stacking + خ£loops`. Key parameters â€” WC stacking **all negative** (GC-rich most stable, `GC/CG` âˆ’3.42, `GG/CC` âˆ’3.26; `AA/UU` âˆ’0.93); **G-U wobble variable, two positive** (`UG/GU` +0.30, `GU/UG` +1.29), note-a `GG/UU`=âˆ’0.5, note-b `5'GGUC/3'CUGG` special 3-stack total âˆ’4.12 (vs âˆ’1.77); **hairpin-loop init positive & non-monotonic** (3â†’5.4, 4â†’5.6, 6â†’5.4, 9â†’6.4, Jacobson-Stockmayer beyond 9); special UNCG/GNRA tri/tetra/hexaloop total energies; all-C loop penalty (3-nt +1.5 / >3-nt 0.3n+1.6); terminal mismatch (96); +0.45 per AU/GU end. Oracles GC 3-bp stem âˆ’5.78, NNDB hairpin example-1 `GGGAUAAAUCCC` âˆ’3.42, GGUC/CUGG âˆ’4.12; single base pair / empty / poly-A â†’ **خ”Gآ°=0** (stacking needs â‰¥2 adjacent pairs). No assumptions remain (all params = exact NNDB match); three **defined conditions** (37 آ°C, 2-dp precision, unknown stacksâ†’0.0). No contradictions. New concept [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]].
- [[rna-hairpin-001-evidence]] â€” evidence artifact for test unit RNA-HAIRPIN-001 (**Hairpin Loop and Stem Free-Energy Calculation**, Turner 2004 NN model): a focused deep-dive on `RnaSecondaryStructure.CalculateHairpinLoopEnergy` + `CalculateStemEnergy`, **not** a stem-loop enumerator and **not** miRNA-specific â€” it enriches the energy-layer concept [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]] (sibling of [[rna-energy-001-evidence]]) rather than defining a new one; distinct from the miRNA hairpin *finder* [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]]. Stem = per-stack stacking + **+0.45/AU-end**, P pairs â†’ **Pâˆ’1 stacks** (P â‰¤ 1 â‡’ 0). One display-precision item (2-dp intermediate rounding, tests assert `.Within(1e-9)`); no contradictions. **No new concept** â€” enriches [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]].

- [[rna-partition-001-evidence]] â€” evidence artifact for test unit RNA-PARTITION-001 (**RNA partition function (McCaskill) and Boltzmann structure probability** â€” the probabilistic/ensemble layer of the RNA secondary-structure family): the Boltzmann-weighted counterpart of MFE folding that computes the equilibrium partition function `Z`, per-base-pair binding probabilities, and the Boltzmann probability of a given structure. Invariants Z â‰¥ 1 (empty structure weight 1), P(i,j) âˆˆ [0,1] + symmetric, per-base pairing sum â‰¤ 1 (300 random seqs, max 0.983), monotone in E_bp; min-loop m forbids jâˆ’k â‰¤ m pairs, WC+GU only. - [[rna-pkpredict-001-evidence]] â€” evidence artifact for test unit RNA-PKPREDICT-001 (**Pseudoknot structure prediction â€” canonical H-type, pknotsRG class**; the **crossing-helix layer** of the RNA secondary-structure family, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): predict the optimal fold that may contain a single simple recursive pseudoknot (two **crossing** helices, `i<k<j<l` Antczak 2018) â€” the one feature the nested [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding|MFE]] / [[rna-partition-function-mccaskill|McCaskill]] predictors cannot represent. - [[rna-pkrecursive-001-evidence]] â€” evidence artifact for test unit RNA-PKRECURSIVE-001 (**Recursive pknotsRG pseudoknot prediction â€” nested / multiple / over-arching H-type knots**; the **recursive-grammar extension** of the single-knot RNA-PKPREDICT-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): predict the optimal fold that may contain **several** pseudoknots and knots **nested inside loops / over-arched by an enclosing helix**, filling exactly the PARTIAL-coverage gap the single-knot unit recorded. **Same pknotsRG class** (Reeder & Giegerich 2004/2007) â€” same Turner-NN energy on both helices, same penalties **initiation 9.0 / unpaired loop nt 0.3 / pair inside knot 0.0** kcal/mol, same canonization rules â€” but the three loops *u*/*v*/*w* now fold by the **same recursive folder** (a loop may contain a further knot), the top level **chains multiple knots**, and an enclosing helix may **over-arch** a knot. No contradictions. **Enriches** [[rna-pseudoknot-prediction]] (آ§6, the recursive extension of the single-knot concept â€” no new concept).
- [[rna-pseudoknot-001-evidence]] â€” evidence artifact for test unit RNA-PSEUDOKNOT-001 (**Pseudoknot detection** â€” identify **crossing** base pairs in a **given** structure; the detection/analysis facet of the RNA crossing-helix family, `RnaSecondaryStructure.DetectPseudoknots`): given a base-pair **set** (not a sequence), a pure **O(nآ²) combinatorial scan** reports every crossing pair-of-pairs `i<k<j<l`. Sources: **Antczak et al. 2018** *Bioinformatics* 34(8):1304 (rank 1 â€” crossing/conflict `i<j<i'<j'`, pseudoknot **order** = min base-pair-set decompositions to nested, DBL notation order 0 `()`/1 `[]`/2 `{}`/3 `<>`/4â€“8 letters, H-type `([)]`) + **Smit, Rother, Heringa & Knight 2008** *RNA* 14(3):410 (rank 1 â€” pseudoknot presence *requires* crossing pairs; order-assignment / pseudoknot-removal family) + **biotite.structure.pseudoknots** (rank 3 â€” crossing = not purely nestable; nested order 0 / knotted order 1+) + **Wikipedia Pseudoknot** (rank 4, cites Rivas & Eddy 1999). Crossing `i<k<j<l` = pseudoknot; two exhaustive negatives **nested** `i<k<l<j` + **disjoint** `j<k`. Oracles `([)]`=(0,2)+(1,3)â†’`0<1<2<3`â†’one pseudoknot, nested (0,5)+(1,4)â†’none, disjoint (0,2)+(3,5)â†’none. Invariants â‰¥2 pairs required / endpoints normalized min-max to open<close / deterministic / every reported knot satisfies `i<k<j<l`. **Distinct** from the energy-driven [[rna-pseudoknot-prediction]] predictor (pair set vs sequence, O(nآ²) scan vs O(nâپ´) energy DP) â€” it *is* the crossing primitive that predictor's validity invariant leans on. One scope note: pseudoknot-**order** grouping (DBL layering) Not Implemented (reports the binary crossing relations); no contradictions. **New concept** [[rna-pseudoknot-detection]] â€” the analysis-side sibling of the crossing-helix predictor.
- [[rna-stemloop-001-evidence]] â€” evidence artifact for test unit RNA-STEMLOOP-001 (**Stem-Loop (Hairpin) Detection**, area `RnaStructure`): the **enumeration layer** of the RNA secondary-structure family â€” `FindStemLoops(sequence, minStem, minLoop, maxLoop, allowWobble)` / `FindHairpins` **scan a sequence for every stem-loop** it can form (stem of antiparallel WC/wobble pairs + apical loop), an **O(nآ²آ·L)** scan distinct from the single-optimal [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding|MFE folder]], the hairpin *energy* unit [[rna-hairpin-001-evidence]], and the miRNA-specific [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]]. Sources: Wikipedia (Stem-loop / Tetraloop / Pseudoknot â€” loop **â‰¥3 nt** steric floor, optimal **4-8 nt**; UUCG+GNRA **~70%** of 16S-rRNA tetraloops) + Woese 1990 (PNAS 87:8467) + Antao 1991 (NAR 19:5901, **UUCG most stable**) + Heus & Pardi 1991 (Science 253:191) + Rivas & Eddy 1999 (pseudoknot alg) + NNDB Turner 2004 (tetraloop energetics). Tetraloop families **GNRA** (GAAA/GCAA/GGAA/GUAA) / **UNCG** (UACG/UCCG/UGCG/UUCG) / **CUUG**, ~3.0 kcal/mol bonus; `FindPseudoknots` flags crossing pairs `i<k<j<l` (same primitive as [[rna-pseudoknot-detection]]). Oracles `GGGAAAACCC`â†’`(((....)))` (3-bp stem + AAAA loop), `GGGCGAAAGCCC`â†’GNRA tetraloop, `AAAAâ€¦`/`GC`/`GCAUC`â†’none. Invariants non-overlap / â‰¤1 pair per base / contiguous loop / antiparallel stem; defaults wobble-on, minLoop 3, minStem 3. Limitations: no PK prediction from sequence, simplified energy, no internal loops/bulges, single structure. No contradictions. **New concept** [[rna-stem-loop-enumeration]].
- [[rna-struct-001-evidence]] â€” evidence artifact for test unit RNA-STRUCT-001 (**Secondary Structure Prediction**, area `RnaStructure`): the **top-level structure-prediction umbrella** on `RnaSecondaryStructure` â€” `Predict(sequence)` (a **Nussinov & Jacobson 1980** O(nآ³)/O(nآ²) base-pair-**maximizing** DP), `PredictWithConstraints` (forced base pairs, Mathews 2004), `ToDotBracket`/`FromDotBracket` (notation round-trip). - [[pop-hw-001-evidence]] â€” evidence artifact for test unit POP-HW-001 (Hardy-Weinberg equilibrium chi-square test; population-genetics POP-\* unit, **consumes** genotype counts from POP-FREQ-001): Wikipedia *Hardy-Weinberg principle* (Hardy 1908 / Weinberg 1908 â€” expected genotype freqs `f(AA)=pآ²`/`f(Aa)=2pq`/`f(aa)=qآ²`, Ford moth example, deviation causes, genotyping-error note) + Wikipedia *Chi-squared test* (Pearson goodness-of-fit `د‡آ²=خ£(Oâˆ’E)آ²/E`) + Emigh 1980 (chi-square comparison) + Wigginton et al. 2005 AJHG (**exact test** â€” cited as the out-of-scope alternative) sources; allele freq `p=(2آ·n_AA+n_Aa)/(2n)`/`q=1âˆ’p`, expected counts `E={pآ²n,2pqn,qآ²n}`, **df=1** (`#genotypesâˆ’#alleles=3âˆ’2`), p-value via chi-square CDF (lower-incomplete-gamma approx), default **خ±=0.05** critical 3.841; `TestHardyWeinberg` returns InEquilibrium/ChiSquare/PValue; oracles Ford moth (1469,138,5)â†’`pâ‰ˆ0.954`/`د‡آ²â‰ˆ0.83`â†’in-eq (HW-E01), perfect (25,50,25)â†’`د‡آ²=0` (HW-E02), excess-het (10,80,10)â†’`د‡آ²=36 â‰« 3.84`â†’out-of-eq (HW-E03), zero samplesâ†’InEquilibrium true/PValue 1 (HW-E04), fixed (100,0,0)â†’in-eq (HW-E05), all-het (0,100,0)â†’out-of-eq (HW-E06); edge cases **zero nâ†’PValue 1** (no evidence against Hâ‚€), **expected-0 term skipped** (div-by-zero guard); scope = biallelic chi-square goodness-of-fit only (no exact test, no multiallelic); no deviations/contradictions. Own concept [[hardy-weinberg-equilibrium-test]].
- [[pop-ld-001-evidence]] â€” evidence artifact for test unit POP-LD-001 (Linkage disequilibrium â€” `CalculateLD` (D, D', rآ²) + `FindHaplotypeBlocks`; population-genetics POP-\* unit, **consumes** allele/haplotype frequencies from POP-FREQ-001): Wikipedia *Linkage disequilibrium* (`D = p_AB âˆ’ p_Aآ·p_B`; Lewontin 1964 `D' = |D|/D_max` with sign-branched `D_max` clamped [0,1]; Hill & Robertson 1968 `rآ² = Dآ²/(p_Aآ·q_Aآ·p_Bآ·q_B)`; **diploid-frequency result** `R_AB = r_AB` (Wright 1933) â‡’ rآ² computable **without phase**) + Wikipedia *Haplotype block* (Gabriel 2002 / Patil 2001 threshold blocks) sources; implementation `rآ²` = squared Pearson correlation of 0/1/2 genotype dosage vectors `Covآ²/(Varآ·Var)`, `D` from diploid covariance `Cov=2D â‡’ D=Cov/2`; `FindHaplotypeBlocks` = simplified adjacent-pair Gabriel (consecutive `rآ² â‰¥ threshold`, default **0.7**, â‰¥2 variants); oracles perfect LD (identical vectors)â†’`rآ²â‰ˆ1`, no LD (balanced)â†’`rآ²â‰ˆ0`, anti-correlationâ†’`rآ²=1`/`D'=1` (sign-blind), block oracles singleâ†’none / two-highâ†’one / two-lowâ†’none / all-strongâ†’one span / non-contiguousâ†’multiple; INV `0â‰¤rآ²â‰¤1`, `0â‰¤|D'|â‰¤1`, block Startâ‰¤End/â‰¥2/non-overlapping/ordered, distance+IDs preserved; edge cases emptyâ†’`rآ²=0,D'=0`, monomorphic (zero variance/denominator)â†’`rآ²=0` (guarded), all-identicalâ†’`rآ²=0`; scope = two-biallelic-loci rآ²/D' + adjacent-pair blocks only (no full LD matrix, no phasing/EM, no decay-curve fit, no exact Gabriel CI); no deviations/contradictions. Own concept [[linkage-disequilibrium]].
- [[pop-select-001-evidence]] â€” evidence artifact for test unit POP-SELECT-001 (Selection-signature detection â€” `CalculateEhh`, `CalculateIHS`, `StandardizeIHS`, `ScanForSelection` = integrated Haplotype Score iHS; population-genetics POP-\* unit, **consumes** derived/ancestral allele freqs + MAF filter from POP-FREQ-001): Voight et al. 2006 PLoS Biol (**iHS = ln(iHH_A/iHH_D)** ancestral numerator, standardized to std-normal in derived-freq bins, integration truncated at **EHH<0.05**, scan = proportion `|iHS|>2` in ~50-SNP windows, **MAF>5%**) + Sabeti 2002 (EHH = homozygosity prob of two core-allele chromosomes) + selscan Szpiech & Hernandez 2014 (`EHH_c=خ£C(n_h,2)/C(n_c,2)`, trapezoidal iHH, **opposite sign convention** `ln(iHH_1/iHH_0)`) + rehh (worked SNP F1205400 `iHH_A=284429.9`/`iHH_D=2057107.4`â†’ln=**âˆ’1.978569274**, `limehh`/`freqbin`=0.05) sources; oracles constructed panel iHH_A=10/iHH_D=40â†’ln(0.25)=**âˆ’1.386294361** (long derived haplotypeâ†’negative iHS), EHH unit values 0.5/0.3333/1.0/0.0, balanced decayâ†’iHSâ‰ˆ0; INV EHHâˆˆ[0,1], single-element binâ†’std iHS 0, window value = count(|iHS|>2)/size; throws on monomorphic core / null / empty / inconsistent-length / invalid core allele / OOR coreIndex; assumptions (Nâˆ’1 SD, 20 default bins) affect magnitude only; scope = single-core iHS/EHH scan (no XP-EHH, no Fst-outlier/Tajima's-D scan, no genetic-map interpolation); no deviations/contradictions. Own concept [[selection-scan-ihs-ehh]].
- [[primer-tm-001-dimer-evidence]] â€” evidence artifact for test unit PRIMER-TM-001 (self-/hetero-dimer melting temperature; **first PCR-primer-design PRIMER-\* / MolTools unit**): SantaLucia & Hicks 2004 (unified DNA nearest-neighbour خ”Hآ°/خ”Sآ°, bimolecular Tm Eq. 3 with symmetry factor x=1 palindrome / x=4 otherwise, [Naâپ؛] entropy salt correction Eq. 5) + Untergasser 2012 Primer3 `ntthal` thermodynamic-alignment engine + `thal.c` reference constants + primer3-py 2.3.0 numeric oracle; the dimer DP now models the full possibly-non-contiguous optimum (internal mismatch/loop, bulge, `tstack2` terminal overhang), reproducing `calc_homodimer`/`calc_heterodimer` to machine precision (GCGCGCGC self x=1 Tm 40.0906 آ°C, TGCATGCATG/CATGCATGCA x=4 Tm 25.6596 آ°C, GCGCATGCGC 2أ—2 loop Tm 43.1572 آ°C); no stable dimer (poly-A) / invalid input â†’ null/NaN; deviations none remaining. - [[primer-tm-001-evidence]] â€” evidence artifact for the **base** test unit PRIMER-TM-001 (**Primer3 weighted per-primer penalty / objective function** â€” a *selection/scoring* algorithm, not a Tm calc, sibling of the dimer-Tm unit): Primer3 `libprimer3.cc` `p_obj_fn` (weighted sum of sign-gated one-sided deviations â€” Tm `temp_gtآ·(Tmâˆ’opt)`/`temp_ltآ·(optâˆ’Tm)`, GC% `gc_content_gt/lt`, size `length_gt/lt`, plus `compl_anyآ·self_any + compl_endآ·self_end + num_nsآ·#N`; **lower is better**, primers sorted ascending) + `libprimer3.h` (`DEFAULT_OPT_GC_PERCENT` undefined) + manual آ§19 + Untergasser 2012; defaults `opt_tm=60`/`opt_size=20`, weights `temp_*=length_*=1`, `gc/self/num_ns=0` â‡’ **default objective `|Tmâˆ’60|+|lenâˆ’20|`**; oracles (60,20)â†’0.0, (63,20)â†’3.0, (57,18)â†’5.0, combinedâ†’8.0; sign-gated (at optimum term=0), weight-zero short-circuit, penaltyâ‰¥0 (=0 iff all-optimal); `self_any`/`self_end` are caller-supplied `dpal` local-alignment scores (arithmetic exact, input external); no contradictions. - [[primer-tm-001-hairpin-evidence]] â€” evidence artifact for test unit PRIMER-TM-001 (**intramolecular hairpin self-folding MFE + unimolecular hairpin Tm** â€” the hairpin/secondary-structure extension of the primer-Tm unit; same ntthal/`thal.c` engine as the dimer): SantaLucia & Hicks 2004 (Table 1 unified DNA NN خ”Hآ°/خ”Sآ° reused verbatim as `NnUnifiedParams` stem stacks + **Table 4 hairpin-loop خ”Gآ°37 increments** 3â†’3.5â€¦30â†’6.3, loop خ”Hآ°=0 / loop خ”Sآ°=âˆ’خ”Gآ°37آ·1000/310.15, **unimolecular hairpin Tm Eq. 11 `Tm=خ”Hآ°آ·1000/خ”Sآ°âˆ’273.15` with NO `Rآ·ln(C_T/x)` concentration term**, Jacobson-Stockmayer large-loop Eq. 7 coeff 2.44, steric floor loops <3 nt, supplementary triloop/tetraloop + closing-Aآ·T +0.5 as opt-in caller increment) + SantaLucia 1998 NN cross-check + Vallone & Benight 1999 (hairpin Tm concentration-independent 0.5â€“260 آµM); hand-derived oracles `GGGCTTTTGCCC` (4-bp GGGC stem, TTTT loop) â†’ خ”Hآ°=âˆ’25.8, خ”Sآ°=âˆ’75.48486216346927, خ”Gآ°37=âˆ’2.3883700000000054, **Tm=68.6404 آ°C**, `GGGCAAAAAGCCC` (5-nt loop, 3.3) â†’ Tmâ‰ˆ71.585 آ°C, poly-A â†’ no hairpin (null)/NaN; assumptions bimolecular init & terminal-Aآ·T penalty excluded (unimolecular core, UNAFold-consistent); no contradictions. - [[primer-tm-001-nn-evidence]] â€” evidence artifact for test unit PRIMER-TM-001 (**per-oligo nearest-neighbour salt-corrected design Tm**, opt-in â€” the core خ”Hآ°/خ”Sآ°â†’Tm path + salt corrections, same SantaLucia model as the dimer/hairpin siblings): SantaLucia & Hicks 2004 (Table 1 unified NN خ”Hآ°/خ”Sآ°, Tm Eq. 3 with x=1/4 symmetry factor, p.419 worked example **Tm 35.8 آ°C**, Naâپ؛ entropy Eq. 5 `0.368آ·(N/2)آ·ln[Naâپ؛]` valid 0.05â€“1.1 M / â‰¤16 bp, Tables 2 & 3 mismatch/dangling cross-check) + **Owczarzy 2004** monovalent quadratic 1/Tm correction `(4.29آ·f(GC)âˆ’3.95)آ·1eâˆ’5آ·ln[Na]+9.40eâˆ’6آ·(ln[Na])آ²` (non-linear over 69 mMâ€“1.02 M) + **Owczarzy 2008** divalent Mgآ²âپ؛/dNTP 1/Tm correction (dNTP chelation Ka=3أ—10âپ´, mixed-regime reparam, falls back to monovalent) + Biopython `DNA_NN4`/`DNA_IMM`/`DNA_DE`/`Tm_NN`/`salt_correction` methods 5â€“7 (verbatim transcription of Allawi/SantaLucia/Peyret + Bommarito 2000 primaries â†’ `NnInternalMismatch`/`NnDanglingEnd`; complement-not-revcomp key convention mirrored in `CalculateNearestNeighborThermodynamicsMismatch`); oracles GCGCGC self x=1 Tm 35.0473, ATGCATGC x=4 Tm 30.4338, CGCGAATTCGCG 61.1452 (@1 M/0.5 آµM), Owczarzy vs Eq.5 @50 mM Na, CGTGAC/GCGCTG Tآ·G mismatch Tm âˆ’6.4061; assumptions default C_T=0.5 آµM + N=2آ·(lenâˆ’1); non-ACGT â†’ null/NaN; no contradictions. Enriches concept [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]].
- [[primer-tm-001-special-loop-evidence]] â€” evidence artifact for test unit PRIMER-TM-001 (**bundled special tri/tetraloop hairpin bonus tables** â€” the sequence-specific loop stability bonuses ntthal adds to a length-3/4 hairpin loop, now applied inside `calc_hairpin`, completing the opt-in increment the hairpin sibling flagged): libprimer3 `triloop.dh/.ds` (**16** entries, 5-char key incl. closing pair, خ”H âˆ’1500/âˆ’2000 by closing-pair family, **all خ”S=0**) + `tetraloop.dh/.ds` (**76** entries, 6-char key â†’ `NtthalHairpin.TetraloopTable`, e.g. CGAAAG خ”H=âˆ’1100 خ”S=0) + `thal.c` `calc_hairpin` (bonus **added** for loopSize==3/==4 via bsearch, key = full loop string incl. closing pair, خ”H cal/mol / خ”S cal/K/mol; loops.* size خ”Sآ°, unimolecular `Tm=mh/(ms+(N/2âˆ’1)آ·saltCorr)âˆ’273.15`) + SantaLucia & Hicks 2004 Eqs. 8â€“9 (model source) + primer3-py 2.3.0 oracles (tetraloop CGAAAG `GGGGCGAAAGCCCC` Tm 85.0335 آ°C, triloop CGAAG `GGGCGAAGCCC` Tm 84.7061 آ°C, non-special TTTT `GGGCTTTTGCCC` Tm 69.3995 آ°C unchanged, homopolymer/short â†’ structure_found=False); only 3/4-nt loops get a bonus, closing pair is part of the key, legacy `FindMostStableHairpin`+`loopBonusDeltaG37` path unchanged; assumptions none correctness-affecting (verbatim, machine-precision verified); no contradictions. Enriches concept [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]].
- [[probe-design-001-evidence]] â€” evidence artifact for test unit PROBE-DESIGN-001 (**TaqMan 5'-nuclease hydrolysis-probe design rules**, opt-in extension over the unchanged generic hybridization-probe designer; **first PROBE-\* unit**): Applied Biosystems / Thermo Fisher (rank 2, chemistry manufacturer) + PREMIER Biosoft (rank 3) + ScienceDirect "TaqMan" (5'-G quenching rationale) + IDT (corroborating) sources; the TaqMan-specific hard rules â€” **no G at the 5' end** (a 5'-G quenches the reporter *even after cleavage* â†’ hard rule, not a soft penalty; `SelectTaqManStrand` moves to the antisense strand when unavoidable), **more Cs than Gs**, **no run of â‰¥4 consecutive Gs** (separate from the generic homopolymer cap), **GC 30â€“80%**, **length 18â€“22 nt** (default, `minLength`/`maxLength` parameterised), **probe Tm â‰¥ primer Tm + 10 آ°C** (caller-supplied primer Tm; probe Tm via the PRIMER-TM-001-validated salt-adjusted `81.5+16.6آ·logâ‚پâ‚€[Naâپ؛]+41آ·GCâˆ’600/N` formula, not a TaqMan-specific NN calc); oracles CCATCACCCTACATCACC passes-all (primerTm â‰¤ 39.35), GCATCACCCTACATCACC fails 5'-G, ACCCCGGGGACCCTACAT fails GGGG-run, C=1/G=9 fails more-G-than-C, 16-nt fails len<18, GC 100% fails, sense GTTAGGGTTAGGGTTAGG â†’ RC CCTAACCCTAACCCTAAC strand-selection; two parameterisation assumptions (18â€“22 default window, repository salt-adjusted Tm engine), no source contradictions. Own concept [[taqman-probe-design-rules]].
- [[probe-design-001-lna-evidence]] â€” evidence artifact for the **LNA (locked nucleic acid) Tm-adjustment** variant of PROBE-DESIGN-001: an **LNA-adjusted nearest-neighbour Tm** that raises a probe's Tm/specificity (enabling shorter MGB-style 13â€“20 nt probes) by locking internal bases. Sources: **McTigue, Peterson & Kahn 2004** (*Biochemistry*, rank 1 â€” خ”خ”Hآ°/خ”خ”Sآ° increments for all **32** LNA+DNA:DNA nearest neighbours; internal LNA **raises Tm**), **MELTING 5** reference impl (`McTigue2004lockedmn.xml` verbatim table in **cal/mol** + `McTigue04LockedAcid.java` â€” **additive-increment** application and **terminal-LNA rejection**), rmelting worked example. Model: compute plain DNA NN خ”Hآ°/خ”Sآ° then **add** the McTigue increment per LNA-containing step, onto the library's SantaLucia-1998-unified DNA NN engine (same as PRIMER-TM-001 [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]]); terminal/non-ACGT/out-of-range â†’ not-computable. Oracle CCATTGCTACC (LNA@4) â†’ خ”Hآ° âˆ’80.014 / خ”Sآ° âˆ’216.6 â†’ LNA Tm **63.528 آ°C** vs all-DNA 59.692 (**خ”Tm +3.84 آ°C**), agreeing with MELTING `mct04` 63.614 to 0.086 آ°C (documented base-NN-set residual; increments applied exactly). Enriches [[taqman-probe-design-rules]] (LNA section).
- [[probe-valid-001-evidence]] â€” evidence artifact for test unit PROBE-VALID-001 (**hybridization-probe validation / off-target specificity scan** â€” a **gapped Smithâ€“Waterman local alignment** of the candidate probe against a pooled reference, replacing an earlier ungapped Hamming scan; the **specificity-checking sibling** of PROBE-DESIGN-001, a genuinely distinct algorithm): Smith & Waterman 1981 (local-alignment recurrence with the **zero floor** â†’ local, indel-aware; traceback stops at 0 so a mismatched tail is trimmed), Altschul et al. 1990/1997 BLAST (the **gapped-vs-ungapped** improvement â€” a single gapped alignment finds indel off-targets the ungapped HSPs miss; the unit realizes the *gapped local alignment* property, an **exact** full SW scan, not seed-and-extend or a genome-scale index), Karlin & Altschul 1990 / Altschul 1990 statistics (opt-in `ComputeLambdaNucleotide`/`ComputeKarlinAltschul`: `E=Kآ·mآ·nآ·e^(âˆ’خ»S)`, خ» = root of `خ£ p_i p_j e^(خ» s_ij)=1`, bit score `S'=(خ»Sâˆ’ln K)/ln 2`, `E=mآ·nآ·2^(âˆ’S')`; preconditions expected-score<0 **and** a positive score; K caller-supplied), Kane et al. 2000 (empirical **>75% identity** cross-hybridization threshold, `minIdentity` default 0.75, caller-configurable; <14â€“15 contiguous-complement caveat); oracles â€” probe `ACGTACGTACGT` vs an indel copy `ACGTACTGTACGT` aligns `ACGTAC-GTACGT` 12/12 identity 1.0 `HasGaps=true` (**found by gapped, missed by ungapped Hamming maxMismatches=3**); indel+mismatch `ACGTACTGTACTT` â†’ SW trims `TT` tail â†’ 10/12 = 0.8333 (admitted @0.75, rejected @0.90); خ» for +1/âˆ’3 uniform-0.25 = **1.3740631** (â‰ˆ blastn 1.37, expected score âˆ’2.0<0), K=0.711/S=30/m=20/n=1000 â†’ bit **59.9627**, **E=1.7802eâˆ’14**, Eâ†“ in S and linear in mآ·n; BLAST DNA scoring +2/âˆ’3 gap âˆ’2. ASSUMPTION: on-target = first perfect ungapped full-coverage exact match (API/labelling, not a sourced constant); no source contradictions. Own concept [[probe-offtarget-specificity-scan]].

## Concepts

- [[three-front-doors]] â€” one algorithm engine exposed through skills, the C# API, and MCP, with identical results.
- [[skill-layer]] â€” the Agent-Skill routing + discipline layer that keeps 427 tool schemas out of the model's context.
- [[layered-architecture]] â€” the strict up-only dependency layering (Levels 0â€“4) enforced by architecture tests.
- [[scientific-rigor]] â€” runtime honesty: `LimitationPolicy`, tool-only computation, provenance on every result.
- [[validation-and-testing]] â€” 22k+ tests across ten methodologies plus the per-unit validation campaign.
- [[property-based-testing]] â€” P0 methodology (FsCheck): hundreds of generated inputs checked against expressible invariants (R/S/I/M/P/RT/D); 258/258.
- [[metamorphic-testing]] â€” P0 methodology: metamorphic relations across runs (SUB/MON/INV/SYM/COMP/SHIFT) that solve the oracle problem; 258/258, ~200+ relations.
- [[fuzzing]] â€” P2 methodology: random/malformed/boundary input for clean-failure; parsers the hot target; zeroâ†’258/258.
- [[snapshot-testing]] â€” P1 methodology (Verify): golden-master `.verified.txt` regression capture; the least-complete methodology at 37/255.
- [[algebraic-testing]] â€” P1 methodology: explicit algebraic laws (identity/associativity/involution/round-tripâ€¦); 89 applicable + 169 not-applicable.
- [[architecture-testing]] â€” P2 methodology (ArchUnitNET): 22 IL-level module rules enforcing the [[layered-architecture]] Dependency Rule; scales by module not algorithm.
- [[differential-testing]] â€” P2 methodology: two independent implementations cross-checked (ALT/BRUTE/REF/DUAL); 107/255.
- [[combinatorial-testing]] â€” P3 methodology: minimal pairwise parameter-interaction coverage; 193/255 + 65 not-applicable.
- [[characterization-testing]] â€” P3 methodology: golden-master pinning of behaviour before refactors (invariance, not correctness); on-demand.
- [[build-quality-gate]] â€” the build-time static-analysis gate: SonarAnalyzer ratcheted to blocking under `TreatWarningsAsErrors`, fix-or-silence, review-not-blind-fix.
- [[test-unit-registry]] â€” the area-prefixed Test Unit ID scheme and per-unit record behind the validation effort.
- [[definition-of-done]] â€” the six-criterion acceptance bar (TestSpec, tests, â‰¥80% coverage, edge cases, CI, evidence) each unit must clear.
- [[algorithm-validation-evidence]] â€” the templated per-unit `docs/Evidence/` artifact pattern (sources, worked-example dataset, deviations) behind the "Evidence documented" DoD criterion.
- [[global-alignment-needleman-wunsch]] â€” the canonical DP global-alignment algorithm (`GlobalAlign`): linear-gap recurrence, O(nm), traceback, affine-as-extension.
- [[multiple-sequence-alignment]] â€” aligning 3+ sequences (NP-complete): Seqeron's star (`MultipleAlign`), iterative-refinement (MUSCLE), and consistency (T-Coffee) aligners; sum-of-pairs + consensus.
- [[semi-global-alignment-fitting]] â€” ends-free "glocal" alignment: fitting/query-in-reference variant (Rosalind SIMS); NW recurrence with free reference end gaps, traceback from max of last row.
- [[alignment-statistics]] â€” post-alignment metrics: percent identity/similarity/gaps (EMBOSS/BLAST convention, denominator includes gaps, positive-score â‡’ similar) and srspair three-line markup.
- [[coding-potential-hexamer-score]] â€” CPAT hexamer usage-bias coding-potential score: mean of ln(coding/noncoding) over in-frame hexamers (wordSize 6/step 3), sign convention, آ±1 pseudo-scores; Fickett TESTCODE as not-implemented alternative.
- [[relative-synonymous-codon-usage]] â€” RSCU (Sharp & Li 1986) codon-usage-bias measure: n_iآ·x/خ£x normalization, 1.0=no bias, bounded [0,n_i], خ£-over-family=n_i invariant; pooled counts, sense codons only; base anchor of the codon-usage family (vs CAI's max-normalization).
- [[codon-adaptation-index]] â€” CAI (Sharp & Li 1987) whole-gene codon-bias / expression-proxy score in [0,1]: geometric mean of relative adaptiveness w=f/max_synonym_f, low-value-sensitive, stop excluded; dual include/exclude-Met/Trp mode (exclude can give L=0â†’0); E. coli oracles; Seqeron deviation = 1e-6 zero-freq clamp (vs Sharp & Li's 0.5 reference-table pseudocount); one level above RSCU.
- [[rare-codon-analysis]] â€” codon-usage family's *localization/diagnostic* unit (`FindRareCodons` + cluster addendum): a codon is rare when its per-family frequency < threshold (default 0.15), reports position/AA/frequency (E. coli AGA 0.04/AGG 0.02/CGA 0.06/CUA 0.04); addendum adds two published cluster methods â€” Clarke & Clark 2008 %MinMax (18-codon window, signed %Min/%Max âˆˆ[âˆ’100,+100], rare clusters = negative peaks) and Chartier 2012 Sherlocc (7-codon window, â‰¥4 of 7 freqâ‰¤threshold "slow" positions = a rare-codon cluster); single-codon-AA contributes 0 to %MinMax (no NaN), overlapping windows merged; feeds [[codon-optimization]]'s AvoidRareCodons; oracles âˆ’86.36/+100/+36.47% and 7أ—AGAâ†’1 cluster; deviations None.
- [[codon-usage-comparison]] â€” codon-usage family's *raw* end (`CalculateCodonUsage` + `CompareCodonUsage`): unnormalized codon-count table (non-overlapping triplets, Tâ†’U, drop partial codon, Dictionary<codon,int>, خ£counts=total invariant) + Total Variation Distance similarity `1âˆ’خ£|fâ‚پâˆ’fâ‚‚|/2 âˆˆ [0,1]` between two codon-frequency distributions; proven identity 1.0 / symmetry / range [0,1] / disjointâ†’0 / partial-overlap-exact properties; emptyâ†’0, TVD-not-cosine deliberate metric choice; Kazusa-verified organism tables; shares RSCU's counting primitive, the distribution-comparison op none of the bias measures provide.
- [[codon-optimization]] â€” codon-usage family's CDS-*rewriting* operation (`OptimizeSequence`): synonymous substitution to improve host expression; five strategies (MaximizeCAI / BalancedOptimization 40-60% GC / HarmonizeExpression=Mignon 2018 / AvoidRareCodons / MinimizeSecondaryâ†’ReduceSecondaryStructure); invariants protein-preservation + Met/AUG & Trp/UGG fixed + stop preserved + CAIâˆˆ(0,1]; RNA notation, Tâ†’U, trim-to-codon, 1e-6 CAI clamp; E. coli/yeast/human preferred-codon fixtures; actuator to RSCU/CAI/ENC's measurement.
- [[effective-number-of-codons]] â€” ENC/Nc (Wright 1990) reference-free whole-gene codon-bias measure in [20,61]: reciprocal of codon homozygosity Fج‚=(nآ·خ£pآ²âˆ’1)/(nâˆ’1) aggregated by degeneracy class (Nc=2+9/Fج‚â‚‚+1/Fج‚â‚ƒ+5/Fج‚â‚„+3/Fج‚â‚†); 20=max bias / 61=uniform, unbiasedâ†’61, no-bias-simâ†’40.5; Ile absentâ†’(Fج‚â‚‚+Fج‚â‚„)/2 fallback, overshoot re-adjusts to 61; reference-free counterpart of CAI; one assumption = non-source-prescribed lower clamp at 20.
- [[repetitive-element-detection]] â€” repeats/tandem family anchor: tandem (head-to-tail, â‰¥2 copies, primitive unit), inverted (Wآ·Gآ·Wج„ل´؟ / zero-gap palindrome, IUPACpal), and RepeatMasker-class assignment; ClassifyRepeat = exact-substring containment, not Smith-Waterman homology.
- [[consensus-sequence]] â€” assembly CONSENSUS family anchor: column-wise majority/threshold consensus (Biopython dumb_consensus rule) â€” gaps skipped, emit iff unique max and freq â‰¥ threshold else ambiguous, tieâ†’ambiguous, all-gapâ†’N no div-by-zero; N/0.5 parameterized defaults; shared with MSA consensus step.
- [[consensus-from-alignment]] â€” Motif-Analysis consensus-from-a-multiple-alignment (MOTIF-CONS-001, `MotifFinder.CreateConsensusFromAlignment`): pure most-frequent (plurality) column consensus over equal-length aligned strings, deterministic alphabetical tie-break (A<C<G<T), no threshold (always emits); Rosalind CONS `ATGCAACT` oracle; `alternative_to` the threshold/tieâ†’ambiguous assembly [[consensus-sequence]], motif-family sibling of the exact [[known-motif-search]].
- [[iupac-degenerate-consensus]] â€” MotifFinder degenerate-consensus unit (MOTIF-GENERATE-001, `MotifFinder.GenerateConsensus`): collapses equal-length aligned columns into an IUPAC-ambiguity-coded string â€” per column keep every base with `count > 0.25آ·n` (strict `>`), emit the NC-IUB 1984 symbol for that base set (R/Y/S/W/K/M, B/D/H/V, N), no-pass fallback â†’ most-frequent (alphabetical tie); DECIPHER threshold-consensus family + NC-IUB/UCSC/Wikipedia bijective setâ†’symbol table; `A,A,G,G,C`â†’R / strict-`>` boundary / four-wayâ†’A-fallback oracles; `alternative_to` the plurality [[consensus-from-alignment]], degenerate sibling of the exact [[known-motif-search]] and de-novo [[overrepresented-kmer-discovery]].
- [[regulatory-element-detection]] â€” Motif-Discovery regulatory-element unit (MOTIF-REGULATORY-001, `KnownMotifs` catalog scan): matches a **fixed, cited catalog of 12 canonical regulatory consensus elements** (TATA/âˆ’10/âˆ’35/CAAT/GC promoter boxes, Kozak + Shine-Dalgarno translation signals, poly(A), and E-box/AP-1/NF-خ؛B/CREB TF sites) against a DNA sequence, reporting each occurrence's Name/Pattern/Sequence at its 0-based start; mixes exact and one IUPAC-degenerate (E-box `CANNTG`) match; anchors the AP-1 corrected-consensus regression (`TGAGTCA`â†’`TGACTCA`, `AATGAGTCAGG`â†’0 hits); two source-backed representative-site assumptions (NF-خ؛B `GGGACTTTCC`, Kozak `GCCGCCACCATGG`); the curated-biological-catalog specialization of the generic exact [[known-motif-search]], distinct from the generation-direction [[iupac-degenerate-consensus]] and de-novo [[overrepresented-kmer-discovery]].
- [[overrepresented-kmer-discovery]] â€” Motif-Discovery de-novo unit (MOTIF-DISCOVER-001, `MotifFinder.DiscoverMotifs`): finds **unknown** over-represented motifs by enumerating every length-`k` k-mer, counting overlapping occurrences, and ranking by observed/expected enrichment `Count/((Nâˆ’k+1)/4^k)` under a zero-order i.i.d. uniform background (Compeau & Pevzner); deterministic exact single-pass, 0-based positions; `ATGC` in `ATGCATGCATGC` k=4 â†’ 768/9â‰ˆ85.333, `AAA` in `AAAAAAAAAA` k=3 â†’ 64.0 oracles; `k>N`â†’empty, minCount presentation-only, zero-order-only + no-p-value simplifications; the de-novo inverse of the exact [[known-motif-search]] and distinct from the [[consensus-from-alignment]] plurality consensus.
- [[shared-motifs]] â€” Motif-Discovery cross-sequence unit (MOTIF-SHARED-001, `FindSharedMotifs`): the van Helden / RSAT oligo-analysis **"matching sequences"** quorum â€” enumerate every fixed-`k` exact word across a *set* of sequences and report each word present in â‰¥ `minSequences` of them (each carrying its `SequenceIndices` set + `Prevalence`=matching/total); a within-sequence repeat counts **1** (presence/absence, not multiplicity); exact-word only (no degenerate/substitution); the cross-sequence sibling of the single-sequence O/E [[overrepresented-kmer-discovery]] and `alternative_to` the fixed-k-quorum-vs-single-longest LCSM framing of [[longest-common-substring]] (returns all qualifying words, not one longest present in all).
- [[approximate-pattern-matching-mismatches]] â€” pattern-matching PAT-APPROX family anchor (PAT-APPROX-003): Hamming-distance **approximate matching** â€” a `k`-mer appears with â‰¤`d` mismatches when `HammingDistance(P,P')â‰¤d` (BA1H); `Count_d`/`FindApproximateOccurrences` scan windows, `FindFrequentKmersWithMismatches` (BA1I) ranks `k`-mers by their **d-neighborhood** (Hamming-ball) tally so the winner need not occur exactly, `Neighbors` (BA1N) enumerates the ball (includes identity), `FindBestMatch` returns the leftmost min-Hamming window; oracles {GATG,ATGC,ATGT} count 5, {6,7,26,27,78}, Count_1=4, ACG/1â†’10; d=0 degenerates to exact so it is the mismatch-tolerant `alternative_to` [[k-mer-positions]] and the fuzzy sibling of the exact [[known-motif-search]] / de-novo [[overrepresented-kmer-discovery]]; substitution-only (no indels â€” that is the alignment family), deviations none.
- [[coverage-depth-calculation]] â€” assembly COVER family anchor: per-base sequencing depth over a reference (count of placed reads spanning each position, exact); average depth = خ£depth/G = Lander-Waterman C=LN/G, breadth = covered/G = 1âˆ’e^âˆ’c; boundary-clip + empty-input rules; ACGTTGCAATâ†’1.5/1.0 oracle; Poisson (e^âˆ’c gap) as a property check only; read placement (minOverlap best-match) out of scope.
- [[de-bruijn-graph-assembly]] â€” assembly DBG family anchor: k-mer graph (distinct (k-1)-mers = nodes, each k-mer = one prefixâ†’suffix edge, directed multigraph) + Eulerian-walk reconstruction (balanced/semi-balanced, Euler theorems 8.1/8.2, O(|E|) Hierholzer); spelling = path[0]+last char of each node; unique-walk oracles only (AAABBBA, a_longâ€¦, to_everyâ€¦ k=4, ATGGCGTGCA); repeat/gap/error â†’ non-Eulerian; walk-selection unspecified so exact asserts on unique-walk inputs; OLC is the alternative formulation.
- [[overlap-layout-consensus-assembly]] â€” assembly OLC family anchor: the three-stage Overlap-Layout-Consensus paradigm (`FindAllOverlaps` + `AssembleOLC`) â€” overlap graph (read=node, edge on longest suffix-of-A/prefix-of-B â‰¥ threshold), Layout = Hamiltonian path (NP-complete) + transitive reduction + non-branching contigs, Consensus = majority vote; GTACGTACGAT 12-edge / 5-overlap-tiling oracles; suffix-tree O(N+a) vs all-pairs O(Nآ²); NP-complete/repeat-split/greedy-suboptimal failure modes; identity-1.0 + empty-input assumptions; Hamiltonian/overlap-graph alternative to DBG's Eulerian/k-mer formulation.
- [[contig-merge-overlap-collapse]] â€” assembly MERGE family anchor: suffixâ€“prefix overlap collapse primitive (`MergeContigs`) behind greedy SCS and OLC layout; overlap = length-l suffix of X = prefix of Y, longest match reported, collapse keeps one copy so |merge|=|c1|+|c2|âˆ’l; overlap 0 / out-of-range â†’ plain concatenation; BAA+AABâ†’BAAB, chainâ†’AAABBBA oracles; caller-trusts-length + out-of-rangeâ†’concat API-contract assumptions; overlap-based sibling of DBG's k-mer/Eulerian formulation.
- [[scaffolding]] â€” assembly SCAFFOLD family anchor: joining ordered contigs into a scaffold, adjacent contigs separated by `N`-runs of length = the (upstream) inter-contig distance estimate (ABySS 2.0 rule); positive gap `g` â†’ `g`أ—`N`, scaffold length = خ£|contig|+خ£gap; non-positive (zero/negative) estimate â†’ AGP unknown-size default 100 N (negative = overlap, unresolved here); each contig in â‰¤1 scaffold, unlinked â†’ singleton; parameterized fill char; ACGTNNNTTGGNNCCAA / AAAA+100N+TTTT oracles; downstream of DBG/OLC/merge, hands off to contig-merge on the negative-gap overlap case; 100-constant source-backed (INSDC), only the fall-back-not-resolve decision is assumed.
- [[assembly-statistics]] â€” assembly STATS family anchor: contiguity/QC summary metrics over contig lengths (read-only, downstream of DBG/OLC/merge/scaffold) â€” Nx = shortest length covering â‰¥x% (largest-first, inclusive â‰¥; N50/N90), Lx = the matching contig count, N90 â‰¤ N50 / L90 â‰¥ L50, auN = خ£Lلµ¢آ²/خ£Lâ±¼ (area under Nx curve, more stable than N50); + totals/largest/smallest/GC and 0-based inclusive N-run gaps; Miller 2010 + Wikipedia + QUAST + Heng Li 2020; Assembly A N50 70/L50 2, auN 73.333 oracles; emptyâ†’zeros (not None) + upper-median-not-source-derived assumptions.
- [[quality-trimming-running-sum]] â€” assembly TRIM family anchor: BWA/cutadapt running-sum quality trimming â€” subtract cutoff from each Phred quality, take partial sums to the 3' end, cut at the minimum (= BWA argmax of accumulated thresholdâˆ’q, with `s<0` early break + `BWA_MIN_RDLEN=35` floor); Phred+33 decode (Cock 2010); `KI;<)(,%#$`@thr 10â†’first 4 bases oracle; threshold<1 disables / all-high unchanged / all-low dropped / good-base-among-bad refinement; both-end pass + downstream minLength filter as assumptions; read-QC preprocessing upstream of correction/DBG/OLC.
- [[kmer-spectrum-error-correction]] â€” assembly CORRECT family anchor: two-sided k-mer-spectrum read error correction (Musket/Quake) â€” trusted (multiplicity > cut-off) vs untrusted k-mers, base trusted if covered by any trusted k-mer, unique alternative making all covering k-mers trusted, ambiguity/no-setâ†’unchanged; substitution-only (count+length preserved); kmerSize=15/minKmerFrequency=2 non-behavioral defaults.
- [[centromere-analysis]] â€” chromosome centromere/alpha-satellite family anchor (second Chromosome-analysis unit): `AnalyzeCentromere` + 4 additive detectors â€” Levan 1964 q/p arm-ratio classes (Metacentric â‰¤1.7 / Submetacentric â‰¤3.0 / Subtelocentric <7.0 / Acrocentric â‰¥7.0 / Telocentric p=0); alpha-satellite-specific `DetectAlphaSatellite`/`FindCenpBBoxes` (171-bp tandem period آ±5, AT>0.5, 17-bp CENP-B box `YTTCGTTGGAARCGGGA`, no embedded monomer); `DetectHigherOrderRepeat` (HOR period = smallest k with monomers k apart â‰¥95% identical across â‰¥90%, intra-HOR 50â€“70% vs inter-HOR 97â€“100%); `AssignSuprachromosomalFamily` (bundled CC0 Dfam ALR/ALRa=A/ALRb=B, SF3 pentameric/SF4 monomeric/{SF1,SF2} dimeric/SF5 irregular); base AlphaSatelliteContent is density-heuristic-not-specific + SF1/SF2-unresolved (non-redistributable consensus library) limitations.
- [[karyotype-analysis]] â€” chromosome karyotyping/ploidy-detection family anchor (third Chromosome-analysis unit): `AnalyzeKaryotype` builds a karyotype from chromosome descriptors (split sex/autosome, group by base name, count copies, compare to expected ploidy, label nullisomy..pentasomy by absolute count; TotalChromosomes/TotalGenomeSize/MeanChromosomeLength invariants) and `DetectPloidy` estimates whole-genome ploidy from read depth (true-median ratio â†’ round(ratioأ—2) clamped [1,8], confidence 1âˆ’|ratioأ—2âˆ’ploidy|أ—2, emptyâ†’(2,0)); Down/Turner + diploid/tetraploid/haploid oracles; DD4 nullisomy-unreachable-via-GroupBy, DD5 disomy-only-aneuploid-in-polyploid; deviations None. Descriptor-count sibling of depth-log-ratio [[aneuploidy-detection]].
- [[synteny-and-rearrangement-detection]] â€” shared synteny anchor (fourth Chromosome-analysis unit; comparative-genomics COMPGEN-SYNTENY will reuse it): `FindSyntenyBlocks` builds syntenic blocks from ortholog pairs (group by chr pair, sort by ref position, collinear runs merged under maxGap, emit â‰¥minGenes; block carries strand '+'/'-', GeneCount, SequenceIdentity=NaN for coordinate-only input per MCScanX; I1â€“I5) + `DetectRearrangements` classifies adjacent-block signals (diff target chrâ†’Translocation, same chr diff strandâ†’Inversion, gap asymmetryâ†’Deletion, overlapping source diff targetsâ†’Duplication); forward/inverted-block + translocation(50000)/inversion(size 10000) oracles; empty/below-minGenes/maxGap-split/multi-pair edge cases; MCScanX/SyRI/MUMmer + Wikipedia; deviations None.
- [[telomere-analysis]] â€” chromosome telomere family anchor (fifth Chromosome-analysis unit): telomere repeat detection + length estimation â€” 3â€² end forward TTAGGG / 5â€² end reverse-complement CCCTAA (6-bp vertebrate unit, Meyne 1989), configurable 70%-per-window purity so imperfect repeats accepted (5/6 for 6-bp, 5/7 for Arabidopsis TTTAGGG; divergent TTAGGAâ†’0.833), purityâˆˆ[0,1] tracked with length; length direct from run or qPCR T/S ratio (Cawthon 2002) EstimatedLength=referenceLengthأ—(tsRatio/referenceRatio); IsCriticallyShort=(hasTelomere&&length<criticalLength)OR empty; criticalLength 3000 / minTelomereLength 500 / searchLength(truncates) / referenceLength 7000 configurable defaults not biological constants; Wikipedia/Meyne/Cawthon/Blackburn-Gall sources; deviations None. Sibling of [[aneuploidy-detection]].
- [[conserved-gene-clusters-common-intervals]] â€” comparative-genomics common-interval / conserved-cluster unit: a conserved gene cluster = a gene-label SET contiguous in EVERY genome (order- and strand-free inside the window), the common-interval model (Uno & Yagiura 2000, Heber & Stoye 2001 k-permutation O(kn+z), Bui-Xuan/Habib/Paul 2013 unifying view, Didier et al. 2013 sequences-with-duplicates/paralogs); interval size â‰¥2 (singletons excluded), whole set (1..n) trivially common, meaningful only for Kâ‰¥2; Seqeron does the strict O(nآ²آ·K) check with minClusterSize filter; strict gap-free model â€” maxGap retained for API/MCP back-compat only and does NOT relax it, gene-teams gapped extension (Bergeron 2002) not implemented; golden vector Idâ‚‡ vs (7 2 1 3 6 4 5) â†’ {1,2}/{1,2,3}/{3,4,5,6}/{4,5}/{4,5,6}/{1..6} + trivial {1..7}, split-negative {2,3}, duplicates T/S â†’ {1,2,3,4}; order-free sibling of [[synteny-and-rearrangement-detection]] and [[average-nucleotide-identity]]; deviations None.
- [[average-nucleotide-identity]] â€” comparative-genomics ANI family anchor (first COMPGEN unit): the ANIb genome-similarity metric (Goris 2007) that operationalizes the prokaryotic species boundary (ANIâ‰ˆ95%â†”70% DDH) â€” fragment query into 1020 nt pieces, best-match place each against the reference (`CalculateAni`), keep fragments >30% identity over â‰¥70% alignable (both recalculated over the query-fragment length), average the qualifying per-fragment identities; gapped Smith-Waterman placement recovers indels (`gapped:true`), reciprocal/symmetric ANI = mean of both directions (`CalculateReciprocalAni`, order-independent); null/emptyâ†’0, non-positive fragmentLength throws; engine decision = SequenceAligner.LocalAlign (full DP, BLAST DNA scoring) not NCBI-BLASTN, indel handling correct; sibling of [[synteny-and-rearrangement-detection]] in the COMPGEN family; deviations None.
- [[dot-plot-word-match]] â€” comparative-genomics visual pairwise-comparison unit (`COMPGEN-DOTPLOT-001`): the word-match / k-tuple dot matrix (Gibbs & McIntyre 1970 â†’ EMBOSS `dottup`) â€” dot at (x,y) iff the length-`wordSize` word at x in seq1 exactly matches the word at y in seq2 (case-insensitive, x=seq1/y=seq2, all overlapping occurrences via suffix tree), diagonals = similarity / main diagonal = self-comparison / repeats = extra diagonals / indels break the diagonal; `wordSize` (EMBOSS default 10) noise-vs-sensitivity trade-off (longer=less noise/less sensitive), `stepSize` x-subsampling; exact-match `dottup` not scored `dotmatcher`; AGCGT/AT k=1â†’{(0,0),(4,1)}, ACGTACGT self wordSize4â†’{(0,0),(0,4),(1,1),(2,2),(3,3),(4,0),(4,4)}, ACGT self main-diagonal oracles; word>seq/null/empty/disjointâ†’no dots, non-positive wordSize/stepSize throws; sibling of ANI/synteny/conserved-clusters; orientation + case-insensitivity assumptions, deviations None.
- [[ortholog-detection-reciprocal-best-hits]] â€” comparative-genomics ortholog & in-paralog detection unit (`COMPGEN-ORTHO-001`): orthologs by Reciprocal Best Hits (RBH â€” each gene the other's best hit across two genomes, Moreno-Hagelsieb 2008 / Tatusov 1997 / Fitch 1970 speciation-vs-duplication), recent (in-)paralogs by within-genome mutual best hits (Remm 2001); best hit=max-similarity with deterministic tie-break, reciprocity mandatory (one-directional best hit is NOT an ortholog = the guarded defect), â‰¥50% coverage + min-similarity gates, partial-matching output, emptyâ†’no orthologs / single-geneâ†’no paralogs; reciprocity/non-reciprocity(RBH count 1)/in-paralog oracles; one assumption = alignment-free 5-mer Jaccard replaces BLAST bit-score ranking (reciprocity/coverage/threshold source-backed); shared anchor for COMPGEN-RBH-001, the core/shared-gene sub-unit of [[genome-comparison-core-dispensable]]; sibling of ANI/synteny/conserved-clusters/dot-plot; deviations None.
- [[genome-rearrangement-breakpoint-distance]] â€” comparative-genomics signed-permutation / breakpoint rearrangement-detection unit (`COMPGEN-REARR-001` + `COMPGEN-REVERSAL-001`): the Hannenhalliâ€“Pevzner/Bafnaâ€“Pevzner theory â€” signed permutation (strand=sign), extended `(0,â€¦,n+1)` (endpoints=telomeres), breakpoint = consecutive pair where neither `(x,y)` nor `(âˆ’y,âˆ’x)` survives in خ², `b(خ±)` count = `d_BP=nâˆ’sim(common adjacencies)`, reversal-distance lower bound `dâ‰¥b/2`; `ClassifyRearrangement` â†’ Inversion (reversal = sign-flip + local reverse) vs Transposition (block move preserving orientation), Translocation/Deletion/Insertion/Duplication "Not implemented" (single permutation can't express them); Hunter `(âˆ’2,âˆ’3,+1,+6,âˆ’5,âˆ’4)`â†’b=6/dâ‰¥3, identityâ†’0, single-inversion `(+1,âˆ’4,âˆ’3,âˆ’2,+5)`â†’b=2 oracles; `bâˆˆ[0,n+1]` invariant; the signed-permutation `alternative_to` the block-signal [[synteny-and-rearrangement-detection]], sibling of ANI/ortholog/clusters/dot-plot; deviations None.
- [[genome-comparison-core-dispensable]] â€” comparative-genomics end-to-end pipeline (`CompareGenomes`): partitions each genome's genes into core (conserved = RBH ortholog pairs, Tettelin 2005 pan-genome) vs dispensable (genome-specific = the rest), reports Conserved/Specific1/Specific2 + OverallSynteny=(genes in MCScanX syntenic blocks)/min(|g1|,|g2|) clamped â‰¤1; symmetric partition, emptyâ†’all-0; orchestrates RBH ortholog detection (COMPGEN-RBH-001) + synteny (COMPGEN-SYNTENY-001); sibling of [[average-nucleotide-identity]] & [[conserved-gene-clusters-common-intervals]]; two source-backed assumptions (alignment-free RBH gate, MCScanX â‰¥5-anchor block threshold â†’ OverallSynteny can be 0 with conserved orthologs); deviations None.
- [[morf-prediction-dip-in-disorder]] â€” protein-disorder family MoRF unit (DISORDER-MORF-001, second DISORDER-* unit): Molecular Recognition Feature prediction by the "dip within disorder" heuristic (Oldfield 2005 / Cheng-Oldfield PMC2570644 / Mohan 2006) â€” a short ordered run (per-residue TOP-IDP disorder score <0.5) of total length 10â€“70 flanked on both sides by disorder (score â‰¥0.5) = one MoRF; 0.5 order/disorder threshold, خ±/خ²/خ¹ bound-state sub-types (Mohan 2006), MoRF scoreâˆˆ[0,1] rising with dip depth; terminal dip / fully-ordered / fully-disordered / out-of-band â†’ none; TOP-IDP normalized `(raw+0.884)/1.871` per-residue score from `PredictDisorder`; one assumption = exact flank-length params paywalled â†’ qualitative criterion (threshold/band/shape source-traceable); distinct sibling of [[protein-low-complexity-seg]]; deviations None.
- [[protein-low-complexity-seg]] â€” protein disorder / features family anchor (first DISORDER-* unit, DISORDER-LC-001): the SEG algorithm (Wootton & Federhen 1993/1996) partitioning a protein into low-/high-complexity segments; complexity = Shannon entropy `H=âˆ’خ£pلµ¢logâ‚‚pلµ¢` bits/residue (max logâ‚‚20â‰ˆ4.322), two-stage scan with W=12 trigger window / K1=2.2 trigger cutoff / K2=2.5 extension cutoff (NCBI `blast_seg.c` defaults); homopolymer H=0 triggers, 12-distinct Hâ‰ˆ3.585>K2 no segment; X-rich/X-Y-rich label + greedy single-residue extension are flagged repository extensions not moving boundaries; distinct from [[intrinsic-disorder-prediction-top-idp|intrinsic-disorder prediction]] (TOP-IDP) and the genomic-DNA [[repetitive-element-detection]] low-complexity counterpart.
- [[intrinsic-disorder-prediction-top-idp]] â€” protein-disorder family shared anchor (DISORDER-PRED-001 + DISORDER-PROPENSITY-001 + DISORDER-REGION-001): the TOP-IDP `PredictDisorder` sliding-window intrinsic-disorder predictor (Campen 2008) that [[morf-prediction-dip-in-disorder]] + disordered-region detection sit on; also hosts the region-detection layer (contiguous runs â‰¥ minRegionLength, default RegionType classification proline-rich/acidic/basic/Ser-Thr-rich > 0.25 + Long/Standard IDR, opt-in MobiDB-lite flavor scheme); per-residue Sلµ¢=mean over window of min-max-normalized TOP-IDP `(pâˆ’(âˆ’0.884))/1.871 âˆˆ [0,1]`, disordered when Sلµ¢â‰¥0.542 (max-likelihood cutoff), default window 21 (edge-clipped) / minRegionLength 5; Dunker 2001 disorder{A,R,G,Q,S,P,E,K}/order{W,C,F,I,Y,V,L,N}/ambiguous{D,H,M,T} sets + Kyte-Doolittle `CalculateHydropathy`; W30â†’0.0/P30â†’1.0/E30â†’0.866 oracles, null/emptyâ†’empty, non-canonical skipped (all-unknown windowâ†’0.0), case-insensitive, O(nآ·w); also anchors the raw per-residue propensity primitives (DISORDER-PROPENSITY-001: `GetDisorderPropensity` returns the RAW un-normalized Table-2 value, unknownâ†’0.0, + the two public Dunker sets); assumptions None (params source-traced), impl = simplified single-feature heuristic not competitive with IUPred2A/MobiDB-lite; distinct sibling of [[protein-low-complexity-seg]].
- [[coiled-coil-prediction]] â€” ProteinMotif family anchor (first ingested unit, PROTMOTIF-CC-001): the heptad a/d hydrophobic-core occupancy coiled-coil predictor `ProteinMotifFinder.PredictCoiledCoils` â€” for each window `score = (#a/d positions with residue âˆˆ {I,L,V})/(#a/d positions)` maximised over the 7 heptad registers (`p(k,r)=(kâˆ’r) mod 7`, core a=0/d=3), contiguous windows with score â‰¥ threshold mapped to residue regions â‰¥21 residues (3 heptads) with peak `Scoreâˆˆ[0,1]`; defaults window 28 (4 heptads, Lupas 1991) / threshold 0.5 / min-region 21 (Mason & Arndt â‰¥3-heptad); INV-01..05 (scoreâˆˆ[0,1]; regionâ‰¥21; len<windowâ†’empty; off-frame found via 7-register max); (LAALAAA)أ—5â†’(0,34,1.0) / no-{I,L,V}â†’none / (LAAAAAA)â†’0.5 boundary oracles; COILS 21أ—20 PSSM deliberately omitted (weights not retrievable, use COILS/Paircoil2 for P-scores) + {I,L,V}-only core-set assumption (source-verbatim); sequence-only heuristic, distinct from the ProteinPred disorder/features family ([[protein-low-complexity-seg]], [[intrinsic-disorder-prediction-top-idp]], [[morf-prediction-dip-in-disorder]]).
- [[common-protein-motifs]] â€” ProteinMotif family second unit (PROTMOTIF-COMMON-001, `ProteinMotifFinder.FindCommonMotifs`): scans an amino-acid sequence against a fixed built-in `CommonMotifs` dictionary of canonical PROSITE patterns and aggregates every hit carrying its accession/name â€” PS00001 `ASN_GLYCOSYLATION` `N-{P}-[ST]-{P}`, PS00005 `PKC_PHOSPHO_SITE` `[ST]-x-[RK]`, PS00006 `CK2_PHOSPHO_SITE` `[ST]-x(2)-[DE]`, PS00016 `RGD` `R-G-D`, PS00017 `ATP_GTP_A` `[AG]-x(4)-G-K-[ST]`; PROSITE syntax (`x` wildcard, `[ ]` allowed set, `{ }` excluded set, `x(n)`/`x(m,n)` repetition); 0-based-inclusive `MotifMatch.Start`/`End` (PROSITE reports 1-based) + substring invariant + overlaps-all-reported (ScanProsite "overlaps, no includes"); `NFTA`/Pro-exclusion-no-match/`SAR`/`SAAE`+`SDED`/`GXXXXGKS`/`RGD`+`RGD`-overlap oracles; one API-shape assumption (0- vs 1-based origin, no correctness effect); the **protein** fixed-catalog analogue of the DNA [[regulatory-element-detection]], sibling of the windowed [[coiled-coil-prediction]], distinct from the caller-supplied-set DNA exact [[known-motif-search]].
- [[protein-domain-and-signal-peptide-prediction]] â€” ProteinMotif family third unit (PROTMOTIF-DOMAIN-001): protein **domain** prediction + **signal-peptide** prediction. `ProteinMotifFinder.FindDomains` scans PROSITE **domain patterns** (PS00028 C2H2 zinc finger/PF00096, PS00017 P-loop/PF00069, PS00678 WD40 15-residue/PF00400; ScanPrositeâ†’regex), 0-based inclusive hits, tandem repeats all detected â€” SH3/PDZ excluded (PROSITE **PROFILEs**, no deterministic pattern). Opt-in `FindDomainsByHmm`/`Plan7ProfileHmm` reproduces the **HMMER3** engine over 3 bundled CC0 Pfam HMMs (SH3/PDZ/WD40): Viterbi/Forward log-odds (exact 1e-9 hand-HMM), local-multihit `pre_score` vs Swiss-Prot `bg->f` (~1e-5-bit hmmsearch parity), null2 bias (omega 1/256), Gumbel/exponential E-values (`E=Pآ·Z`), `p7_domaindef` multi-domain envelope decomposition (GBB1/PF00400â†’7 blades exact) + stochastic-traceback clustering for overlapping tandems (fixed-seed Easel LCG 42), verified vs pyhmmer 0.12.1. `PredictSignalPeptide` = von Heijne tripartite n(K/R+)/h(hydrophobic خ±-helix)/c(polar) + âˆ’1,âˆ’3 rule {A,G,S}, score (n+2h+c)/4 with evidence-based constraints (nScore>0, hScoreâ‰¥0.5) and Probability=Score. Six resolved design decisions; MSV/bias prefilters + exact-RNG-bit parity + full-Pfam coverage out of scope (research-grade). Sibling of [[coiled-coil-prediction]] & [[common-protein-motifs]].
- [[protein-motif-pattern-search]] â€” ProteinMotif family general engine (PROTMOTIF-FIND-001, `ProteinMotifFinder.FindMotifByPattern`): the **general, arbitrary caller-supplied** PROSITE-pattern protein motif finder underneath the fixed-dictionary [[common-protein-motifs]]. Three primitives â€” `ConvertPrositeToRegex` (PROSITEâ†’regex: `x`â†’`.`, `[ABC]`â†’`[ABC]`, `{ABC}`â†’`[^ABC]`, `x(n)`â†’`.{n}`, `x(n,m)`â†’`.{n,m}`, `<`â†’`^`, `>`â†’`$`); `FindMotifByPattern` (all matches incl. overlaps via zero-width lookahead `(?=(pattern))` per ScanProsite, 0-based `MotifMatch.Start`/`End`, case-insensitive, empty/nullâ†’empty, invalid regex handled gracefully); and information-content scoring `CalculateMotifScore` IC=خ£logâ‚‚(20/allowed_count) over constrained positions (`x`=0 bits, fixedâ‰ˆ4.32 bits) + `CalculateEValue` E=(Nâˆ’L+1)آ·2^(âˆ’IC), Schneider & Stephens 1990 (NOT BLAST statistics â€” that citation was removed). Pins the PROSITE-pattern catalog (PS00001/00004â€“00009/00016â€“00018/00028 C2H2/00029 leucine-zipper) and fixed two impl bugs (PS00007 exact repeat counts; PS00018 EF-hand `{W}`+trailing `[LIVMFYW]`); five non-PROSITE linear motifs literature-verified (NLS1/NES1/SIM1/WW1/SH3_1); SKIP-FLAG=TRUE common sites noted. Sibling of the fixed-catalog [[common-protein-motifs]], windowed [[coiled-coil-prediction]], and longer-signature [[protein-domain-and-signal-peptide-prediction]]; all assumptions eliminated (0-vs-1-based coordinate convention only). Revalidated by PROTMOTIF-PATTERN-001 ([[protmotif-pattern-001-evidence]]), which adds the end-to-end `FindMotifByProsite` path and the `*`-rejection / range-only-on-`x` PA-line grammar contracts.
- [[transmembrane-helix-prediction]] â€” ProteinMotif family transmembrane-helix unit (PROTMOTIF-TM-001): the classic **Kyte-Doolittle (1982) hydropathy sliding window** for membrane-spanning خ±-helices â€” slide a window `W=19`, score each window as the **arithmetic mean** of per-residue Kyte-Doolittle hydropathy (`HydropathyScale` I 4.5â€¦R âˆ’4.5), emit contiguous runs with window mean **â‰¥ threshold 1.6** as segments (`[iâ‚€, iâ‚پ+Wâˆ’1]`, peak `Score`); profile length `nâˆ’W+1`, non-standard residues excluded from the mean, `<W`/null/emptyâ†’empty; window 19 & min-span=W justified by ~18â€“21 residues / ~3â€“4 nm bilayer. Oracles `Dأ—10+Lأ—20+Dأ—10`â†’(5,34) peak 3.8 / `Dأ—40`â†’none / `Lأ—19`â†’(0,18,3.8). One assumption (`End=lastPassingProfileIndex+Wâˆ’1` clamped, 2026-06-16 off-by-one fix), no deviations; sequence-only hydrophobicity heuristic â€” no in-out topology / positive-inside rule / TMHMM-Phobius HMM. Shares the Kyte-Doolittle scale with [[intrinsic-disorder-prediction-top-idp]]'s `CalculateHydropathy`; distinct sibling of [[coiled-coil-prediction]] (heptad a/d, not window-mean), [[common-protein-motifs]], [[protein-domain-and-signal-peptide-prediction]] (cleaved signal peptide, not membrane span) & [[protein-motif-pattern-search]].
- [[aneuploidy-detection]] â€” chromosome copy-number/ploidy family anchor (first Chromosome-analysis unit): abnormal chromosome count from read depth â€” per-bin CN=round(2^log2(depth/median)أ—2) clamped [0,10], whole-chromosome call needs dominant CN across â‰¥80% of bins (mosaicism tolerance), confidence=1âˆ’min(1,|CN/2âˆ’2^logRatio|)=1.0 at integer-CN ratios; nullisomy..pentasomy terminology; Down/Edwards/Patau/Turner/Klinefelter oracles; sex-chromosomes-not-special-cased + partial-aneuploidy-needs-80%-bins limitations.
- [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]] â€” epigenetics family bisulfite-sequencing unit (second EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-BISULF-001): base-level DNA-methylation calling from sodium-bisulfite reads â€” distinct from the age clock (it *produces* the خ²-values a clock consumes). Three deterministic ops on `EpigeneticsAnalyzer`: (1) `SimulateBisulfiteConversion` â€” single-strand per-base Frommer 1992 rule (unprotected Câ†’T, protected 5mC stays C, non-C unchanged, case preserved, ACGTCGAA{1}â†’ACGTTGAA); (2) `CalculateMethylationFromBisulfite` â€” reuses `FindCpGSites`, Bismark C=methylated/T=unmethylated tally, level = meth/(meth+unmeth)âˆˆ[0,1], zero-coverage sites excluded (ACGTACGT readsâ†’0.5&0.0); (3) `GenerateMethylationProfile` â€” Schultz 2012 per-context weighted level خ£(levelآ·coverage)/خ£coverage (0.25â‰ unweighted 0.5), zero-total-coverage falls back to unweighted mean; CpG needs C+G, neither-C-nor-T call ignored, past-reference ignored; research-grade, no CHG/CHH calling / no complement merge / no non-conversion-rate correction; sibling of [[epigenetic-age-horvath-clock]]; deviations None.
- [[epigenetic-age-horvath-clock]] â€” epigenetics family anchor (first EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-AGE-001): DNAm ("epigenetic") age from methylation خ²-values via the Horvath 2013 multi-tissue clock â€” two-stage model, linear predictor `Y = intercept + خ£ coef_iآ·خ²_i` over 353 elastic-net-selected clock CpGs (transformed-age units), then the two-branch inverse calibration `anti.trafo` (adult.age=20): `21آ·exp(Y)âˆ’1` for Y<0 (exponential), `21آ·Y+20` for Yâ‰¥0 (linear), continuous at (0,20)=age 20; embedded intercept 0.695507258 + 353 `CoefficientTraining` weights cross-verified byte-identical; invariants Y=0â†’20 / CpGs-absent-ignored / empty-mapâ†’Fâپ»آ¹(intercept); nullâ†’ArgumentNullException, empty coefficientsâ†’ArgumentException; anti.trafo oracles (0â†’20, 1â†’41, âˆ’1â†’6.7254682646, âˆ’2.5â†’0.7237849711) + Y=0.684247258â†’34.369192418; scope = multi-tissue only (algorithm doc later extends to Horvath-2018 skin&blood 391-CpG + Levine-2018 PhenoAge 513-CpG no-transform); no BMIQ input normalisation (research-grade); sibling [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]] (produces the خ²-values); third Epigenetics sibling [[chromatin-state-prediction]] (histone-mark axis).
- [[cpg-island-detection]] â€” epigenetics family CpG site & island unit (fourth EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-CPG-001): sequence-only CpG dinucleotide detection (no methylation state â€” distinct from all siblings). Three ops on `EpigeneticsAnalyzer`: `FindCpGSites` (linear scan, 0-based C position, `CGCG`â†’2 sites, reused by [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]]); `CalculateCpGObservedExpected` (Gardiner-Garden O/E=CpG/((Cآ·G)/L), div-by-zero guardâ†’0, oracles CGCGأ— 2.0/ACGTCGACG 3.0/ACGT 4.0/AT-only 0); `FindCpGIslands` (sliding-window merge, default â‰¥200bp/GCâ‰¥0.5/O-Eâ‰¥0.6 inclusive, 0-based inclusive-Start/exclusive-End tuple, 400bp CGCGâ†’1 island, O(nآ·w)); GpCâ‰ CpG, case-insensitive; Takai-Jones 2002 stricter (â‰¥500/55%/0.65) + Saxonov 2006 alt-expected not preset (custom args); Gardiner-Garden & Frommer 1987 + Takai-Jones + Saxonov + Wikipedia; assumptions None. Siblings [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]]/[[epigenetic-age-horvath-clock]]/[[chromatin-state-prediction]].
- [[chromatin-state-prediction]] â€” epigenetics family chromatin-state / histone-mark unit (third EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-CHROM-001): ChromHMM-style (Ernst & Kellis 2012) annotation of a locus from the *combination of present histone marks* â€” distinct from the methylation siblings (operates on histone ChIP-seq signals, not DNA methylation). Binary present/absent mark model (ChromHMM binarizes then learns; state = function of the SET of present marks, magnitude beyond the call irrelevant = binary invariance); `PredictChromatinState` takes the six Roadmap 18-state marks {H3K4me3, H3K4me1, H3K27ac, H3K36me3, H3K27me3, H3K9me3} as [0,1] signals, calls present > threshold (default 0.5), maps pattern â†’ ActivePromoter(TssA, H3K4me3آ±H3K27ac)/ActiveEnhancer(H3K4me1+H3K27ac)/WeakEnhancer(H3K4me1 no H3K27ac)/Transcribed(Tx, H3K36me3)/Repressed(ReprPC, H3K27me3)/Heterochromatin(Het, H3K9me3)/BivalentPromoter(TssBiv, H3K4me3+H3K27me3)/BivalentEnhancer(EnhBiv, H3K4me1+H3K27me3)/LowSignal(Quies, none); two combinatorial rules â€” bivalency is a state not a contradiction, promoter(H3K4me3) dominates enhancer(H3K4me1); companions `AnnotateHistoneModifications` (per-mark region label) + `FindAccessibleRegions` (ATAC-like contiguous-merge + minWidth); research-grade â€” state-assignment logic source-backed, NOT a trained HMM (no LearnModel/Poisson binarization/spatial context); two assumptions (0.5 threshold, single-locus precedence); sibling of [[epigenetic-age-horvath-clock]] & [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]]; no contradictions.
- [[differentially-methylated-regions]] â€” epigenetics family DMR-detection unit (fifth EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-DMR-001): methylKit (Akalin 2012) two-sample tiling-window + Fisher's-exact-test model â€” *compares* methylation between two samples (distinct from the single-sample siblings), consuming the per-CpG C/(C+T) خ²-values [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]] produces over the CpGs [[cpg-island-detection]] locates. Fixed tiles (`win.size=1000/step.size=1000/cov.bases=0`, `tileMethylCounts`), meth.diff=group2%âˆ’group1% (percentage points), per-window pooled 2أ—2 methylated/unmethylated counts â†’ Fisher's exact (one sample per group; replicatesâ†’logistic regression out of scope), hypergeometric single-table p `(a+b)!(c+d)!(a+c)!(b+d)!/(a!b!c!d!n!)` + two-sided â‰¤-observed sum; report q<0.01 AND |meth.diff|>25 strict (`getMethylDiff`): hyper meth.diff>+25 / hypo <âˆ’25; emptyâ†’no DMRs, zero-coverage group / zero marginalâ†’p=1.0, |meth.diff|=25â†’excluded; oracles Fisher a=1/b=9/c=11/d=3â†’â‰ˆ0.001346076, hyper window g1=0.0/g2=1.0â†’+100/pâ‰ˆ0; two evidence-backed assumptions (per-window pooling, numC/numT=round(levelأ—coverage)); research-grade (no logistic path/SLIM/overlapping tiles); siblings [[epigenetic-age-horvath-clock]]/[[chromatin-state-prediction]]; no contradictions.
- [[kmer-jaccard-similarity]] â€” Analysis alignment-free pairwise-similarity unit (`GENOMIC-SIMILARITY-001`, `GenomicAnalyzer.CalculateSimilarity`): Jaccard index of the two sequences' distinct k-mer sets (Jaccard 1901 `|Aâˆ©B|/|AâˆھB|` over HashSet k-mer sets, Ondov 2016 *Mash* fraction-of-shared-k-mers), exact (no MinHash sketch) Jأ—100 in `[0,100]`, O(n+m); INV symmetry / identicalâ†’100 / disjointâ†’0 / distinct-set (repeats once); default k=5, empty-unionâ†’0 (ASM-1 convention), أ—100 scaling; k=3 oracles 80/(100/3)/100/0; `alternative_to` positional [[alignment-statistics]], the 5-mer-Jaccard metric behind [[ortholog-detection-reciprocal-best-hits]] and the exact-set basis Mash sketches for [[average-nucleotide-identity]]; limitations = exact-match/composition-only; deviations None.
- [[k-mer-euclidean-distance]] â€” K-mer family alignment-free word-frequency **distance** unit (`KMER-DIST-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.KmerDistance`): Euclidean (L2) distance between two sequences' normalized k-mer **frequency** vectors `f_s(w)=count/(Lâˆ’k+1)` over the union of observed k-mers (absent wordâ†’0 component), exact/O(n+m); Zielezinski 2017 word-vector model + Lau 2022 frequency normalization + Vinga-Almeida 2003 4^k-vector + Boden 2014 relative-frequency Euclidean; INV d(x,x)=0 / symmetric / â‰¥0 / disjoint-single-kmerâ†’âˆڑ2; âˆڑ0.11â‰ˆ0.3316624790 (ATGTGTG/CATGTG k=3) + âˆڑ0.125 (AAAA/AAAT k=1) oracles; case-insensitive (ASM-01) + empty/L<kâ†’zero-vector (ASM-02); count-based/Manhattan/Canberra/Chebyshev/cosine/D2/spaced-word not implemented, deviations None; `alternative_to` the presence/absence [[kmer-jaccard-similarity]] (this captures abundance), shares the `CountKmers` primitive with [[both-strand-kmer-counting]]/[[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]; record [[kmer-dist-001-evidence]].
- [[asynchronous-kmer-counting]] â€” K-mer family async count unit (`KMER-ASYNC-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.CountKmersAsync`): the cooperatively cancelable, progress-reporting thread-pool wrapper over synchronous `CountKmers` â€” numeric result identical to the sync reference (counts fixed by the k-mer formula `L âˆ’ k + 1`, nلµڈ possible), so the distinctive validated content is *execution* not arithmetic: the .NET cancellation contract (`ThrowIfCancellationRequested`â†’OperationCanceledException + Canceled state, pre-start `Task.Run(func,token)` cancellation, awaiting a canceled task throws) + `IProgress<double>` 0â†’1.0; INV خ£counts=Lâˆ’k+1 / emptyآ·k>Lâ†’empty dict / kâ‰¤0â†’ArgumentOutOfRangeException via awaited task; uppercased (case-insensitive) + alphabet-agnostic (IUPAC N counted literally); ATGGâ†’{ATG:1,TGG:1} + GTAGAGCTGT oracles; one assumption = numeric contract identical to sync (non-correctness-affecting); single-thread offload (not parallelized), suffix-tree evaluated-not-used; wraps sync KMER-COUNT-001 (not yet ingested); record [[kmer-async-001-evidence]].
- [[k-mer-generation]] â€” K-mer family *space-enumeration* unit (`KMER-GENERATE-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.GenerateAllKmers`): exhaustive enumeration of ALL possible k-mers of length `k` over an alphabet â€” the complete k-mer universe `خ£^k` of size `n^k` (4^k for DNA), depends only on `k`+alphabet not on any sequence; DISTINCT from counting (produces the full n^k word set / address space, siblings extract observed substrings + counts); k-fold Cartesian product `itertools.product(خ£,repeat=k)`, lazy recursive prefix-extension, odometer emission â†’ lexicographic for a sorted alphabet; INV n^k count / all-distinct-set / length-k / sortedâ†’lexicographic; k=1â†’{A,C,G,T}, k=2â†’16 (AA..TT), k=3â†’64, protein 20^2=400, single-letter 1^4=1 oracles; kâ‰¤0â†’ArgumentOutOfRangeException, empty alphabetâ†’ArgumentException, unsortedâ†’positional order, verbatim/no-dedup; O(kآ·n^k) time/O(k) lazy space, suffix-tree N/A (generates not searches); shares the "ACGT"-default + kâ‰¤0-throws API contract with [[both-strand-kmer-counting]]/[[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]/[[k-mer-euclidean-distance]] but NOT the `CountKmers` primitive; supplies the index space for [[kmer-jaccard-similarity]]/[[k-mer-euclidean-distance]]/[[de-bruijn-graph-assembly]]; deviations None; record [[kmer-generate-001-evidence]].
- [[k-mer-positions]] â€” K-mer family *occurrence-index* unit (`KMER-POSITIONS-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.FindKmerPositions`): the ascending 0-based positions where a given k-mer occurs in a sequence â€” *where*, not *how many* (the inverse index to the counting units) â€” solving the exact Pattern Matching Problem `Occ(P,T)={iâˆˆ[0,Lâˆ’k]:T[i..i+k)=P}` with all overlapping starts reported; INV-01..04 (match predicate / ascending / count=overlap-occurrences / range `[0,Lâˆ’k]`, empty when k>L); case-insensitive upper-casing (sibling `CountKmers`), unrestricted-text alphabet, null/empty & k>L & absent â†’ empty (no throw), whole-seqâ†’`[0]`; `ATAT`/`GATATATGCATATACTT`â†’`[1,3,9]` + `AA`/`AAAA`â†’`[0,1,2]` oracles; O(Lآ·k) naive span scan, suffix-tree evaluated-not-used (unordered leaves, single-query no amortization); three API-shape assumptions (0-based, case-fold, empty-not-throw), deviations None; the single-pattern K-mer sibling of multi-pattern [[known-motif-search]], distinct from the counting siblings [[both-strand-kmer-counting]]/[[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]; record [[kmer-positions-001-evidence]].
- [[both-strand-kmer-counting]] â€” K-mer family strand-aware count unit (`KMER-BOTH-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.CountKmersBothStrands`): the ADDITIVE / kPAL-"balance" both-strand profile `count[w] = forward[w] + forward[RC(w)]` (count k-mers of S and of RC(S), sum per key), grounded in inversion symmetry (Shporer 2016) + kPAL balance (Anvar 2014); distinct from â€” and does NOT implement â€” the canonical-collapsing convention (lexicographically-smaller of {w,RC(w)} as one key, Jellyfish `-C` / Mash); INV خ£count=2آ·(Lâˆ’k+1) / count[w]=count[RC(w)] strand-symmetric / palindrome RC(w)=wâ†’count doubled on one key; two linear passes O(nآ·k), suffix-tree evaluated-not-used; case-insensitive/IUPAC-complemented, emptyآ·k>Lâ†’empty dict, kâ‰¤0â†’ArgumentOutOfRangeException (inherited from `CountKmers`); ATGGC k=2â†’{AT:2,TG:1,GG:1,GC:2,CC:1,CA:1} + ACGTâ†’{AC:2,CG:2,GT:2} + AAAâ†’{AA:2,TT:2} oracles; built on the same sync `CountKmers` primitive as [[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]; two API-shape assumptions, deviations None; record [[kmer-both-001-evidence]].
- [[k-mer-statistics]] â€” K-mer family *summary-statistics* unit (`KMER-STATS-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.AnalyzeKmers`): a companion summary layer over the shared `CountKmers` multiset that reduces the count profile to `KmerStatistics` {TotalKmers=Lâˆ’k+1=خ£counts, UniqueKmers=**distinct** count, MaxCount, MinCount, AverageCount=total/distinct (rounded 2dp), Entropy=Shannon **k-entropy** `âˆ’خ£ p(خ±)logâ‚‚p(خ±)`, `p=mult/(Lâˆ’k+1)`, bits}; the one distinct piece of content is the k-entropy (Manca 2021 + Entropyâ€“Rank Ratio, corroborated by Wikipedia/BioInfoLogics count tables); GOTCHA `UniqueKmers` = distinct count NOT the count==1 singletons (that is KMER-UNIQUE-001); INV Total=خ£counts / Unique=distinct(CountKmers) / homopolymerâ†’H0,max=min=total / all-distinctâ†’H logâ‚‚D,max=min=1 / k>Lآ·emptyâ†’all-zero; GTAGAGCTGT k=1 (10/4/4/1/2.5/1.8464) + k=3 (8/8/1/1/logâ‚‚8=3.0) + ATCGATCAC k=3 (7/6/2/1/2.5216) + AAAA k=2 (3/1/3/3/0) oracles; case-insensitive, kâ‰¤0â†’ArgumentOutOfRangeException; two presentation-only assumptions (AverageCount 2dp, Entropy unrounded); shares the `CountKmers` primitive with [[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]/[[both-strand-kmer-counting]], distinct from generation/positions/distance siblings; deviations None; record [[kmer-stats-001-evidence]].
- [[unique-and-mincount-kmers]] â€” K-mer family *frequency-filtering* unit (`KMER-UNIQUE-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.FindUniqueKmers` + `FindKmersWithMinCount`): selects k-mers by their per-k-mer **Count** (overlapping occurrences, Compeau & Pevzner `Count(Text,Pattern)`) at opposite ends of the frequency distribution â€” `FindUniqueKmers` = the `Count==1` **singletons**, `FindKmersWithMinCount` = the `Countâ‰¥minCount` **recurrent** k-mers ordered by count desc; total/distinct/unique terminology (BioInfoLogics: unique = "appear only once"; Wikipedia Lâˆ’k+1 total); GOTCHA "unique"=singleton set here â‰  [[k-mer-statistics]]'s `UniqueKmers`=distinct count (ATCGATCAC k=3 â†’ 5 unique vs 6 distinct, ATC=2 excluded); oracles ATCGATCAC k=3â†’{TCG,CGA,GAT,TCA,CAC}, AGAT k=2â†’{AG,GA,AT}, ACGTACGT k=4 FindKmersWithMinCount(â€¦,2)â†’{(ACGT,2)}/(â€¦,1)â†’all-4-count-desc/FindUniqueKmersâ†’{CGTA,GTAC,TACG}, AAAAA k=3â†’âˆ…; case-insensitive, kâ‰¤0â†’ArgumentOutOfRangeException, emptyآ·k>Lâ†’empty; two assumptions (minCountâ‰¤1â†’all distinct count-desc; upper-casing), deviations None; filters the shared `CountKmers` multiset like [[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]/[[both-strand-kmer-counting]]; record [[kmer-unique-001-evidence]].
- [[longest-common-substring]] â€” Sequence-Comparison longest-common-substring / common-region-detection unit (`GENOMIC-COMMON-001`): the maximal *contiguous* substring shared by two strings (distinct from the gapped longest common *subsequence*) via a generalized suffix tree (LCS = deepest internal node whose subtree holds leaves from both strings, خک(n+m) build + DFS, Gusfield 1997); `FindLongestCommonRegion` (0-based positions in both) + `FindCommonRegions(minLength)` (all distinct shared runs â‰¥ minLength), None=empty/len 0/pos âˆ’1, identicalâ†’whole seq at 0/0; documented deterministic first-found-in-`other` tie-break (CACAGAG/TACATAGAT ties ACA vs AGA â†’ ACA); Wikipedia + GeeksforGeeks sources, shares the suffix-tree exact-match engine with [[dot-plot-word-match]]; deviations None.
- [[longest-repeated-substring]] â€” Repeat-Analysis LRS + repeat-enumeration unit (`GENOMIC-REPEAT-001`): the longest substring recurring within *one* DNA sequence (`GenomicAnalyzer.FindLongestRepeat`) + all distinct substrings occurring â‰¥2أ— with length â‰¥ minLength (`FindRepeats`), both via the *single-string* suffix tree's deepest internal node with â‰¥2 leaves (string depth = repeat length; CMU آ§2.1 / Wikipedia / GeeksforGeeks App-3 / Gusfield 5.4); overlaps counted, no-repeat/emptyâ†’`RepeatInfo.None`, `minLengthâ‰¤0`â†’`max(1,minLength)`, ACGT-only, no reverse-complement/maximal-repeat classification; FindRepeats via sorted-suffix adjacent-LCP *every-prefix* enumeration (O(nآ²), FINDINGS_REGISTER short-prefix fix); ATCGATCGAâ†’ATCGA{0,4}, AAAAAAAAAAâ†’AAAAAAAAA{0,1}, ATATATAâ†’ATATA{0,2}, ACGTACGTTTTTACGT@3â†’8-substring oracles; the *single-string* sibling of [[longest-common-substring]], distinct from the tandem/inverted [[repetitive-element-detection]] anchor; tie-break + ascending-positions assumptions, deviations None.
- [[open-reading-frame-detection]] â€” Analysis ORF-detection unit (`GENOMIC-ORF-001`): six-frame ATGâ†’first-in-frame-stop enumeration (`GenomicAnalyzer.FindOpenReadingFrames`), standard code (start ATG / stops TAA-TAG-TGA), reported span **includes** the stop (Length%3==0) while the translated protein **excludes** it; THE correctness rule = every in-frame ATG reaching a stop reported, so **nested ORFs sharing a stop** both returned (Rosalind `MGMTPRLGLESLLE`/`MTPRLGLESLLE`), ATG-with-no-stopâ†’none; `minLength` in **nucleotides** inclusive (default 100), 0-based Position, Frame 1â€“3 + IsReverseComplement, INV-01..05 (starts ATG / ends stop / len%3==0 / â‰¥minLength / six-frame), O(nآ²) worst / O(n) typical; Rosalind_99â†’4 distinct proteins + ATGAAAAAATAAâ†’MKK oracles; Rosalind + Wikipedia + NCBI ORFfinder + transl_table=1 sources; deviations None (one fixed greedy bug); deliberately **not** contract-equivalent to annotation `GenomeAnnotator.FindOrfs` (ANNOT-ORF-001: ATG/GTG/TTG, aa-length, strand/start flags) or `Translator.FindOrfs` (genetic-code-parameterized); coding potential is a separate step ([[coding-potential-hexamer-score]]).
- [[known-motif-search]] â€” Motif-Analysis known-motif-search anchor (`GENOMIC-MOTIFS-001`): multi-pattern **exact** substring matching of a caller-supplied set of known query motifs (`GenomicAnalyzer.FindMotif`) â€” the "you know what you're looking for" exact-equality baseline, distinct from motif *discovery* and *degenerate* (IUPAC/PROSITE/PWM) matching; THE correctness rule = all **overlapping** occurrences reported (AAA in AAAAAâ†’{0,1,2}, per Gusfield/Biopython `count_overlap` 3-not-2); 0-based sorted positions, per-motif position lists with absent motifs omitted, upper-cased result keys, empty/whitespace motifâ†’no entry (`Array.Empty<int>()`); EcoRI GAATTCâ†’{0,9} + `{ACGT,AA,TTT}` in ACGTACGTAA oracles; Tufts/Gusfield + Biopython `Seq.search` + Wikipedia "Restriction site" sources; shares exact-all-occurrences semantics with [[longest-common-substring]]/[[dot-plot-word-match]]; deviations None.
- [[alpha-diversity]] â€” Metagenomics diversity family anchor (first META-* unit, META-ALPHA-001): within-sample diversity indices from one taxonâ†’abundance map (`MetagenomicsAnalyzer.CalculateAlphaDiversity` â†’ `AlphaDiversity` record) â€” observed richness S_obs, Shannon H=âˆ’خ£pلµ¢ln(pلµ¢) in nats, Simpson concentration خ»=خ£pلµ¢آ², inverse Simpson 1/خ» (Hill order-2 effective species), Pielou evenness J=H/ln(S) for S>1 else 0, Chao1 S_obs+fâ‚پآ²/(2fâ‚‚) (fâ‚‚=0â†’bias-corrected S_obs+fâ‚پ(fâ‚پâˆ’1)/2, non-integer/proportionalâ†’S_obs); Whittaker 1960 خ±/خ²/خ³ framework, Shannon 1948/Simpson 1949/Hill 1973/Chao 1984/Pielou 1966; counts-or-proportions internally normalized, non-positive filtered, O(n); empty/nullâ†’all-0, single speciesâ†’H0/خ»1/J0; one accepted deviation = Chao1 count-vs-proportion gate; between-sample [[beta-diversity]] its sibling; deviations else None.
