- [[metagenomic-binning]] â€” Metagenomics family binning unit (third META-* unit, META-BIN-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.BinContigs`): groups mixed-community contigs back to their genome of origin (MAGs) by k-means over a composite distance `|خ”GC|+|خ”coverage|+TNF-Pearson-distance` (GC-sorted deterministic centroid init, â‰¤50 iters, minBinSize 500 kb filter) â†’ `GenomeBin` records; completeness=`min(L/expectedGenomeSizeأ—100,100)` (default 4 Mbp) + contamination=`min(gcStdDev/0.5أ—100,100)` are LENGTH-RATIO/GC-VARIANCE **proxies** (CheckM marker-gene QC now built as a SEPARATE opt-in path â€” CheckM Eqs. 1â€“2 over CC0 Pfam marker sets, `EstimateBinQualityFromMarkerCounts`/`DetectMarkers`, NOT wired into `BinContigs`; see [[meta-bin-001-markerqc-evidence]]); INV unique BinId / metrics [0,100] / GC [0,1] / TotalLength=خ£ / disjoint partition / Coverage=mean; M5 50.0 / M6 0-100 / M7 1.0-0.0 / M12 25 oracles; opt-in TETRA z-score signature (`CalculateTetranucleotideZScores`/`TetranucleotideZScoreCorrelation`) â€” RC-extended strand, 256-word Markov expectation `E=N(n1n2n3)آ·N(n2n3n4)/N(n2n3)`, Schbath variance, Pearson correlation of z-vectors (scale-invariant), z(ACGT)=âˆڑ5 for ACGTACGTGGCC, N(n2n3)=0/non-positive-varâ†’z=0; Maguire 2020 limits (plasmids 1-29%/GIs 38-44% poorly recovered), similar-GC+coverageâ†’co-bin; three prior assumptions resolved, deviations None; record [[meta-bin-001-evidence]]; Metagenomics-family sibling of [[alpha-diversity]]/[[beta-diversity]].
- [[taxonomic-classification]] â€” Metagenomics family taxonomic-classification unit (fourth META-* unit, META-CLASS-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.ClassifyReads` + `BuildKmerDatabase` + `TaxonomyTree.Lca`): faithful Kraken (Wood & Salzberg 2014) per-read/contig assignment â€” canonical-k-mer (`min(kmer,revcomp)`, default k=31) database mapping each k-mer to the **LCA of all owning reference taxa**, per-read **classification tree** (hit taxa + ancestors weighted by k-mer count) scored over **root-to-leaf (RTL)** paths â†’ assigned taxon = max-scoring path's leaf, equal-max â†’ LCA of leaves, no k-mer hits â†’ **Unclassified** (taxonomy root, C=0); Confidence = **C/Q** (Kraken 2: C = clade k-mers under assigned label, Q = non-ambiguous k-mers queried); ambiguous (non-ACGT) k-mers skipped/not in Q, upper-cased, semicolon/pipe taxonomy strings; invariants |out|=|in| / 0â‰¤C/Qâ‰¤1 / Câ‰¤Q / Q=lenâˆ’k+1 (all-ACGT) / canonical uniqueness / DB-build LCA / LCA siblingsâ†’parent, ancestor/descendantâ†’ancestor, selfâ†’self, disjointâ†’root; empty/short-<k/no-match â†’ Unclassified, empty DB â†’ all Unclassified; scoped to **per-read classification** (abundance *profiling* Taxonomic_Profile is a separate later unit); research-grade, no deviations / no open questions; siblings [[metagenomic-binning]] (per-contig MAGs) & [[alpha-diversity]]/[[beta-diversity]] (consume the abundance profile); record [[meta-class-001-evidence]].
- [[beta-diversity]] â€” Metagenomics diversity family between-sample unit (second META-* unit, META-BETA-001): between-sample dissimilarity from two taxonâ†’abundance maps (`MetagenomicsAnalyzer.CalculateBetaDiversity` â†’ `BetaDiversity` record) â€” Bray-Curtis BC=1âˆ’2آ·خ£min(N_ij,N_ik)/خ£(N_ij+N_ik) (abundance-sensitive, range [0,1], NOT a true metric) + Jaccard distance J=1âˆ’|Aâˆ©B|/|AâˆھB| (presence/absence via abundance>0, true distance metric); Whittaker 1960 خ±/خ²/خ³ (beta=turnover), Bray & Curtis 1957, Jaccard 1901; single union-pass O(u), no BC normalization (caller-scaled), +SharedSpecies/UniqueToSample1/2 counts; identicalâ†’0/0, disjointâ†’1/1, both-emptyâ†’0/0 & one-emptyâ†’1 guards; fish-tank BC 13/33 & J 1/3, symmetry BC 3/5 & J 2/3 oracles; one accepted deviation = UniFracDistance placeholder 0 (no phylo tree); within-sample sibling [[alpha-diversity]]; ecological-Jaccard shares the index math but not domain with sequence [[kmer-jaccard-similarity]].
- [[functional-prediction]] â€” Metagenomics family functional-prediction unit (fifth META-* unit, META-FUNC-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.PredictFunctions` + `FindPathwayEnrichment`): predicts a community's *functional* capability (PICRUSt / KO-pathway style) in two exact-numeric pieces â€” (A) homology-based annotation transfer: exact-signature `string.Contains` hit scored by BLOSUM62 self-score S, bit `S'=(خ»Sâˆ’lnK)/ln2` and E-value `E=Kآ·mآ·nآ·e^(âˆ’خ»S)=mآ·nآ·2^(âˆ’S')` (ungapped BLOSUM62 خ»=0.3176/K=0.134, Altschul/`blast_stat.c`), best hit = lowest E-value / highest bit (INV-01..03,06); (B) hypergeometric pathway ORA `P(Xâ‰¥x)=1âˆ’خ£ C(M,i)C(Nâˆ’M,nâˆ’i)/C(N,n)` in log-Gamma space, background=union-of-pathways default + query unioned in, sorted ascending, pâˆˆ[0,1], x/M/n=0â†’p=1 (INV-04,05); oracles WWWâ†’S'18.0202932787533/E 3.3852730346546eâˆ’5 + N8000/M400/n100/x20â†’7.88eâˆ’8; *Simplified* â€” exact substring not gapped alignment (ASM-01, divergent homologs missed), no gapped خ»/K / composition stats / HMM / FDR; asks "what can they do" vs the "who is there" of [[taxonomic-classification]]/[[metagenomic-binning]] and the diversity of [[alpha-diversity]]/[[beta-diversity]]; BLAST significance distinct from percent-id [[alignment-statistics]]; ORA half owned by [[pathway-enrichment-ora]] (the dedicated META-PATHWAY-001 unit); record [[meta-func-001-evidence]].
- [[pathway-enrichment-ora]] â€” Metagenomics family pathway-enrichment unit (META-PATHWAY-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.FindPathwayEnrichment` / `HypergeometricUpperTail`): the GO::TermFinder / clusterProfiler over-representation statistic â€” score each pathway by the hypergeometric **right-tail** `P(Xâ‰¥x)=1âˆ’خ£_{i=0}^{xâˆ’1}C(M,i)C(Nâˆ’M,nâˆ’i)/C(N,n)` (N=background, M=pathway size, n=query, x=overlap; sampling without replacement, upper tail only), `phyper(xâˆ’1,M,Nâˆ’M,n,lower.tail=FALSE)` reference (the q=xâˆ’1 shift gives P(Xâ‰¥x)); log-Gamma summation to N=8000, pâˆˆ[0,1], pathways sorted ascending; p=1 when x/M/n=0, **Mâ†”n symmetry**, without-replacement feasibility drops C(آ·,آ·)=0 terms; background = explicit `backgroundGenes` else union-of-pathway-members default (query always unioned in), members intersected with background; **no BH/Bonferroni FDR** correction; Boyle 2004 + PNNL ORA آ§8.2 sources, oracles 7.88eâˆ’8 + 1/252 + 5/6 + 251/252; one caller-overridable background-defaulting assumption; **owns** the ORA machinery that [[functional-prediction]] uses as component B; generic statistic (GO/proteomics), research-grade, no contradictions; record [[meta-pathway-001-evidence]].
- [[taxonomic-profile]] â€” Metagenomics family community-abundance profiling unit (sixth META-* unit, META-PROF-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.GenerateTaxonomicProfile`): the **aggregation/estimation** step downstream of per-read [[taxonomic-classification]] â€” takes an `IEnumerable<TaxonomicClassification>` and returns a `TaxonomicProfile` with **relative-abundance maps at four ranks** (kingdom/phylum/genus/species, abundance = count(taxon)/خ£count(classified)), **inline species-level diversity** (Shannon H=âˆ’خ£pلµ¢ln(pلµ¢) in nats + Simpson concentration خ»=خ£pلµ¢آ²), and **read counts** (TotalReads/ClassifiedReads); Unclassified excluded from denominators, empty rank strings filtered, per-rank خ£â‰ˆ1.0; invariants ClassifiedReadsâ‰¤TotalReads / ClassifiedReads=خ£(counts any rank) / Shannonâ‰¥0 / 0â‰¤Simpsonâ‰¤1; oracles Shannon=ln(3) (3 uniform), Simpson=0.375 ([2,1,1]); emptyâ†’0/0/empty & single taxonâ†’1.0/H0/خ»1 (vs emptyâ†’خ»0); count-based tally (NOT MetaPhlAn marker-coverage, no genome-size correction), inherits upstream classifier accuracy; the profiling unit [[taxonomic-classification]] deliberately deferred, sibling of [[alpha-diversity]] (richer six-index within-sample summary) / [[beta-diversity]]; MetaPhlAn/Segata 2012, research-grade, no contradictions; record [[meta-prof-001-evidence]].
- [[antibiotic-resistance-gene-detection]] â€” Metagenomics family AMR gene-detection unit (seventh META-* unit, META-RESIST-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.FindAntibioticResistanceGenes`): ResFinder-style screen of assembled contigs against a **caller-supplied** resistance-gene reference DB, reporting the single **best-matching gene per contig** â€” `BestUngappedMatch` slides each reference across the contig (offsets âˆ’(mâˆ’1)..nâˆ’1, overhanging both ends), keeps the max-match window (tieâ†’shorter/higher-identity), then identity=matches/w (BLAST gapless, Heng Li 2018) & coverage=w/m (fraction of **reference** length, so contig-edge/split genes still scored), reported iff identityâ‰¥idThreshold AND coverageâ‰¥covThreshold; best match = max identity, tieâ†’max coverage (Zankari 2012 "best-matching gene", CARD RGI best-hit); INV-01..05, defaults 0.90 ID / 0.60 cov (named constants), Perfect=1.0/1.0 (CARD); oracles CGTACGT@AAACGTACGTâ†’1.0/1.0, CGTTCGT vs CGTACGTâ†’6/7â‰ˆ0.857/1.0, edge CGTAâ†’1.0 / 4âپ„7â‰ˆ0.571; *Simplified* â€” gapless ungapped (ASM-01, indel matches under-scored vs gapped BLAST; substitution + edge-truncation exact), no SNP/protein-homology (CARD variant/homolog models out of scope), nucleotide-only case-sensitive, legacy `FindResistanceGenes` motif stub separate; asks "**which known resistance genes are present**" vs the who/what/how-diverse of [[taxonomic-classification]]/[[functional-prediction]]/[[alpha-diversity]]; BLAST-style homology screen sharing machinery with [[functional-prediction]] but scoring nucleotide identity/coverage not BLOSUM62 bit-score (identity denominator = [[alignment-statistics]] rule); provenance note flagged (evidence 0.80/0.98 vs impl 0.90 default); record [[meta-resist-001-evidence]].
- [[significant-taxa-detection]] â€” Metagenomics family differential-abundance unit (eighth META-* unit, META-TAXA-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.MannWhitneyU` / `FindSignificantTaxa`): per-taxon **two-group Mannâ€“Whitney U (Wilcoxon rank-sum)** test asking "which taxa differ in abundance between two groups?" â€” non-parametric, rank-based, suits compositional/zero-inflated data (Xia & Sun 2017). Poolâ†’midranks (tied values averaged, accumulate خ£(tآ³âˆ’t))â†’`U1=R1âˆ’n1(n1+1)/2`, `U2=n1آ·n2âˆ’U1`; `m_U=n1آ·n2/2`, tie-corrected `دƒ_U=sqrt(n1آ·n2آ·(n1+n2+1)/12 âˆ’ n1آ·n2آ·خ£(tآ³âˆ’t)/(12n(nâˆ’1)))`; `z=(|Uâˆ’m_U|âˆ’cc)/دƒ_U` on `max(U1,U2)`, ccâˆˆ{0,0.5} (0.5 on by default = SciPy `use_continuity`); two-tailed `p=2آ·(1âˆ’خ¦(z))` clamped [0,1], خ¦ via `StatisticsHelper.NormalCDF` (A&S 7.1.26, â‰ˆ1eâˆ’6 accuracy). `FindSignificantTaxa` runs it per taxon over label-defined ({1,2}) groups â†’ `SignificantTaxon` ascending by p. INV-01..06 (U1+U2=n1آ·n2, 0â‰¤Uâ‰¤n1آ·n2, pâˆˆ[0,1], Significantâ‡”p<threshold, all-tiedâ†’دƒ0â†’z0â†’p1, group-swap symmetric); oracles SciPy x[19,22,16,29,24]/y[20,11,17,12]â†’U1=17/U2=3/دƒ=4.0825/z_cc=1.5922â†’pâ‰ˆ0.11135 (z_nocc=1.7146â†’pâ‰ˆ0.08641) + tortoise/hare U_T=11/U_H=25/sum=36; empty groupâ†’ArgumentException, absent taxonâ†’abundance 0 (ASM-03); asymptotic-not-exact, no FDR (caller applies BH), ignores compositionality; **consumes** [[taxonomic-profile]] abundance vectors; distinct-by-**test** from the hypergeometric [[pathway-enrichment-ora]] and Fisher's-exact [[differentially-methylated-regions]]; siblings [[alpha-diversity]] / [[beta-diversity]]; record [[meta-taxa-001-evidence]].
- [[methylation-context-classification]] â€” epigenetics family CpG/CHG/CHH context-classification unit (sixth/final EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-METHYL-001): sequence-only trinucleotide classifier partitioning cytosines into CpG/CHG/CHH from the downstream base(s) â€” distinct because it handles the *non-CpG* CHG/CHH contexts [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]] does not call from reads. Rule (Cornish-Bowden 1985 IUPAC H={A,C,T}="not G"): CpGâں؛bâ‚پ=G, CHGâں؛bâ‚پâˆˆH & bâ‚‚=G, CHHâں؛bâ‚پâˆˆH & bâ‚‚âˆˆH; CpG/CHG symmetric, CHH asymmetric (Krueger-Andrews 2011). Three ops on `EpigeneticsAnalyzer`: `GetMethylationContext` (O(1), null when not a classifiable C), `FindMethylationSites` (O(n) scan â†’ one site/classifiable C, 0-based, sequence-only level=0/coverage=0 placeholder), `GenerateMethylationProfile` (shared with [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]], Schultz 2012 weighted خ£(levelآ·cov)/خ£cov, zero-coverageâ†’unweighted-mean fallback); CGACAGCAAâ†’CpG@0/CHG@3/CHH@6 + weighted (8+2)/(10+10)=0.5 oracles; G-never-H (CGGâ†’CpG), terminal-CG-still-CpG, incomplete-trailing / non-ACGT unclassified; Lister 2009 realism (IMR90 99.98% CG vs H1 ES ~25% non-CG); single-strand only, no symmetric-strand pairing; two assumptions (level=0 placeholder, 0.5 MethylatedCpG count cutoff); no contradictions.
- [[rna-base-pairing]] â€” MiRNA family anchor + shared RNA base-pairing primitive (first MiRNA unit, MIRNA-PAIR-001, `MiRnaAnalyzer`): deciding **whether two RNA bases can pair** and building the antiparallel miRNA-mRNA duplex from that rule. `CanPair`âں؛{A-U,U-A,G-C,C-G,G-U,U-G} = Watson-Crick {A-U,G-C} (Agarwal 2015) + the single standard **G-U wobble** (Crick 1966); `IsWobblePair`âں؛{G-U,U-G}, wobbleâٹ†pairable, wobble counted **separately** from matches (PMC4870184). `GetReverseComplement` = antiparallel RNA reverse complement for seedâ†’target motif (Lewis 2005; let-7a `GAGGUAG`â†’`CUACCUC`). `AlignMiRnaToTarget` pairs miRNA[i]â†”target[lenâˆ’1âˆ’i] over the shorter overlap, ungapped, emitting `|`(WC)/`:`(wobble)/space(mismatch); counts sum to min(len), Gaps=0; خ”G = **simplified** Turner-2004 stacking sum over consecutive paired runs (sign reliable â€” fully-WC â‰¤0, all-mismatch â‰¥0 â€” magnitude not). Oracles AAAA/UUUUâ†’4 matches, GGGG/UUUUâ†’4 wobbles, AAAA/AAAAâ†’4 mismatches; DNA Tâ†’U normalised, unknown baseâ†’N never pairs, emptyâ†’empty duplex. The **shared** pairing rule RNA secondary-structure classification also uses; **not** target-site efficacy prediction (that is `FindTargetSites`/MIRNA-TARGET-001), and the A-opposite-position-1 preference is Argonaute recognition, not base pairing; record [[mirna-pair-001-evidence]].
- [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]] â€” MiRNA family precursor-hairpin unit (second MiRNA unit, MIRNA-PRECURSOR-001, `MiRnaAnalyzer`): finding stem-loop pre-miRNA precursors (~60-120 nt) from which Dicer excises the ~22 nt mature duplex. **Default heuristic** `FindPreMiRnaHairpins` counts uninterrupted complementary pairs ({A-U,G-C}+G-U wobble, [[rna-base-pairing]] primitive) from both ends inward â†’ accept iff stem â‰¥18 bp (Krol 2004) + loop 3-25 nt (Bartel 2004); extracts mature(5' arm)/star(3' arm), balanced dot-bracket, Turner-2004 خ”G; **documented limitation** â€” consecutive-pairing is stricter than real structure, rejects natural miRBase precursors (hsa-mir-21 16 end-pairs, let-7a-1 5, tests M18/M19). **Opt-in** `AssessHairpinByMfe`/`FindPreMiRnaHairpinsByMfe` fold with the RNA-STRUCT-001 Zukerâ€“Stiegler engine and read the hairpin from the real MFE structure (single dominant hairpin/no multibranch + stem â‰¥16 (Ambros 2003) + loop 3-25 + MFEI â‰¥0.85 (Zhang 2006, AMFE=100آ·|خ”Gآ°|/n, MFEI=AMFE/GC%)) â†’ detects hsa-mir-21 (خ”Gآ° âˆ’35.13/MFEI 1.0037) & let-7a-1; rejects a stronger-خ”Gآ° multibranch 5S-rRNA-like on **structure**. **Opt-in** `PredictDroshaDicerCleavage` = published ruler (Drosha +11 bp basal junction/Han 2006, Dicer 22-nt 5'-count/Park 2011, RNase III 2-nt overhang/Lee 2003, CNNC 16-18 nt confidence flag/Auyeung 2013; hsa-miR-21-5p cross-check). **Opt-in** `ClassifyPreMiRna` = logistic regression over [خ”G,AMFE,MFEI,GC,%paired], 13 public-domain miRBase positives vs Altschul-Erickson di-shuffle negatives (Bonnet 2004 convention), held-out AUC 1.0, no GPL miRDeep2 code; read-stacking miRDeep2 signal out of scope (needs reads); record [[mirna-precursor-001-evidence]].
- [[seed-sequence-analysis]] â€” MiRNA family seed-extraction unit (third MiRNA unit, MIRNA-SEED-001, `MiRnaAnalyzer`): **string-level** extraction and comparison of the mature-miRNA 5' seed â€” the primary determinant of animal target recognition â€” not binding prediction. `GetSeedSequence` returns positions **2-8** (7 nt, extended seed) via `Substring(1,7)` uppercase (casing only, **no** Tâ†’U); `<8 nt`/null/empty â†’ `""`. `CreateMiRna(name, sequence)` normalises `ToUpperInvariant()`+`Tâ†’U`, extracts the seed from the normalised sequence, stores `SeedSequence` + fixed **zero-based** `SeedStart=1`/`SeedEnd=7`. `CompareSeedRegions` = Hamming over the 7-nt seed (`Matches`+`Mismatches`=7, mismatches also count any length diff), `IsSameFamily` âں؛ **exact seed-string equality**; empty seed â†’ zeroed result. **miRNA family = identical 2-8 seed** (let-7a/-7b/-7c-5p all `GAGGUAG` â†’ same family; miR-21-5p `AGCUUAU` differs); selfâ†’0 mismatches. Domain context: TargetScan site ladder 8mer/7mer-m8/7mer-A1/6mer over the 2-7-vs-2-8 distinction, but matching-to-target + site-class assignment is deferred to target-site prediction (MIRNA-TARGET-001, future); seedâ†’target motif reverse complement is owned by [[rna-base-pairing]] (`GetReverseComplement`). **Intentionally simplified** â€” exact-7-mer family equality (no isomiR/offset/noncanonical seeds, not a curated taxonomy); 2-7-vs-2-8 terminology collapse flagged, no source contradictions; record [[mirna-seed-001-evidence]].
- [[mirna-target-site-prediction]] â€” MiRNA family target-site-prediction unit (fourth & **final** MiRNA unit, MIRNA-TARGET-001, `MiRnaAnalyzer`, **completes** the family): finding mRNA target sites for a miRNA and classifying the **Bartel/TargetScan hierarchy**. `FindTargetSites(mRna, miRna, minScore=0.5)` = two-pass, `Tâ†’U`, 0-based-inclusive antiparallel scan for the seed reverse complement (`seedRC=revcomp(mâ‚‚â€¦mâ‚ˆ)`, 6mer core `seedRC[2..7]`): pass-1 upgrades 6mer-core hits to **8mer** (pos 2-8 + A opposite pos 1) / **7mer-m8** (2-8) / **7mer-A1** (2-7 + A1) / **6mer** (2-7); pass-2 finds **offset-6mer** (3-8) only where not overlapping a retained higher-priority site (INV-04). Heuristic `Scoreâˆˆ[0,1]` (base 1.0/0.52/0.32/0.15/0.10, +0.05 >10 matches, âˆ’0.01/mismatch) + heuristic `FreeEnergy` (sign-reliable) â€” ranking aid, **not** calibrated repression. **Depends on** [[seed-sequence-analysis]] (the 2-8 seed determines targeting) + [[rna-base-pairing]] (`GetReverseComplement` motif + `AlignMiRnaToTarget` `|`/`:`/space duplex). **Opt-in `ScoreTargetSiteContextPlusPlus`** = source-fitted TargetScan **context++** (Agarwal 2015): per-site-type MLR, sum of `coeffأ—scaledScore`, continuous features min-max scaled + indicators raw; realises Intercept/Local_AU/sRNA1/sRNA8/Site8/3P_score/Min_dist/Len_3UTR/Off6m, **computes** TA_3UTR=log10 N (`ComputeTa3Utr`, Garcia 2011) + SA (Turner-2004 McCaskill partition unpaired-prob) + PCT (Friedman Blsâ†’published sigmoid); SPS/Len_ORF/ORF8m/PCT-`b0..b3` caller-supplied (compiled TargetScan tables, not bundled) â†’ honest **partial** `ContextScorePartial` + `OmittedFeatures` (8mer let-7a all-G-flank partial CS = âˆ’0.7561913315126536). `Centered`/`Supplementary` enum members not emitted (accepted); bulged/centered/supplementary/noncanonical + isoforms out of scope; no contradictions; record [[mirna-target-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]] â€” RNA secondary-structure family **notation layer** (RNA-DOTBRACKET-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): parse an extended-**WUSS** structure string into base pairs `(i,j)` and validate well-formedness. `ParseDotBracket` uses **one stack per bracket family** â€” `()`/`<>`/`{}`/`[]` + uppercase(5' open)/lowercase(3' close) letter pairs â€” each an **independent pairing system** (ViennaRNA / Infernal `vrna_db_from_WUSS()`: any matched pair = a base pair, symbol has no meaning); a shared stack would mis-pair `([)]`. `ValidateDotBracket` âں؛ every family's stack empty at end & never underflows; a closer must match a **same-family** opener. **Pseudoknots** (crossing families) are valid; `(]` (mismatched families) is not. Non-bracket WUSS symbols `-`/`,`/`:`/`.` are single-stranded (Rfam). Oracles `((((....))))`â†’4 pairs, `([)]`â†’(0,2)+(1,3), `<<<<[[[[....>>>>]]]]`â‰،`((((AAAA....))))aaaa`â†’two crossing 4-bp helices; valid `(((...)))`/`(([[]]))`/`([)]`, invalid `(((...)` / `...)` / `)(` / `(]`. Notation-only (does not fold/score); distinct from the base-pairing chemistry [[rna-base-pairing]]; the structure the [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]] unit emits and the MFE folder reads. Two API-contract assumptions (malformedâ†’best-effort parse; empty/nullâ†’valid). Record [[rna-dotbracket-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]] â€” RNA secondary-structure family **energy layer** (RNA-ENERGY-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): the individual **Turner 2004 nearest-neighbor free-energy terms** summed into a fold's خ”Gآ° at 37 آ°C (`CalculateStackingEnergy`/`CalculateStemEnergy`/`CalculateHairpinLoopEnergy`/`CalculateMinimumFreeEnergy`), all verified exact against **NNDB Turner04**. Model `خ”Gآ°total = init + خ£stacking + خ£loops`. **WC stacking all negative**, GC-rich most stable (`GC/CG` âˆ’3.42, `GG/CC` âˆ’3.26; `AA/UU` âˆ’0.93); **G-U wobble variable** â€” mostly negative but **two positive** (`UG/GU` +0.30, `GU/UG` +1.29), note-a `GG/UU`=âˆ’0.5, **note-b special 3-stack** `5'GGUC/3'CUGG`=âˆ’4.12 (vs âˆ’1.77). **Hairpin-loop initiation positive and NOT monotonic** (3â†’5.4, 4â†’5.6, 6â†’5.4, 8â†’5.5, 9â†’6.4; Jacobson-Stockmayer `خ”G(n)=خ”G(9)+1.75RTآ·ln(n/9)` beyond 9). **Special UNCG/GNRA tri/tetra/hexaloops** use NNDB total energies keyed by closing pair+loop (replace the model; GNRA>random). **All-C loop** penalty (3-nt +1.5, >3-nt 0.3n+1.6), terminal mismatch (96 entries), **+0.45 per-AU/GU-end**. A single base pair contributes **0** stacking (needs â‰¥2 adjacent); empty/poly-Aâ†’0. Oracles GC 3-bp stem âˆ’5.78, NNDB hairpin example-1 `GGGAUAAAUCCC` âˆ’3.42, GGUC/CUGG âˆ’4.12. The **energy** the folding units consume (pre-miRNA `FreeEnergy`, RNA-STRUCT-001 MFE), assigned to [[rna-base-pairing]] pairs, distinct from the [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]] notation. No contradictions; three defined conditions (37 آ°C, 2-dp, unknown stacksâ†’0), not assumptions. Record [[rna-energy-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding]] â€” RNA secondary-structure family **folding/search layer** (RNA-MFE-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): the **Zukerâ€“Stiegler dynamic-programming MFE folder** that searches structure space for the fold of lowest total free energy (`CalculateMinimumFreeEnergy` / `PredictStructure`). Loop decomposition (hairpin / stacking / bulge-interior / multibranch); DP matrices **C(i,j)=min(hairpin, interior/bulge over an inner pair, multiloop)** + multiloop **M** (â‰¥1 component)/**M1** (exactly one) + exterior **F** (Ward 2017); **standard affine multiloop model â†’ O(nآ³) time / O(nآ²) space** ("simplest model is best"; logarithmic model would be O(nâپ´)). The unit that **consumes** the [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]] Turner-2004 terms (summing them over candidate structures) and **produces** a [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]] structure; builds on [[rna-base-pairing]]. Oracles `CACAAAAAAAUGUG`â†’`((((......))))` âˆ’1.41 (NNDB Example 1), `CACAGAAAGUGUG` âˆ’1.91 (Example 2). Invariants MFE â‰¤ 0 (INV-01, empty structure always available), suffix-monotone `MFE(s) â‰¤ MFE(prefix)` (INV-02), optimized DP == classic O(nآ³) baseline (INV-03); empty/null / unfoldable homopolymer / sequence `< minLoopSize+2` â†’ 0 (hairpin loop â‰¥ 3 nt); intramolecular â‡’ no helix-init constant. The folder the [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]] opt-in `AssessHairpinByMfe` path uses (once generically called *RNA-STRUCT-001* before that artifact was ingested â€” RNA-STRUCT-001 is now the **distinct sibling** Nussinov predictor [[rna-secondary-structure-prediction]], sharing this unit's Zuker MFE machinery). Two documented simplifications (multiloop per-unpaired `c=0`; 2-dp rounding), no source contradictions; sources Zuker & Stiegler 1981 + Lorenz 2011 (ViennaRNA) + Ward 2017 + NNDB Turner 2004 + Mathews 2004. Record [[rna-mfe-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-partition-function-mccaskill]] â€” RNA secondary-structure family **probabilistic/ensemble layer** (RNA-PARTITION-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): the **McCaskill 1990** partition function â€” the Boltzmann-weighted counterpart of MFE folding that computes the equilibrium `Z = خ£_P exp(âˆ’E(P)/RT)` over all pseudoknot-free structures plus per-base-pair binding probabilities and the Boltzmann probability of a given structure, in **O(nآ³) time / O(nآ²) space**. Inside recursion `Q_ij = Q_{i,j-1} + خ£_{iâ‰¤k<j-m} Q_{i,k-1}آ·Q^b_{kj}` (base `Q_ij=1` for iâ‰¥jâˆ’m), total **`Z = Q_{1n}`** (disjoint/unambiguous decomposition); pair probability needs the **outside** recursion `p_kl = Q^b_klآ·O_kl/Z` â€” the external-only term is **wrong for nestable pairs** (`GGGAAACCC` P(2,6)=6/20 not 1/20; outside matches Boltzmann brute force to 3.3e-16). Oracles (E_bp=0 â‡’ Z counts structures) `AAAA`â†’1, `GC`â†’1, `GGGGCCCC`â†’16, `GGGAAACCC`â†’20; invariants Z â‰¥ 1 (empty structure weight 1), P(i,j) âˆˆ [0,1] + symmetric, per-base pairing sum â‰¤ 1, monotone in E_bp; WC + GU pairing only, min-loop forbids jâˆ’k â‰¤ m. The **`alternative_to` / ensemble counterpart** of the single-optimum [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding]] MFE folder; Boltzmann-weights the [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]] energies (ViennaRNA default 37 آ°C = Turner standard); builds on [[rna-base-pairing]]. One simplification (fixed-per-pair `E_bp` energy model vs full Turner NN â€” energy model only, invariants conformant with McCaskill 1990), no source contradictions. Record [[rna-partition-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-pseudoknot-prediction]] â€” RNA secondary-structure family **crossing-helix layer** (RNA-PKPREDICT-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): predict the optimal fold that may contain a single **canonical H-type pseudoknot** â€” two helices whose pairs **cross** (`i<k<j<l`), the one feature the nested [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding|MFE folder]] and [[rna-partition-function-mccaskill|McCaskill ensemble]] cannot represent. **pknotsRG class** (Reeder & Giegerich 2004): "two crossing helices with three intervening loops", H-type 5'â†’3' stem1-5'â†’loop1â†’stem2-5'â†’loop2â†’stem1-3'â†’loop3â†’stem2-3', two-layer dot-bracket `((((..[[[[..))))..]]]]`; full grammar **O(nâپ´)/O(nآ²)**. Canonization rules (equal-length bulge-free helices / maximal extent / fixed overlap boundary) bound the search. Energy = Turner NN stacking on **both** helices (same model as nested, `Energy.lhs`) + penalties **initiation 9.0** (anti-spurious-knot gate â€” a knot is reported only when it beats both the penalty and the best nested alternative) / **unpaired loop nt 0.3** / **base pair inside knot 0.0** kcal/mol. **Depends on** [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]] (helix scoring) and [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding]] (MFE fallback baseline `FreeEnergy â‰¤ CalculateMfeStructure().FreeEnergy` + folds internal loops); emits two-layer [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]]; builds on [[rna-base-pairing]]. Oracles designed H-type `GGGGAACCCCAACCCCAAGGGG`â†’knot with two crossing 4-bp helices; plain `GGGGAAAACCCC`â†’no knot = MFE; BWYV `GGCGCGGCACCGUCCGCGGAACAAACGG` (PDB 437D) **not** recovered (tertiary-stabilized, outside NN model â€” documented limit of all NN-only pseudoknot predictors). Two boundaries: PARTIAL pknotsRG coverage (single H-type only; recursive/over-arching/multiple knots not implemented) + tertiary-stabilized knots not recovered. No contradictions. Record [[rna-pkpredict-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-pseudoknot-detection]] â€” RNA secondary-structure family **crossing detection layer** (RNA-PSEUDOKNOT-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure.DetectPseudoknots`): given a **set of base pairs** describing a known structure, a pure **O(nآ²) combinatorial scan** finds every **crossing** pair-of-pairs `i<k<j<l` (Antczak 2018) â€” one pair's opener inside the other while its closer lies outside. Two exhaustive negatives: **nested** `i<k<l<j` (one pair fully inside) and **disjoint** `j<k` (side-by-side). Each crossing pair-of-pairs = one pseudoknot (binary relation); â‰¥2 pairs required, endpoints normalized min-max to open<close, deterministic. Oracles `([)]`=(0,2)+(1,3)â†’one, nested (0,5)+(1,4)â†’none, disjoint (0,2)+(3,5)â†’none. The **detection/analysis facet** â€” genuinely distinct from the energy-driven [[rna-pseudoknot-prediction]] predictor (input = pair set vs sequence, machinery = combinatorial scan vs Turner-NN energy DP, cost = O(nآ²) vs O(nâپ´)) â€” and the crossing primitive that predictor's validity invariant leans on. Operates on the pairs the [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]] parser emits; complements the nested-only [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding]] / [[rna-partition-function-mccaskill]]. One scope note: pseudoknot-**order** assignment (Antczak DBL layering / Smit 2008 removal) Not Implemented. Sources Antczak 2018 + Smit & Knight 2008 + biotite + Wikipedia, no contradictions. Record [[rna-pseudoknot-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-stem-loop-enumeration]] â€” RNA secondary-structure family **enumeration layer** (RNA-STEMLOOP-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): **scan a sequence for every stem-loop (hairpin)** it can form under size constraints â€” `FindStemLoops(sequence, minStem, minLoop, maxLoop, allowWobble)` / `FindHairpins`, extending an antiparallel WC/wobble stem outward around each candidate loop, **O(nآ²آ·L)**. The general, sequence-agnostic hairpin *finder* â€” distinct from the single-optimal-fold [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding|MFE folder]] (O(nآ³) DP), the hairpin *energy* unit [[rna-hairpin-001-evidence]], and the miRNA-specific [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]] precursor detector. Loop **â‰¥3 nt** (steric floor, shared with the MFE/Turner units), optimal **4-8 nt**. **Tetraloops** â€” GNRA / UNCG / CUUG, UUCG the most stable, UUCG+GNRA ~70% of 16S-rRNA tetraloops, ~3.0 kcal/mol bonus via [[rna-free-energy-turner-model|Turner 2004]]. `FindPseudoknots` shares the `i<k<j<l` crossing primitive with [[rna-pseudoknot-detection]]. Builds on [[rna-base-pairing]], emits [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]]. Invariants non-overlap / â‰¤1 pair per base / contiguous loop / antiparallel stem; limitations no PK-from-sequence, simplified energy, hairpin loops only, single structure. Record [[rna-stemloop-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-secondary-structure-prediction]] â€” RNA secondary-structure family **top-level prediction umbrella** (RNA-STRUCT-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): predict a structure from a sequence by a **Nussinov base-pair-maximizing** DP â€” `Predict` / `PredictWithConstraints` (forced pairs, Mathews 2004) / `ToDotBracket` / `FromDotBracket`. Nussinov & Jacobson 1980 O(nآ³)/O(nآ²) maximizes the **(weighted) base-pair count** (WC âˆ’2.0 / wobble âˆ’1.0), signalling **relative stability, not physical energy units** â€” the **`alternative_to`** the physical Turner-kcal/mol [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding|MFE folder]] (RNA-MFE-001), same problem / different objective. A **distinct sibling** test unit, **not an alias** of RNA-MFE-001: both share the `RnaSecondaryStructure` Zuker MFE machinery (this unit's D5 added `CalculateMfeStructure`/`PredictStructureMfe`). Builds on [[rna-base-pairing]], converts to/from [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]], consumes [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]] stem-loop terms, shares the `i<k<j<l` crossing test with [[rna-pseudoknot-detection]] (detects, never predicts, pseudoknots). Oracles `GGGGAAAACCCC`â†’`((((....))))`, poly-Aâ†’MFE 0; min loop 3 nt (steric), single-sequence only, int21/int22 lookup tables blocked. Record [[rna-struct-001-evidence]].
- [[clinical-actionability-oncokb-levels]] â€” Oncology family anchor (first ONCO-* unit, ONCO-ACTION-001): **clinical actionability assessment** by the OncoKB Therapeutic Levels of Evidence (Chakravarty 2017). A **pure ranking** â€” given a variant's caller-supplied leveled drug associations, return the **maximum** level under the fixed combined order `R1 > 1 > 2 > 3A > 3B > 4 > R2` (sensitivity axis `1 > 2 > 3A > 3B > 4`, resistance axis `R1 > R2`), the two axes reported separately (a variant may carry both); no leveled association â†’ **NotActionable**. Seven tiers: 1 (FDA in-indication) / 2 (NCCN in-indication) / 3A (clinical evidence in-indication) / 3B (another indication) / 4 (biological evidence) / R1 (standard resistance) / R2 (investigational resistance); 1/2/R1 = standard vs 3A/3B/4/R2 = investigational (SOP v3, consistent with AMP/ASCO/CAP Li 2017). **Knowledgebase is a caller input** â€” the library ranks, it does not embed/annotate the OncoKB DB; NotActionable-name is the library's; not for clinical use; record [[onco-action-001-evidence]].
- [[cancer-variant-tier-classification-amp-asco-cap]] â€” Oncology family, second ONCO-* unit (ONCO-ANNOT-001): **cancer variant tier classification** by the **AMP/ASCO/CAP 2017 four-tier** consensus (Li MM et al. 2017). A **pure decision rule** over caller-supplied evidence level (Aâ€“D) + population MAF + cancer-association flag â†’ **Tier I** (strong, Level A/B) / **II** (potential, Level C/D) / **III** (unknown, no level + rare + cancer assoc) / **IV** (benign, no level + MAF â‰¥ 1% **or** no assoc). Population frequency is the **IIIâ†”IV discriminator**; **evidence level dominates frequency** (a significant biomarker stays Tier I at high MAF). 1% (0.01) is the guideline **primary benign cutoff**, inclusive (MAF 0.01 â†’ Tier IV). `AnnotateCancerVariants` = one annotation per variant in input order; `GetCOSMICAnnotation` = null-on-miss lookup against a **caller-supplied** COSMIC catalog (external DB, not embedded). Distinct from but **consistent with** the sibling OncoKB level-ranking [[clinical-actionability-oncokb-levels]]; not for clinical use; record [[onco-annot-001-evidence]].
- [[sequencing-artifact-detection]] â€” Oncology family, third ONCO-* unit (ONCO-ARTIFACT-001): **sequencing artifact detection** (`FilterArtifacts`) â€” the **QC** sibling that removes false-positive somatic calls from DNA damage / mapping bias **before** clinical interpretation (distinct from the two clinical-significance ONCO units). Three disjoint signals: **substitution class** (OxoG oxidation G>T/C>A per Chen 2017 vs FFPE cytosine-deamination C>T/G>A per Do & Dobrovic 2015; else not-an-artifact), the **GIV** read-pair imbalance ratio (`GIV_G_T = count(G>T in R1)/count(G>T in R2)`, neutral 1 / damaged > 1.5, Chen 2017 + Damage-estimator), and **FisherStrand** FS = âˆ’10آ·log10(two-sided Fisher-exact p) on the `[ref_fwd,ref_rev,alt_fwd,alt_rev]` 2أ—2 table (GATK, FS â‰ˆ 0 no bias / high = artifact). Result âٹ† input; **no BAM parser** (per-strand/read-mate evidence supplied on the variant record); GIV thresholds from the Nature Methods summary; not for clinical use; record [[onco-artifact-001-evidence]].
- [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] â€” Oncology family, fourth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-ASCAT-001): the **upstream tumor copy-number layer** â€” allele-specific integer copy number (nA/nB) from per-locus **logR/BAF** by a joint **purity دپ / ploidy دˆ** grid fit (**ASCAT**, Van Loo 2010: `nA/nB` inversion, minimise length-weighted squared minor-allele distance to non-negative integers, BAF=0.5 down-weighted أ—0.05, GoF = (1âˆ’d/maxdist)آ·100, **خ³=1 for sequencing**). Four disjoint stages: (1) ASCAT core (دپ,دˆ) fit; (2) **ASPCF** penalised-least-squares joint segmentation `L=خ£(yâˆ’ب³)آ²+خ³|S|` via O(nآ²) DP (Nilsen 2012) with common change points + BAF mirroring (Ross 2021); (3) **subclonal** two-state mixture `n_obs=fآ·nâ‚پ+(1âˆ’f)آ·nâ‚‚` over bracketing integers (Battenberg / Nik-Zainal 2012); (4) **multiplicity/CCF** VAF inversion `VAF=(mآ·CCFآ·p)/(cآ·p+2(1âˆ’p))`, clamp m to [1,major-CN] (McGranahan 2016 / PICTograph / DeCiFering). Planted-truth tests invert the forward model (دپâ‚€=0.80, دˆâ‚€âˆˆ{2,3}). The allele-specific/clonal counterpart to the total-CN [[aneuploidy-detection]]; substrate beneath the clinical-interpretation ONCO siblings; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-ascat-001-evidence]].
- [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]] â€” Oncology family, fifth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CCF-001): the **downstream clonal-structure layer** â€” estimate each mutation's **cancer cell fraction** `CCF = fآ·(دپآ·N_T+2(1âˆ’دپ))/(دپآ·m)` (`EstimateCCF`; McGranahan 2016 / PICTograph / Tarabichi 2021, corroborated three ways; m âˆˆ [1,tumor CN], دپ âˆˆ (0,1]) with a reported-value **[0,1] cap** that exposes the uncapped raw (the raw formula can exceed 1 â€” CNAqc 1.06 noise case), then **`ClusterCCFValues`** deconvolutes the CCF vector into clones/subclones by a **deterministic 1D Lloyd k-means** (Lloyd 1982, quantile seeding, no RNG) with **highest-centroid = clonal** (Tarabichi 2021). Consumes the purity دپ / copy number N_T / multiplicity m from the upstream [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] (whose آ§4 carries the same CCF closed form); two source-consistent assumptions ([0,1] cap; Lloyd k-means as the concrete 1D method); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-ccf-001-evidence]].
- [[clonal-hematopoiesis-cfdna-filtering]] â€” Oncology family, sixth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CHIP-001): the **pre-interpretation biological-origin filter** for liquid biopsy â€” removes **clonal-hematopoiesis (CHIP)** false positives, the dominant cfDNA confounder (Razavi 2019: 81.6% controls / 53.2% cancer). `IdentifyCHIPVariants` flags a driver-gene variant ({DNMT3A,TET2,ASXL1,TP53,JAK2,SF3B1,SRSF2,PPM1D}, top-3 DNMT3A/TET2/ASXL1) at **VAF â‰¥ 0.02** (Steensma 2015 / Genovese 2014); `FilterCHIP` removes CH calls by **matched-WBC subtraction** (present in matched WBC â‡’ blood-derived, the definitive origin test, Razavi 2019) plus a **conservative labelled gene+VAF heuristic fallback** (over-removes; strict mode = empty gene panel); `CallVariantOrigin` = the strict **Bolton 2020** rule (WBC VAF â‰¥ 2% AND â‰¥ 10 reads AND â‰¥ د†أ— tumour VAF, د†=2.0 / 1.5 lymph node). The **biological-origin sibling** of the technical-artifact QC filter [[sequencing-artifact-detection]], upstream of the clinical-interpretation and clonal-structure ONCO units; two source-consistent assumptions (canonical default gene set, â‰¥1-alt-read WBC presence test); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-chip-001-evidence]].
- [[clonal-subclonal-classification-ccf-posterior]] â€” Oncology family, seventh ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CLONAL-001): the **probabilistic clonal-structure classifier** â€” per-mutation **Bayesian CCF posterior** `P(c) âˆ‌ Binom(a|N,f(c))` (uniform prior, 100-point grid `câˆˆ[0.01,1]`) with expected allele fraction `f(c) = خ±Mc/(2(1âˆ’خ±)+خ±q)` (Landau 2013 ABSOLUTE-style; multiplicity M generalisation, Satas 2021 DeCiFering Eq. 1), classified **clonal iff `P(CCF>0.95) > 0.5`** (two distinct thresholds: 0.95 CCF cut, 0.5 posterior-mass cut) via `ClassifyClonality(variants, purity)`, plus the point-estimate `IdentifyClonalMutations` (strict CCF > 0.95, boundary excluded â†’ indices {0,2,4}). The **`alternative_to`** the point-estimate + Lloyd-k-means [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]] â€” same clonal/subclonal question, but classifies each mutation on its own read-count uncertainty without clustering; consumes purity خ± / local copy number q / multiplicity M from the upstream [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]]; one API-shape assumption (per-variant local copy number q over a genome-wide ploidy scalar); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-clonal-001-evidence]].
- [[copy-number-alteration-classification]] â€” Oncology family, eighth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CNA-001): the **total-copy-number classification layer** â€” a single **log2 copy ratio** â†’ absolute integer CN `n = 2آ·2^log2` (CNVkit `_log2_ratio_to_absolute_pure`, diploid ref_copies=2) â†’ discrete **CNA state** via CNVkit's `absolute_threshold` hard-threshold caller (default `âˆ’1.1/âˆ’0.25/0.2/0.7` â†’ DeepDeletion/Loss/Neutral/Gain/Amplification; CN = index of the **first** threshold with `log2 <= thresh`, **boundary-inclusive â†’ lower bin**; above the last â†’ `ceil(2آ·2^log2)` open-ended Amplification; NaN â†’ neutral CN 2), corroborated by **GISTIC2** (Mermel 2011: آ±0.1 noise band subsumed by the neutral bin + +0.848/âˆ’0.737 high-amplitude cutoffs). The **total-CN** counterpart to the allele-specific [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] and the per-segment oncology-state sibling of the whole-chromosome [[aneuploidy-detection]] (both share the `n = 2آ·2^log2` conversion); distinct from SV-CNV-001's `round`-based integer CN (no state classification). One diploid-ploidy=2 assumption; threshold-variant note (docs germline `âˆ’0.4/0.3` vs code tumor `âˆ’0.25/0.2`); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-cna-001-evidence]].
- [[focal-amplification-detection]] â€” Oncology family, ninth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CNA-002): the **focal-amplification layer** â€” a two-part predicate `DetectFocalAmplifications` keeps segments both **amplified** (log2 gain > GISTIC2 `t_amp` 0.1) **and** **focal** (SegLen / ArmLength < `broad_len_cutoff` 0.98 â€” Mermel 2011's length-based, not amplitude-based, focal-vs-arm-level split; strict `< 0.98`, exactly 0.98 â†’ arm-level), then `IdentifyAmplifiedOncogenes` maps each focal amplification's arm prefix to a built-in oncogene panel (17qâ†’ERBB2 آ· 8qâ†’MYC آ· 7pâ†’EGFR آ· 11qâ†’CCND1 آ· 12qâ†’MDM2 **and** CDK4, NCBI Gene cytobands). Orthogonal to the log2â†’5-state [[copy-number-alteration-classification]] (ONCO-CNA-001) â€” a **length** question, not an amplitude bin â€” sharing only the GISTIC2 `t_amp`=0.1 amplitude gate. Sources GISTIC2 Mermel 2011 + GISTIC2 docs (`broad_len_cutoff`/`t_amp`) + CNVkit (single-copy gain log2 0.585 > 0.1) + NCBI Gene. Worked oracles A 17q 0.50â†’ERBB2 / B 8q 0.99 arm-level / C 7p log2 0.05 not-amplified / D 11q 0.98 boundary. Two assumptions (amplitude+length fusion; caller-supplied arm label + length, no cytoband table); deletions out of scope (ONCO-CNA-003); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-cna-002-evidence]].
- [[homozygous-deletion-detection]] â€” Oncology family, tenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CNA-003): the **deep-deletion layer**, the **deletion mirror of ONCO-CNA-002** â€” filter segments whose classified integer copy number is **exactly 0** (a homozygous / deep deletion: cBioPortal `âˆ’2` "Deep Deletion", Cheng et al. 2017 "zero copies of both alleles" / two hits; **reuses** [[copy-number-alteration-classification]]'s CN-0 = `DeepDeletion` call, **no new threshold**), then `IdentifyDeletedTumorSuppressors` maps each arm prefix to a built-in tumour-suppressor panel (17pâ†’TP53 آ· 13qâ†’RB1 **and** BRCA2 آ· 9pâ†’CDKN2A آ· 10qâ†’PTEN آ· 17qâ†’BRCA1, NCBI Gene cytobands). A single-copy loss (`âˆ’1`, heterozygous, CN â‰¥ 1) is NOT a homozygous deletion. The loss-side counterpart of the amplification unit [[focal-amplification-detection]] (`IdentifyDeletedTumorSuppressors` mirrors `IdentifyAmplifiedOncogenes`) and a consumer of [[copy-number-alteration-classification]]'s CN-0 state. Two assumptions (CN-0 reuse, caller-fixed panel); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-cna-003-evidence]].
- [[ctdna-detection-and-tumor-fraction]] â€” Oncology family, eleventh ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CTDNA-001): the liquid-biopsy **quantification / limit-of-detection** layer for **circulating tumor DNA (ctDNA)** â€” the Poisson detection probability `DetectionProbability` **p = 1 âˆ’ e^(âˆ’nآ·dآ·k)** (n genome equivalents, d mutant allele fraction, k reporters; Patent US 11,085,084 restating Avanzini 2020, corroborated by Pessoa 2023's خ» = nآ·d = 15) with a detectability test (caller threshold default 0.95 **and** خ» = nآ·dآ·k â‰¥ 1; only p is non-assumption), **`CalculateTumorFraction` = 2 أ— mean clonal-heterozygous VAF** (copy-neutral diploid, CNAqc/Antonello 2024 v = د€/2), `CalculateMeanVaf` = mean altReads/totalReads across reporters (Newman 2014 CAPP-Seq across-reporter fraction, detection 0.025%â€“10%), and a genome-equivalents helper (3.3 pg/haploid, Devonshire 2014 â‡’ â‰ˆ303 GE/ng, Alcaide 2020). The **quantification counterpart** on the same cfDNA input as the biological-origin filter [[clonal-hematopoiesis-cfdna-filtering]] (measures signal vs filters it), sharing the diploid-heterozygous VAF inversion with [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] / [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]]; underpins MRD monitoring; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-ctdna-001-evidence]].
- [[driver-gene-classification-20-20-rule]] â€” Oncology family, twelfth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-DRIVER-001): the **gene-level** driver classifier â€” the Vogelstein 2013 **20/20 rule** classifying a cancer gene **Oncogene** (> 20% missense at **recurrent** positions, â‰¥ 2أ— = activating), **TumorSuppressor** (> 20% **truncating / inactivating** â€” nonsense / frameshift / splice donor-acceptor / stop gain-loss = loss of function), or **Ambiguous** (neither criterion, or exact dual-pass tie), via `IdentifyDriverMutations` (driver âٹ† somatic) + `MatchCancerHotspots` (caller-supplied (gene, position) hotspot set) + `ScoreDriverPotential` (= max of the two criterion fractions in [0,1]; CADD/SIFT/PolyPhen are caller-supplied, not implemented). Oracles: IDH1 10 missense@codon 132 â†’ recurrent-missense 1.00 â†’ Oncogene; dispersed 8/10 truncating â†’ 0.80 â†’ TumorSuppressor; truncating exactly 0.20 â†’ NOT TSG (strict `>`). A **heuristic, not a statistical test** (passenger truncations / low-recurrence drivers mislead it; 20/20+ / MutSigCV successors out of scope), **orthogonal** to the variant-level clinical classifiers [[cancer-variant-tier-classification-amp-asco-cap]] and [[clinical-actionability-oncokb-levels]]. Three assumptions (strict `> 0.20`, dual-pass tie-break by larger fraction with Ambiguous on tie, ScoreDriverPotential proxy); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-driver-001-evidence]].
- [[expression-outlier-zscore-signature-score]] â€” Oncology family, thirteenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-EXPR-001), and the wiki's **first expression/transcriptome method**: the per-gene **outlier z-score** `z = (r âˆ’ خ¼)/دƒ` against a caller-supplied **reference (base) population** (cBioPortal's diploid or all-samples convention) with **دƒ = sample SD, divisor (n âˆ’ 1)** (settled by `NormalizeExpressionLevels.java`), classified over/under-expressed under the **strict آ±2** default threshold (exactly آ±2 is NOT an outlier), plus the **combined-z signature/pathway activity** `a = (خ£لµ¢ zلµ¢)/âˆڑk` (Lee et al. 2008, the GSVA `zscore` method). Zero-SD reference **throws** (reference-code `fatalError`, a behavioural deviation from the prose "z â†گ NA" spec â€” the two cBioPortal sources disagree); reference `{2,2,4,6,6}` â†’ دƒ=2 so x=10â†’3.0 over / x=8â†’2.0 boundary-not-outlier / x=4â†’0.0 / x=âˆ’1â†’âˆ’2.5 under, signature `{3,1,âˆ’1,1}`â†’2.0 & single-gene `{2.5}`â†’2.5 oracles. **Orthogonal** to the copy-number / clonal-structure ONCO units ([[copy-number-alteration-classification]], [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]]) â€” the diploid reference option touches copy number only as an input filter. Two scope assumptions (caller-supplied cohort + signature; inputs pre-normalized) + one behavioural deviation (throw not NA); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-expr-001-evidence]].
- [[gene-fusion-detection-read-evidence]] â€” Oncology family, fourteenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-FUSION-001), and the wiki's **first gene-fusion / read-evidence structural-rearrangement method**: the STAR-Fusion / Arriba **split-read + discordant-pair + minimum-support** candidate-fusion caller (BCR-ABL1 / EML4-ALK / TMPRSS2-ERG). **DETECTED** iff (junction â‰¥ `MIN_JUNCTION_READS`=1 AND total â‰¥ `MIN_SUM_FRAGS`=2) OR (zero junction AND discordant â‰¥ `MIN_SPANNING_FRAGS_ONLY`=5), where **total support = split_reads1 + split_reads2 + discordant_mates** (Arriba) and the **gene5p â‰  gene3p** distinct-gene invariant rejects self-fusions; results ordered by descending support (STAR-Fusion scores by "abundance of fusion-supporting reads"). Plus a standalone **exon-phase in-frame** check `(5' coding bases âˆ’ 3' start phase) mod 3 == 0` (Genomics England / Wikipedia Reading-frame). Oracles: EML4-ALK(3,2,4)/TMPRSS2-ERG(1,0,1)/CD74-ROS1(0,0,5) DETECTED, NCOA4-RET(0,0,4) span<5 / KIF5B-RET(1,0,0) sum<2 / ALK-ALK same-gene REJECTED, frame 300/0â†’in 301/0â†’out 301/1â†’in. Consumes **already-grouped candidate breakpoint counts** (Arriba schema, not raw BAM â€” chimeric-read extraction is a separate `FindChimericReads`) and does **not** scan for a premature stop before the junction (Arriba `stop-codon` value, ONCO-FUSION-003 scope). **Orthogonal** to the copy-number/clonal and clinical-interpretation ONCO units, distinct from the gene-order [[genome-rearrangement-breakpoint-distance]]. Two scope assumptions; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-fusion-001-evidence]].
- [[gene-fusion-nomenclature-known-fusion-lookup]] â€” Oncology family, fifteenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-FUSION-002), the wiki's fusion **annotation/naming** method: the **HGNC gene-fusion designation** `GetFusionAnnotation(5p,3p) = "5p::3p"` (Bruford et al. 2021 â€” `::` double-colon separator, **5â€²-partner-first** directional order irrespective of chromosomal location, HGNC approved symbols, read-throughs keep the hyphen `INS-IGF2`) plus the **directional known-fusion match** `MatchKnownFusions` against a **caller-supplied** set keyed by `5â€²::3â€²`, case-insensitive. A **Framework** algorithm â€” format/keying source-backed (Bruford 2021 + consortium extension letter), set contents caller-supplied (no bundled Mitelman/COSMIC/ChimerDB). `BCR::ABL1` worked example; `A::B â‰  B::A` reciprocal-direction and hyphen â‰  `::` corner cases; null/empty rejected. The **naming layer downstream** of the read-evidence caller [[gene-fusion-detection-read-evidence]] (annotation round-trips through a `DetectFusions` `FusionCall`), distinct from the ONCO-FUSION-003 premature-stop scope; orthogonal to the copy-number/clonal and clinical-interpretation ONCO units. Two assumptions (caller-supplied set, case-insensitivity); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-fusion-002-evidence]].
- [[fusion-breakpoint-frame-and-protein-prediction]] â€” Oncology family, sixteenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-FUSION-003), the **protein-consequence** third member of the fusion trio: given a fusion breakpoint it computes the **four-state** `BreakpointFrameStatus` (`InFrame`/`OutOfFrame`/`StopCodon`/`NotPredicted`) and reconstructs the **fusion protein**. Follows **Arriba's two-way** native-frame model (Uhrig 2021 `reading_frame`/`site` columns) â€” the in/out call is whether the 3â€² gene is read in its NATIVE frame via the exon-phase rule `(5' coding bases âˆ’ 3' start phase) mod 3 == 0` (reused from [[gene-fusion-detection-read-evidence]] ONCO-FUSION-001) â€” deliberately **not** AGFusion's three-way class (`in-frame (with mutation)`, contiguous ORF multiple-of-3 but 3â€² frameshifted, maps to **`OutOfFrame`**). Gated by breakpoint-site classification: a breakpoint in UTR/intron/non-coding-exon/intergenic â†’ `NotPredicted`. `PredictFusionProtein` follows AGFusion `model.py` exactly: 5â€² CDS prefix + 3â€² CDS suffix â†’ concatenate â†’ translate (transl_table=1) â†’ **truncate at first stop** (out-of-frame trims to whole codons first). Oracles `ATGAAA|GATGGT`â†’`MKDG`, `ATGAAA|GATTAAGGT`â†’`MKD` (in-frame premature stop), `ATGA|AAGGT` phase-0â†’`OutOfFrame` yet clean `MKG` (the Arriba-vs-AGFusion divergence point) / phase-1â†’in-frame, `ATGAA|GATGGT`â†’trim-to-9 `MKM`. Downstream of ONCO-FUSION-001 (elaborates its binary in-frame check into a full consequence + transcript/peptide reconstruction, the premature-stop scope both siblings deferred here), orthogonal to the naming unit [[gene-fusion-nomenclature-known-fusion-lookup]] and to the copy-number/clonal and clinical-interpretation ONCO units. One API-shape assumption (caller supplies CDS strings + junction offsets, no bundled GTF); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-fusion-003-evidence]].
- [[intratumor-heterogeneity-metrics]] â€” Oncology family, seventeenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-HETERO-001): the **scalar-summary ITH-metric layer** that reduces the reconstructed clonal structure to comparable numbers â€” the **MATH score** `100آ·1.4826آ·median(|VAFâˆ’median VAF|)/median(VAF)` (Mroz & Rocco 2013 / Mroz 2015 / maftools `mathScore.R`, three-way identical; the ratio of the width to the centre of the mutant-allele-fraction distribution, no clustering needed), the **Shannon clonal diversity** `H = âˆ’خ£ pلµ¢ ln pلµ¢` (natural log, Liu 2017 / Shannon 1948), the **subclone count** (Liu richness = number of occupied CCF clusters), and the **subclonal fraction** `#(CCF<0.95)/n` (Landau 2013 threshold). MATH oracles 49.42 (odd) / 59.304 (even); Shannon 0 / ln2 / ln4; zero-median-VAFâ†’throw, MAD=0â†’MATH=0. **Depends on** [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]] (subclone count + Shannon pلµ¢ consume its CCF clusters) and reuses the 0.95 clonal threshold of [[clonal-subclonal-classification-ccf-posterior]]; a summary layer, NOT per-mutation reconstruction; shares the Shannon-index math but not the domain with [[alpha-diversity]]. Two source-consistent assumptions (Shannon pلµ¢ = per-cluster mutation proportions; R even-count median); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-hetero-001-evidence]].
- [[hla-nomenclature-and-allele-specific-loh]] â€” Oncology family, eighteenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-HLA-001), the wiki's **first HLA / immuno-oncology antigen-presentation method**: two disjoint pieces sharing the HLA locus â€” (1) **HLA allele nomenclature parsing/validation** of the WHO IPD-IMGT/HLA name `HLA-[Gene]*[F1]:[F2][:F3][:F4][suffix]` (Marsh 2010 colon-delimited convention; Field1 type/allele-group / Field2 specific protein / Field3 synonymous / Field4 non-coding; **two-field "four-digit" minimum**, four-field maximum, `HLA-` prefix required, numeric fields, `N/L/S/C/A/Q` expression-suffix set â€” `HLA-A*24:02:01:02L` valid, `HLA-A*02`/`A*02:01`/five-fields/`â€¦X` rejected), and (2) **allele-specific HLA LOH** by the **LOHHLA** rule (McGranahan 2017 *Cell* / `mskcc/lohhla`): per-allele copy number from tumor-vs-germline logR + BAF, call HLA LOH iff min copy number **< 0.5** AND allelic-imbalance paired Student's t-test **p < 0.01** â€” both strict `<`, the p-test the explicit "avoid over-calling LOH" guard; oracles (1.8, 0.30, 0.001)â†’LOH allele 2 / (1.60, 0.40, 0.05)â†’no (pâ‰¥0.01) / (1.50, 0.50, 0.001)â†’no (0.5 not <0.5) / (1.70, 0.40, 0.01)â†’no (0.01 not <0.01); the **HLA-locus specialization** of the genome-wide allele-specific copy-number / LOH derivation [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] (same logR + BAF allelic-contrast idea restricted to the HLA genes), a mechanism of immune escape via lost neoantigen presentation; one assumption (both alleles <0.5 â†’ distinct `HomozygousLoss` label, thresholds unchanged); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-hla-001-evidence]].
- [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]] â€” Oncology family, nineteenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-HRD-001): the **HRD composite genomic-scar score** `HRD = LOH + TAI + LST`, an **unweighted sum** of three large-scale copy-number scar counts with the **HRD-high cutoff â‰¥ 42** inclusive (Telli 2016 + Stewart 2022, independently corroborated). All three components **derived per segment** from the [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] major/minor CN substrate in `DetectHRD(segments)`: **HRD-LOH** = LOH regions > 15 Mb & < whole chromosome, excluding whole-chr-LOH chromosomes (Abkevich 2012 / oncoscanR / scarHRD `calc.hrd.R`, no centromere table needed); **TAI** = imbalanced (major â‰  minor CN) segments reaching a sub-telomere but not crossing the centromere (Birkbak 2012 / scarHRD `calc.ai_new.R`, sub-1 Mb dropped, single-segment whole-chr imbalance excluded); **LST** = adjacent â‰¥ 10 Mb same-arm regions separated by < 3 Mb after iterative 3 Mb smoothing (Popova 2012 / scarHRD `calc.lst.R`, autosomes only). TAI + LST need the per-chromosome centromere `[start,end]` **acen** table embedded for GRCh38/GRCh37 (UCSC cytoBand cross-verified vs NCBI GRC â€” resolving the prior "centromere table unretrievable" blocker). Oracles (14,14,14)â†’42 HRD-high / (14,13,14)â†’41 negative / (0,0,0)â†’0. The genomic-scar aggregation layer above [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]], distinct from the total-CN [[aneuploidy-detection]]; one even-ploidy AI-path assumption; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-hrd-001-evidence]].
- [[immune-infiltration-deconvolution]] â€” Oncology family, twentieth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-IMMUNE-001), the wiki's **second expression/transcriptome method**: **immune infiltration estimation** â€” quantifies the tumor immune microenvironment two ways. (1) **Cell-type deconvolution** of the linear mixture `m = Sآ·f` (خ£f=1, fâ‰¥0): CIBERSORT **خ½-SVR** `DeconvoluteImmuneCellsNuSvr` (Newman 2015 / Schأ¶lkopf 2000 linear-kernel خ½-SVR â€” z-standardize m + signature columns, sweep خ½âˆˆ{0.25,0.5,0.75} by **lowest RMSE**, zero-clip negatives + normalize to خ£=1; cross-validated by planted-truth `m=Sآ·f` recovery + scikit-learn `NuSVR`/libsvm match) with the NNLS/LLSR baseline `DeconvoluteImmuneCells` (Abbas 2009) retained. (2) **ESTIMATE** ssGSEA immune/stromal enrichment `EstimateInfiltration` (**simplified** = rank-weighted mean of signature genes, not full KS running-sum) + opt-in **tumor purity** `EstimateTumorPurity` = `cos(0.6049872018 + 0.0001467884آ·ESTIMATE)` (verbatim, confirmed 3 sources + tidyestimate R; **Affymetrix-only** calibration, negative cosine â†’ **NaN**, monotone-decreasing). MCP-counter geometric-mean marker abundance noted. Signature matrices: **LM22** (547 genes أ— 22 cell types) **caller-supplied** â€” Stanford licence forbids redistribution/modification/commercial use, no exact-CIBERSORT parity claim, `LoadSignatureMatrix` LM22-format loader only; **ABIS-Seq** (Monaco 2019, CC BY 4.0, 1296 genes أ— 17 types) **bundled** as embedded resource via `LoadBundledAbisSignatureMatrix` so deconvolution works out-of-the-box (not an LM22 substitute); synthetic 5-marker `DefaultSignatureMatrix` for tests. Oracles: planted {CD8 0.60,B_naive 0.30,Mono 0.10}â†’{0.5971,0.2989,0.1040} corr 0.99997; sklearn cross-check خ½=0.75 {A 0.5085,B 0.1795,C 0.3120}; ABIS {NK 0.60,MonoC 0.40}â†’{â‰ˆ0.650,â‰ˆ0.350} corr 0.996 (tol 0.06) & pure MonoC 1.0 exactly; ABIS ref `CD8A`/T CD8 Mem=1060.1507652944399. Corner cases: collinear cell types (resting/activated NK) recover support but looser proportions; missing/non-overlapping genes â†’ unreliable/zero; non-hematopoietic content in residual; ESTIMATE solid-tumors-only. Antigen-agnostic quantitative sibling of the immuno-oncology [[hla-nomenclature-and-allele-specific-loh]], shares the ssGSEA signature-scoring layer with [[expression-outlier-zscore-signature-score]]; two scope assumptions (LM22 caller-supplied, simplified ssGSEA) + Affymetrix purity domain, no contradictions; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-immune-001-evidence]].
- [[loss-of-heterozygosity-detection]] â€” Oncology family, twenty-first ONCO-* unit (ONCO-LOH-001): the standalone genome-wide **LOH caller** â€” `DetectLOH` counts **HRD-LOH** regions (minor CN 0 **and** major CN â‰  0 = allelic loss not homozygous deletion; length **strictly > 15 Mb**, length = end âˆ’ start; excluding any **whole-chromosome** global-LOH chromosome via `chrDel`) and `CalculateLOHFraction` returns the length-weighted per-chromosome LOH fraction âˆˆ [0,1]. Abkevich 2012 (intermediate-size LOH â†” BRCA1/2 deficiency) + scarHRD `calc.hrd.R`/`scar_score.R` (exact R criterion + 15 Mb cut-off + `chrDel`; major CN capped to 1 so LOH state, not absolute CN, drives merging) + oncoscanR `score_loh` (independent corroboration; adjacent/overlapping LOH merged â‰¤ 1 bp first). Synthetic 7-segment dataset â†’ score **1** (only the 20 Mb chr1 segment; exactly-15 Mb / het-retained / homozygous-deletion / whole-chr-LOH all excluded); LOH-fraction 0.333/0.0/1.0. This **is** the LOH term the composite [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]] sums with TAI + LST (centromere-free, unlike its siblings), reads its segments off [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]], and is the genome-wide counterpart of the HLA-locus [[hla-nomenclature-and-allele-specific-loh]] (LOHHLA). Two assumptions (segment input shape; length-weighted LOH-fraction is a definitional/API choice); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-loh-001-evidence]].
- [[mhc-peptide-binding-prediction]] â€” Oncology family, twenty-second ONCO-* unit (ONCO-MHC-001): the wiki's first **MHC / peptide-presentation prediction** method â€” the affinity gate of neoantigen candidate scoring, three layers over one `Strong`/`Weak`/`NonBinder` output. (1) **Classification**: IC50 tiers `< 50` Strong / `< 500` Weak / `â‰¥ 500` NonBinder (Sette 1994 â‰ˆ 500 nM CTL threshold + IEDB) and NetMHCpan-4.1 %Rank tiers (class I SB `< 0.5` / WB `< 2`, class II `< 2` / `< 10`, all strict `<`; Reynisson 2020), + peptide-length validity (class I **8â€“14**, class II 13â€“25). (2) **Matrix prediction**: BIMAS **product rule** (Tآ½ = const آ· âˆڈ coeffs, 180 coeffs + const, unlisted = 1.0; Parker 1994) and SMM **additive** rule `IC50 = 50000^(1âˆ’score)` (Peters & Sette 2005 / IEDB log50k; 0â†’50000, 0.5â†’223.6068, 1â†’1 nM). (3) Ported **MHCflurry 2.0** pan-allele class-I NN (BLOSUM62 `left_pad_centered_right_pad` 45أ—21 peptide + 37-residue allele pseudosequence 37أ—21, `tanh` Dense `feedforward`/`with-skip-connections`, `to_ic50 = 50000^(1âˆ’x)`, geometric-mean ensemble; matches `mhcflurry` 2.1.5 to < 0.03 %). **Framework/packaging** â€” trained matrices caller-supplied (BIMAS CGI defunct / Parker paywalled / IEDB non-commercial) and 80 MB ensemble not embedded (one member for CI + `LoadWeightPack`), explicitly analogized in-file to CIBERSORT LM22 of [[immune-infiltration-deconvolution]]. Downstream of neoantigen generation [[neoantigen-peptide-generation]] (ONCO-NEO-001), presentation-machinery sibling of [[hla-nomenclature-and-allele-specific-loh]] (HLA LOH removes the platform); class I 8â€“14 resolved vs NetMHCpan-4.1; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-mhc-001-evidence]].
- [[tumor-informed-mrd-detection]] â€” Oncology family, twenty-third ONCO-* unit (ONCO-MRD-001): the liquid-biopsy **MRD calling / statistical-detection** layer that `depends_on` and reuses the Poisson quantification primitive [[ctdna-detection-and-tumor-fraction]] (ONCO-CTDNA-001). Two engines. (1) **Signatera positivity** (`DetectMRD`): tumor-informed workflow â€” up to 16 WES-selected clonal somatic SNVs tracked in plasma cfDNA â€” **MRD-positive iff â‰¥ 2 of the 16 tracked variants are detected** (Reinert 2019 / PMC9265001 Table 1; 0/1â†’negative, 2/3â†’positive), panel Poisson `p = 1 âˆ’ e^(âˆ’nfm)`, sensitivity scales with panel size (>8 markers at â‰¤0.1% VAF, LoD 0.01% / specificity >99.5%; post-op ctDNA+ â†’ HR 7.2 relapse), longitudinal `TrackVariantsOverTime` (per-timepoint + first-positive). (2) **INVAR GLRT** (Wan 2020 + INVAR2 verbatim): per-locus mixture `q = pآ·g + e(1âˆ’p)`, EM ctDNA-fraction, `LR = logL(pج‚) âˆ’ logL(0)` (pure background â†’ pج‚â‰ˆ0/LRâ‰ˆ0; AF/SNR-weighted, monotone), `IntegratedMutantAlleleFractionV2` background-subtracted depth-weighted, fragment-size-weighted GLRT (`EstimateInvarSignalWithSize`/`FragmentSizeProfile`/`InvarMolecule`; discrete `COUNT/TOTAL` default + opt-in Gaussian-KDE `FromKernelDensity`; flat P1==P0 â†’ reduces to no-size), outlier suppression `SuppressOutlierLoci` (repolish binomial + Bonferroni), control-derived background `EstimateLocusBackground`/`PassesBothStrandsFilter`. Distinct from ONCO-CTDNA-001 (multi-variant verdict vs single-reporter probability); one flagged per-variant "detected"=â‰¥1 alt read assumption (tunable); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-mrd-001-evidence]].
- [[microsatellite-instability-detection]] â€” Oncology family, twenty-fourth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-MSI-001): the **microsatellite-instability biomarker** â€” MSI from unstable-loci fraction + status classification. Two inputs, two classifiers. (1) **Continuous MSI score** = `unstable loci / valid loci` (as %) with **MSI-High cutoff â‰¥ 20%** inclusive (MSIsensor2 niu-lab README verbatim; per-site **chi-square** tumor-vs-normal repeat-length test at **FDR 0.05**, score = "% sites with a somatic indel", Niu 2014; tumor-only mode unchanged; the original cohort's **3.5%** separation is dataset-specific, not the production cutoff) â†’ classified **binary** MSI-H (â‰¥20%) vs not-High only. (2) **Categorical Bethesda** marker-count over the validated 5-marker panel (BAT-25/BAT-26/D2S123/D5S346/D17S250): **0/5â†’MSS آ· 1/5â†’MSI-L آ· â‰¥2/5â†’MSI-H** (Boland 1998, cross-checked vs the 2004 revised-Bethesda â‰¥40% / â‰¥20%&<40% fraction form BJC 2014). Key modelling choice: **no MSI-L band is fabricated for the continuous score** â€” the three-way MSS/MSI-L/MSI-H scheme applies only to the discrete marker count. Oracles 5/25â†’20%â†’MSI-H(boundary) آ· 4/25â†’16%â†’not-High آ· 0/25â†’0%â†’MSS-range; corner cases zero-valid-lociâ†’undefined(throws) آ· unstable>valid/negativeâ†’throws آ· MSS-vs-MSI-L 1-marker low-confidence. An independent immunotherapy/mismatch-repair biomarker orthogonal to the copy-number-scar [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]], consumed by [[cancer-variant-tier-classification-amp-asco-cap]] / [[clinical-actionability-oncokb-levels]]; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-msi-001-evidence]].
- [[neoantigen-peptide-generation]] â€” Oncology family, twenty-fifth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-NEO-001): the **upstream partner** of the affinity gate [[mhc-peptide-binding-prediction]] â€” **neoantigen candidate peptide window generation** (`GenerateNeoantigenPeptides`). Given a somatic **missense SNV** at 1-based position `p` in a protein of length `L`, enumerate **every length-`k` window of the mutant protein that spans the mutated residue** (valid 0-based start `s âˆˆ [max(0, pâˆ’1âˆ’k+1), min(pâˆ’1, Lâˆ’k)]`, count `= last âˆ’ first + 1`; an interior mutation gives exactly `k` windows per length), each paired with its matched **wild-type (germline)** peptide at the same coordinates + the mutation offset â€” the mutant/WT **agretope** on which the differential agretopic index (DAI, Wells 2020 TESLA) is computed. Class I search lengths **8â€“11** (pVACtools Hundal 2020; a 21-mer with the substitution centred = ProGeo-neo Li 2020's آ±10-flank construction contains exactly every overlapping 8â€“11-mer; NetMHCpan 8â€“14 / 9-mer-dominant Jurtz 2017 motivates enumerating 8â€“11 not 9 alone). Oracles: interior **Y5C** on `MKTAYIAKQRSTVWLNDEFGH` â†’ 5 windows per k = 8/9/10/11 â†’ **20** candidates (each WT = mutant with `C`â†’`Y` at the offset); **terminal M1V** k = 9 â†’ exactly 1 truncated window `VKTAYIAKQ`/`MKTAYIAKQ` offset 0; corner cases non-coding/synonymous â†’ no peptide, length outside 8â€“11 not enumerated, short-protein skips that `k`. **Missense-only** (frameshift/indel/fusion neopeptides out of scope, separate translation) and **binding affinity out of scope** (IC50/%Rank scoring caller-supplied via the downstream [[mhc-peptide-binding-prediction]] ONCO-MHC-001 gate, whose resolved class I 8â€“14 window propagates to this generator's default); presentation-platform sibling [[hla-nomenclature-and-allele-specific-loh]] (HLA LOH removes the restricted allele). Two source-backed scoping assumptions; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-neo-001-evidence]].
- [[tumor-phylogeny-clonal-tree-reconstruction]] â€” Oncology family, twenty-sixth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-PHYLO-001): the **clonal-tree reconstruction** layer â€” assemble per-cluster **cancer cell fractions (CCF)** into a rooted **clonal-evolution tree**, deciding parentâ†’child descent via two per-sample CCF-ordering constraints from **LICHeE** (Popic 2015) and **PICTograph** (Zheng 2022): **lineage precedence** (ancestor CCF â‰¥ descendant CCF âˆ’ خµ per sample, + presence pattern `u.CCF=0 â‡’ v.CCF=0`; LICHeE Eq. 2) and the **sum rule** (children CCF sum â‰¤ parent CCF + خµ per node â€” the cell-fraction **pigeonhole generalization**; LICHeE Eq. 5 / PICTograph sum condition â€” what forces **branching vs nesting**), plus **trunk** (CCF-â‰ˆ1 root-path clusters = clonal) vs **branch** (subclones) identification. A **constraint-satisfaction / perfect-phylogeny** builder, **not** distance-based Neighbor-Joining / UPGMA. Oracles: linear Normalâ†’Aâ†’Bâ†’C (1.0/1.0/0.6/0.3, Trunk {A}); two-sample branching Aâ†’{B,C} (B 0.6/0.0, C 0.0/0.7 â€” each private, absent in the other's sample, so mutually non-ancestral; sum under A per sample 0.6 & 0.7 â‰¤ 1.0); equal 0.6/0.6 siblings forced into a chain Normalâ†’Aâ†’Bâ†’C by the sum rule (0.6+0.6=1.2 > 1.0). Two reconstructed-tree **invariants** as oracles (ancestor CCF â‰¥ descendant per edge; per-node sum rule); emptyâ†’root-only, single clusterâ†’trunk. **Downstream of** the CCF clustering [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]] (ONCO-CCF-001, which produces the clusters it orders), the structural counterpart of the per-mutation trunkâ†”clonal / branchâ†”subclonal [[clonal-subclonal-classification-ccf-posterior]], and the structure the heterogeneity metrics [[intratumor-heterogeneity-metrics]] summarize. Two source-consistent assumptions (deepest-valid-ancestor deterministic tie-break; default خµ=0 strict inequalities); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-phylo-001-evidence]].
- [[tumor-ploidy-estimation-and-whole-genome-doubling]] â€” Oncology family, twenty-seventh ONCO-* unit (ONCO-PLOIDY-001): two **post-hoc genome-state summaries** over already-called allele-specific segments (shared `AlleleSpecificSegment` = Major+Minor CN, not raw logR/BAF): (1) **average ploidy** `EstimatePloidy` = length-weighted mean total CN **دˆ = خ£(CN_iآ·L_i)/خ£(L_i)** (Patchwork PMC4053982; n-scale Van Loo 2010, pure diploid â†’ 2.0, >2.7n aneuploidy; CN 2/4/3 at 100/100/50 Mb â†’ 3.0, genuinely length-weighted not plain segment mean); (2) **whole-genome doubling** `DetectWholeGenomeDoubling` = facets-suite `is_genome_doubled` / Bielski 2018 rule â€” WGD iff **autosome-restricted fraction at major CN â‰¥ 2 strictly > 0.5** (`mcn = tcn âˆ’ lcn`; major not total CN, so all-1:1 â†’ not doubled), denominator = **reference chromosome-size table** (`ReferenceGenome {GRCh38,GRCh37}`, UCSC hg38/hg19 Ensembl-verified, خ£chr1â€“22 = 2,875,001,522 / 2,881,033,286 bp) NOT supplied segments, autosomes only (sex chromosomes excluded); half+1â†’true / exactly-halfâ†’false (strict) / 100 Mb ampâ†’0.035 false / chrX-onlyâ†’false oracles, legacy `DetectWholeGenomeDoublingFromSuppliedLength` keeps the supplied-length denominator (60%â†’true/50%â†’false). **Distinct from** the joint grid fit [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] (ONCO-ASCAT-001 *fits* دپ/دˆ from raw logR/BAF; this *summarizes* دˆ post-segmentation), reads the same segment substrate as [[loss-of-heterozygosity-detection]] / [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]]. Two assumptions (input shape; resolved reference-genome WGD denominator); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-ploidy-001-evidence]].
- [[tumor-purity-from-mutation-vaf]] â€” Oncology family, twenty-eighth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-PURITY-001): a **standalone closed-form tumor-purity estimator** that inverts the **CNAqc expected-VAF generative model** `v = mآ·د€آ·c/[2(1âˆ’د€)+د€(n_A+n_B)]` (Antonello 2024) to recover purity د€ from a somatic-SNV VAF + local allele-specific copy number: `EstimatePurityFromVAF` = the copy-neutral diploid heterozygous special case **د€ = 2آ·VAF** (clonal c=1, het m=1, n_tot=2; VAF 0.30â†’0.60, band 0.55â€“0.65â†”VAF 0.275â€“0.325, invariant 0â‰¤د€â‰¤1) and `EstimatePurity` = the general inversion `د€ = 2v/(mآ·c + 2v âˆ’ vآ·n_tot)` recovering د€=1 on a 2:1 (n_tot=3) segment for both m=1 (v=1/3) and m=2 (v=2/3). The `2(1âˆ’د€)+د€آ·n_tot` denominator (normal diploid weighted 1âˆ’د€ + tumour) is confirmed by **FACETS** (Shen & Seshan 2016) and inverted the other way by **ABSOLUTE** (Carter 2012). Corner cases: multiplicity ambiguity on amplified segments (two VAF peaks 1/3, 2/3 â€” need CN state + m), subclonal c<1 depresses VAF (use **clonal** mutations or underestimate purity), purity <0.1 below detection, no informative variants â†’ undefined. **`alternative_to`** the joint logR/BAF grid fit [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] (ONCO-ASCAT-001 â€” same purity scalar, different substrate + method), mutation-VAF counterpart to the ploidy-side [[tumor-ploidy-estimation-and-whole-genome-doubling]], shares the diploid `د€=2آ·VAF` inversion with [[ctdna-detection-and-tumor-fraction]]. Two modelling-scope assumptions (copy-neutral-diploid default, median cross-variant aggregation); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-purity-001-evidence]].
- [[sbs96-mutational-signature-catalog]] â€” Oncology family, twenty-ninth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-SIG-001): the wiki's first **mutational-signature** method â€” the **SBS-96 trinucleotide context catalog**, the classification step that builds the 96-channel single-base-substitution spectrum downstream signature fitting decomposes. A **channel** = a substitution + its centred trinucleotide context: **6** subtypes named by the **pyrimidine** of the mutated Watsonâ€“Crick pair (`C>A/C>G/C>T/T>A/T>C/T>G`) **أ— 4** 5â€² bases **أ— 4** 3â€² bases = **96**, labelled `5'[REF>ALT]3'` (COSMIC SBS96 + SigProfilerMatrixGenerator Bergstrom 2019 + Alexandrov 2013, identical 6أ—4أ—4 definition). The defining rule is **pyrimidine-strand folding**: a **purine (A/G) reference** base is reverse-complemented (context via Aâ†”T/Câ†”G then reverse, plus the substitution) onto the pyrimidine strand before counting; a C/T reference classifies to itself, centre unchanged. Worked fold TGA/Gâ†’T â†’ revcomp TCA + G>Tâ†’C>A â†’ `T[C>A]A`; oracles A,C,A,Aâ†’A[C>A]A آ· G,T,C,Aâ†’G[T>C]A آ· A,A,T,Aâ†’T[T>A]T. Catalog **partition** invariants: exactly 96 canonical keys, خ£ per-channel counts = number of classifiable SBS variants. Corner cases: purine-ref must fold (never counted directly), non-SBS variants (indels/DBS) excluded, non-ACGT context unclassifiable, ref==alt out of scope. **Catalog/classification only** â€” the NMF/NNLS signature-exposure fitting against COSMIC reference signatures is a separate downstream concern. A somatic-mutation-spectrum biomarker orthogonal to the copy-number-scar [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]] and the mismatch-repair [[microsatellite-instability-detection]]; one cosmetic label-rendering assumption; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-sig-001-evidence]].
- [[mutational-signature-fitting-and-extraction]] â€” Oncology family, thirtieth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-SIG-002): the **downstream signature-deconvolution** partner of the catalog [[sbs96-mutational-signature-catalog]] (which it `depends_on`) â€” decompose the 96-channel SBS spectrum into **signatures أ— exposures** two ways. **Supervised refit** by **non-negative least squares** `min_x â€–Sآ·xâˆ’dâ€–â‚‚آ², xâ‰¥0` (MutationalPatterns/deconstructSigs; Lawson-Hanson active-set â€” clamp any would-be-negative coefficient to 0 and refit, S=[[1,1],[0,1]], d=[0,1]â†’x=[0,0.5]; reconstruction `Sآ·x`, **cosine â‰¥ 0.95** quality gate, raw counts + proportion `x/خ£x` exposures). **Unsupervised de-novo extraction** by **NMF** `V â‰ˆ WH` (Lee & Seung multiplicative updates, **Frobenius** default + **KL/Poisson** enhancement, both **monotonically non-increasing**; Alexandrov blind-source-separation W=signatures/H=exposures; COSMIC **L1-normalize** each W column to 1). Shared **cosine similarity** `Aآ·B/(â€–Aâ€–â€–Bâ€–)âˆˆ[0,1]` (identicalâ†’1, orthogonalâ†’0, [1,1]/[1,0]â†’1/âˆڑ2, scale-invariant, **zero-normâ†’0.0** by convention). **Rank selection** = Brunet-2004 **cophenetic correlation** (consensus of argmax-over-H connectivity matrices; rank-1 trivially 1.0) + SigProfiler **silhouette stability**; **reference matching** = greedy best-cosine to COSMIC. Sharp edges: NMF **non-convex â†’ local minimum** (planted-truth + fixed-seed recovery only), **permutation/scale ambiguity**, خµ-guarded denominators. The NNLS refit and NMF extraction are `alternative_to` each other over the same `V â‰ˆ WH` model; the fitted exposure profile feeds the clinical-interpretation ONCO units, orthogonal to [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]] / [[microsatellite-instability-detection]]; five modelling assumptions (Frobenius, seeded init, proportions, zero-cosine, consensus/silhouette/greedy matching); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-sig-002-evidence]].
- [[signature-exposure-bootstrap-confidence-intervals]] â€” Oncology family, thirty-first ONCO-* unit (ONCO-SIG-003): the **signature-exposure uncertainty** layer over the NNLS refit [[mutational-signature-fitting-and-extraction]] (which it `depends_on`) â€” a **resample â†’ refit â†’ percentile** loop that turns the point-estimate exposure vector into a **per-signature confidence interval**. Resample the 96-channel catalog `R` times (default 1000; sigminer â‰¥100), re-run the ONCO-SIG-002 **NNLS** `FitSignatures` per replicate, and report the **[2.5%, 97.5%] percentiles** (Efron 1979 percentile CI) read off the finite bootstrap sample by the **type-7** quantile (Hyndman & Fan 1996, `h=pآ·(nâˆ’1)`, R/NumPy default). **Two resampling schemes** differing only by whether total burden N is fixed: **multinomial** (sigminer `sample(...,prob=catalog/خ£)` = fixed-N multinomial(N,p), the byte-for-byte **default**) vs **Poisson** (Senkin 2021 MSA variant, each channel `Poisson(observedâ‚–)`, N unfixed, justified by the Poissonâ†”multinomial conditional equivalence). The **discriminating** corner case is a single non-zero channel: multinomial **collapses deterministically** (width 0, point=mean=lower=upper) while **Poisson(خ»>0) fluctuates** (variance=mean â†’ positive width â€” the reason the Poisson variant was added); plus N=0â†’[0,0] and R=1â†’lower=upper=mean. Invariants Lowerâ‰¤Meanâ‰¤Upper, exposures â‰¥0 (NNLS), fixed-seed determinism; type-7 oracles [0,1,2,3,4]â†’0.1/2.0/3.9 and [2,4,6,8]â†’2.15/5.0/7.85. The uncertainty layer two steps above the [[sbs96-mutational-signature-catalog]] spectrum; two source-aligned assumptions (type-7 interpolation, fixed seed 42); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-sig-003-evidence]].
- [[mutational-process-classification]] â€” Oncology family, thirty-second ONCO-* unit (ONCO-SIG-004): the **aetiology-annotation** layer over the fit [[mutational-signature-fitting-and-extraction]] (which it `depends_on`) â€” turn per-signature **exposures** into a set of **active mutational processes** via **normalize â†’ cutoff â†’ map â†’ aggregate**. Normalize to relative contributions `Wلµ¢ = exposureلµ¢/خ£exposure` (deconstructSigs "weights between 0 and 1"); drop any `Wلµ¢ < 0.06` (the deconstructSigs `signature.cutoff = 0.06` / `weights[weights < signature.cutoff] <- 0`, **strict `<`** so exactly 0.06 is retained, empirically 1.4% false-negative rate); map each surviving COSMIC label to its **proposed aetiology** (SBS1/5â†’**Aging** clock-like, SBS2/13â†’**APOBEC**, SBS4â†’**Tobacco**, SBS7aâ€“dâ†’**UV**, SBS6/15/20/26â†’**MMR deficiency**; COSMIC + Alexandrov 2020); **sum** member contributions per process â†’ **active-process set** + `argmax` **dominant process**. Worked oracle SBS2/13/1/4 = 50/30/15/5 (خ£=100) â†’ APOBEC 0.80 (dominant) / Aging 0.15 / Tobacco 0 (SBS4 0.05 below cutoff). Corner cases: surviving mass can sum < 1 (rest "unknown"), several processes reported simultaneously, an unmapped or "Unknown"-aetiology label contributes to no process (SBS5's aetiology is literally "Unknown (clock-like)" yet grouped as Aging), خ£=0 â†’ no active/dominant process, custom `signature.cutoff` overridable.
