The interpretation layer answering "**which processes are active?**" one step above ONCO-SIG-002's "how much of each signature?" and ONCO-SIG-003's "how confident?"; orthogonal to the copy-number-scar [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]] and mismatch-repair [[microsatellite-instability-detection]] (whose MMR signal SBS6/15/20/26 echo here as a signature-based read), feeds [[cancer-variant-tier-classification-amp-asco-cap]] / [[clinical-actionability-oncokb-levels]]; two source-aligned assumptions (per-process summation, per-signature-cutoff-then-group); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-sig-004-evidence]].
- [[somatic-variant-calling-tumor-normal]] â€” Oncology family, thirty-third ONCO-* unit (ONCO-SOMATIC-001): the **foundational somatic SNV caller** at the head of the pipeline â€” classify each candidate variant **Somatic / Germline / NotDetected** by comparing **tumor allele frequency `f_t`** against **matched-normal `f_n`** (`VAF = altReads/totalReads`). Strelka's somatic state `S = {(f_t,f_n): f_tâ‰ f_n}` restricted to a **ref/ref normal genotype** (Saunders 2012; the raw somatic probability over-calls in LOH/CN regions) / Strelka2 continuous-VAF somatic-LOD+VAF comparison (Kim 2018). **Three configurable thresholds**: tumor **LoD f_t â‰¥ 0.05** (Yan 2021 WES 5% LoD, â‰¤5% frequently sequencing errors â†’ NotDetected), normal **"absent" ceiling f_n â‰¤ 0.01** (`normalVafThreshold`), f_n above ceiling with substantial f_t â†’ **Germline** (Mutect2 germline filter, Benjamin 2019). Bounded monotone **somatic score `max(0, f_t âˆ’ f_n)` âˆˆ [0,1]** (a documented simplification, not a caller LOD). **Tumor-only mode**: no matched normal â†’ Mutect2 `â„“_n = 1`, tumor-only call; `FilterGermlineVariants` returns the somatic **subset** of input. Oracles A 0.25/0.00â†’Somatic(0.25) آ· B 0.48/0.50â†’Germline(0) آ· C 0.02â†’NotDetected آ· D CHIP-like 0.30/0.03â†’Germline آ· E tumor-only 0.20/(0/0)â†’Somatic آ· boundaries f_t=0.05 present / f_n=0.01 absent. The **upstream caller** whose raw call set the two pre-interpretation QC filters clean â€” technical-artifact [[sequencing-artifact-detection]] + biological-origin [[clonal-hematopoiesis-cfdna-filtering]] â€” before the clinical-significance units; two flagged source-consistent assumptions (1% normal ceiling parameterized not invented; score a documented simplification); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-somatic-001-evidence]].
- [[chromothripsis-inference]] â€” Oncology family, thirty-fourth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-SV-001), and the wiki's **first complex-rearrangement / chromothripsis** method: a **region-level pattern classifier** that consumes a per-segment integer copy-number profile (+ breakpoints / a clustered-SV count) and classifies **Chromothripsis** vs **NotComplex** by the **Korbel & Campbell 2013** six hallmark criteria, computing two directly â€” criterion B **oscillating copy-number states** (an oscillation = an adjacent-segment CN-state reversal; profile must alternate between â‰¤3, canonically **two**, states) gated by the Magrangeas-2011 **â‰¥10 first-pass oscillation screen**, the Cortأ©s-Ciriano-2020 confidence tiers (**â‰¥7** adjacent oscillating segments high / **4â€“6** low / **<4** not-called), the **>60%** two-state fraction, and the **â‰¥6 clustered intrachromosomal SV** burden floor; and criterion A **breakpoint clustering** via the exponential-null coefficient-of-variation flag (**CV>1**, exponential CV=1). Oracles `2,1,2,1,2,1,2,1,2,1,2`â†’10 two-stateâ†’Chromothripsis آ· `2,1,2,1,2,1`â†’5<10â†’NotComplex آ· `2,3,4,5,6,7` monotoneâ†’0 oscillations/>2 statesâ†’NotComplex (progressive amplification/BFB â€” the "clustering necessary but not sufficient" failure mode). **Consumes** the per-segment CN states of [[copy-number-alteration-classification]] (ONCO-CNA-001) â€” a pattern classifier over that profile, not a per-segment caller â€” orthogonal to the single-junction [[gene-fusion-detection-read-evidence]] and the length-based [[focal-amplification-detection]], distinct from the gene-order [[genome-rearrangement-breakpoint-distance]]. Two operationalisation assumptions (oscillation = CN-state-transition count; clustering = CV>1 vs exponential null); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-sv-001-evidence]].
- [[tumor-mutational-burden]] â€” Oncology family, thirty-fifth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-TMB-001): the **tumor-agnostic immunotherapy biomarker** â€” the continuous **TMB = (counted somatic mutations) / (sequenced coding region in Mb)** in mut/Mb (Chalmers 2017 Methods; the assay's **coding footprint** is the denominator â€” FoundationOne 315-gene = **1.1 Mb**, F1CDx 324-gene â‰ˆ 0.8 Mb, WES â‰ˆ 30â€“40 Mb, taken as a parameter) and the **TMB-High = TMB â‰¥ 10 mut/Mb** classification (FDA pembrolizumab tumor-agnostic approval June 16 2020, F1CDx companion diagnostic, Marcus 2021; boundary **inclusive** â€” 10.0 High, 9.9 not; mut/Mb reporting + cutoff cross-confirmed by the Friends of Cancer Research Harmonization Project, Merino 2020). Panel counting **includes synonymous** alterations to reduce sampling noise while WES counts nonsynonymous; germline/driver filtering happens **upstream** â€” this unit counts the caller-supplied somatic list of [[somatic-variant-calling-tumor-normal]] (ONCO-SOMATIC-001). Oracles 11/1.1â†’10.0 High (315-gene) آ· 300/30â†’10.0 High (WES) آ· 150/10â†’15.0 High آ· 99/10â†’9.9 not-High آ· 0â†’not-High; corner cases `targetRegionMb=0`â†’division-by-zero throws, negative count/region rejected, **<0.5 Mb** panels compute but are known-unstable (documentation, not error), TMB monotone non-decreasing in count / non-increasing in region. An independent immunotherapy biomarker alongside [[microsatellite-instability-detection]] (MSI-H) and correlated with the neoantigen load of [[neoantigen-peptide-generation]], acted on by [[cancer-variant-tier-classification-amp-asco-cap]] / [[clinical-actionability-oncokb-levels]]. **One flagged conflict**: the unsupported registry three-tier "Low <6 / Intermediate 6â€“20 / High >20" scheme (no authoritative source for the 6/20 boundaries) resolved to the single source-backed two-tier â‰¥10 cutoff; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-tmb-001-evidence]].
- [[variant-allele-frequency-and-binomial-ci]] â€” Oncology family, thirty-sixth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-VAF-001): the **foundational VAF primitive** the VAF-based Oncology family sits on â€” three model-free quantities. (1) **Empirical VAF = altReads/totalReads** (= alt AD / sum AD, GATK Mutect2 FAQ; the model-free ratio, **not** Mutect2's model-estimate `AF` field). (2) The **Wilson score binomial confidence interval** on the proportion `center=(pج‚+zآ²/2n)/(1+zآ²/n)`, `margin=(z/(1+zآ²/n))آ·âˆڑ(pج‚(1âˆ’pج‚)/n+zآ²/4nآ²)`, **z=1.96** for 95% (Wilson 1927) â€” the genuinely distinct statistical content **not represented elsewhere**, chosen over **Wald** because it stays within [0,1] with non-zero width at the extremes (`pج‚=0`â†’lower exactly 0 / `pج‚=1`â†’upper exactly 1) where Wald overshoots/collapses. (3) The CNAqc purity/ploidy correction **`AdjustVAFForPurity`** = `mآ·CCF = VAFآ·(2(1âˆ’د€)+د€آ·n_tot)/د€` (inverting CNAqc *Genome Biology* 2024 `v=mد€/(2(1âˆ’د€)+د€آ·n_tot)`, normal ploidy 2). Oracles 25/100â†’0.25 آ· 0/10â†’0.00 آ· 10/10â†’1.00, Wilson (25,100)â†’0.2592 [0.1755,0.3430] & no-overshoot (0,10)â†’[0,0.2775] / (10,10)â†’[0.7225,1], correction (0.40,0.80,2)â†’1.00 / (0.20,0.50,2)â†’0.80 / (0.30,0.50,4)â†’1.80; corner cases VAF>1 alignment-artifact/totalReads=0/د€=0 all guarded. The empirical VAF is the same `altReads/totalReads` [[somatic-variant-calling-tumor-normal]] compares and [[ctdna-detection-and-tumor-fraction]] averages; `AdjustVAFForPurity` shares the CNAqc/Tarabichi model [[tumor-purity-from-mutation-vaf]] inverts for د€ and [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]] divides by m for CCF; two source-backed assumptions (z=1.96 verbatim, normal CN=2); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-vaf-001-evidence]].
- [[pan-genome-gene-clustering]] â€” comparative-genomics pan-genome family anchor (first PANGEN-* unit, PANGEN-CLUSTER-001): greedy incremental homolog/ortholog clustering (`ClusterGenes`) on the CD-HIT model (Li & Godzik 2006) â€” process genes longâ†’short, assign each to the first existing cluster whose representative it matches at â‰¥ identity threshold else start a new cluster; global identity = identical aligned positions / alignment length (`-G 1`), Roary default 95% for orthologs (Page 2015); homolog groups only (no gene-neighbourhood/synteny paralog-split step), alignment-free identity may underestimate when internal indels are needed; sibling of [[genome-comparison-core-dispensable]] / [[ortholog-detection-reciprocal-best-hits]] / [[average-nucleotide-identity]]; upstream of [[pan-genome-core-accessory-partition]]; deviations None; record [[pangen-cluster-001-evidence]].
- [[pan-genome-core-accessory-partition]] â€” comparative-genomics pan-genome family, second PANGEN-* unit (PANGEN-CORE-001): the **pan-genome partition** `ConstructPanGenome` **downstream** of the clustering step â€” split gene clusters across N genomes into **core / accessory / unique** by cluster **occupancy** with the fractional Roary rule `occupancy/N â‰¥ coreFraction` ("at least 99% of samples", **not** `floor(coreFractionآ·N)`; hard core >99% / soft core 95â€“99% / shell 15â€“95% / cloud <15%, Page 2015), compute **genomic fluidity** `د†=[2/(N(Nâˆ’1))]آ·خ£_{k<l}(U_k+U_l)/(M_k+M_l)` âˆˆ[0,1] (Kislyuk 2011; 0 identical / 1 disjoint; 3-genome oracle 10/18=0.5ج„), and classify **open âں؛ alpha<1 / closed âں؛ alpha>1** by the **Heaps'-law** decay exponent (Tettelin 2008, micropan); the N-genome occupancy counterpart of the pairwise-RBH [[genome-comparison-core-dispensable]], both the Tettelin 2005 core/dispensable model; downstream of [[pan-genome-gene-clustering]]; two source-backed assumptions (clustering delegated to k-mer-Jaccard `ClusterGenes`, empty-pair fluidity termâ†’0); no contradictions; record [[pangen-core-001-evidence]].
- [[pan-genome-heaps-law-fit]] â€” comparative-genomics pan-genome family, third PANGEN-* unit (PANGEN-HEAP-001): the **pan-genome growth model** / dedicated **Heaps'-law fitting engine** underneath the partition's open/closed facet â€” binarize the gene **presence/absence matrix** (count>0â†’1), extract the **new-gene curve** by the micropan first-appearance rule (a cluster is new at genome iâ‰¥2 when cumulative presence is 1 at row i and 0 at row iâˆ’1; genome index starts at 2), pool over random orderings (n.perm 100), fit the **power law** `y=Kآ·x^(-alpha)` by bounded least squares `J=sqrt(خ£(yâˆ’Kآ·x^(-alpha))آ²)/|x|` over Kâˆˆ[0,10000]/alphaâˆˆ[0,2] from start `(mean(y at x==2),1)`, classify **open âں؛ alpha<1 / closed âں؛ alpha>1** (micropan verbatim, boundary not-open); exact oracles x=[2,3] y=[8,4]â†’alpha ln2/ln(3/2)â‰ˆ1.7095 Kâ‰ˆ26.164 closed, constant y=[1,1]â†’alpha 0 K 1 open, Tettelin 2005 qualitative anchor; the fitting engine whose alpha [[pan-genome-core-accessory-partition]] reports, consuming the families of [[pan-genome-gene-clustering]]; two assumptions (optimizer method non-correctness-affecting, fixed-seed RNG); no contradictions; record [[pangen-heap-001-evidence]].
- [[phylogenetic-marker-selection]] â€” comparative-genomics pan-genome family, fourth PANGEN-* unit (PANGEN-MARKER-001): **phylogenetic marker selection** `SelectPhylogeneticMarkers` + the `CountParsimonyInformativeSites` primitive â€” from gene clusters across N genomes pick **single-copy core genes** (present **exactly once in every genome**, panX; **core** = "at least 99% of samples", Roary; paralog clusters filtered out) that carry **variable positions**, then **rank by descending parsimony-informative-site count** capped at `maxMarkers`; a **parsimony-informative site** (Zvelebil & Baum 2008) = a column with â‰¥2 states, each in â‰¥2 sequences â†’ **monomorphic**/**singleton** columns score 0, a single-copy core cluster with **0 PIS** excluded; the input-selection step **upstream of** core-genome tree building (panXâ†’FastTree), makes no tree-accuracy claim (recombination caveat); oracles `AAAAA`/`AAACA`/`AACCG`/`ACCTG`â†’PIS 2 (cols 3,5), 3-genome selection excludes paralog/not-core/conserved; selects the single-copy subset of [[pan-genome-core-accessory-partition]], consumes families of [[pan-genome-gene-clustering]], single-copy-ortholog constraint shared with [[ortholog-detection-reciprocal-best-hits]]; one assumption (no in-repo aligner â†’ PIS over equal-length members, unequalâ†’PIS 0); no contradictions; record [[pangen-marker-001-evidence]].
- [[phylogenetic-bootstrap-support]] â€” the anchor for the **phylogenetics** `PHYLO-*` family (first PHYLO-* unit, PHYLO-BOOT-001): **Felsenstein's bootstrap** (Felsenstein 1985) â€” attach a **confidence to each clade** of an inferred tree by **resampling alignment columns (sites) with replacement** into same-length pseudo-alignments (taxa kept, characters resampled), rebuilding a tree per replicate (distance matrix â†’ UPGMA/NJ), and scoring each **non-terminal clade of the reference tree** by the **fraction of replicate trees containing a clade with the identical terminal-leaf-name set** (Biopython `get_support`; Lemoine 2018 "proportion of pseudo-trees containing that branch"); binary per-replicate, only reference-tree clades scored, support = `count/replicates`, thresholds 70%/95% descriptive; oracles two-group `AAAAAAAAAA`/`GGGGGGGGGG` UPGMA+JukesCantor seed 42 â†’ support{A,B}={C,D}=1.0, all-identical `ACGTACGT`â†’all clades 1.0; invariants supportâˆˆ[0,1] / determinism / keys=non-trivial reference clades / null/<2-seq/replicates<1 throw; the **first general distance-based-phylogenetics concept** in the wiki (no NJ/UPGMA/distance-matrix page yet), **distinct from** the CCF-constraint oncology builder [[tumor-phylogeny-clonal-tree-reconstruction]] (no distance matrix, no resampling) and a confidence layer over the tree the marker selector [[phylogenetic-marker-selection]] feeds; two source-consistent assumptions (rooted-clade scoring vs unrooted bipartitions matching Biopython, proportion [0,1] vs percentage أ—100); no contradictions; record [[phylo-boot-001-evidence]].
- [[tree-comparison-metrics]] â€” the second phylogenetics `PHYLO-*` unit (PHYLO-COMP-001): **tree comparison** â€” three operations on an already-built rooted binary `PhyloNode` tree. **Robinsonâ€“Foulds distance** (`RobinsonFouldsDistance` = symmetric difference `A+B` of the two trees' canonical split/bipartition sets, Robinson & Foulds 1981; raw count, proper metric, **even**, rooted-clade = Wikipedia dummy-leaf-at-root; **max RF = 2(nâˆ’2) rooted vs 2(nâˆ’3) unrooted**), **MRCA** (`FindMRCA`, deepest common ancestor, O(n) recursive leaf-name match, not-in-treeâ†’null), **patristic distance** (`PatristicDistance` = `dist(x,MRCA)+dist(y,MRCA)` branch-length sum, not-in-treeâ†’NaN, zero-branchesâ†’0); invariants RF identity/symmetric/â‰¥0/even, MRCA symmetric/always-ancestor/unique, patristic PD(x,x)=0/symmetric/â‰¥0; scope rooted-binary-only (two آ§7 decisions); the deterministic **compare** counterpart to the resampling-confidence [[phylogenetic-bootstrap-support]] (agreement vs disagreement of the same split primitive, no resampling), distinct from [[tumor-phylogeny-clonal-tree-reconstruction]]; no deviations, no contradictions; record [[phylo-comp-001-evidence]].
- [[evolutionary-distance-matrix]] â€” the third phylogenetics `PHYLO-*` unit (PHYLO-DIST-001): the **pairwise evolutionary-distance** primitive emitting the symmetric *nأ—n* matrix distance-based tree building (NJ/UPGMA) consumes â€” `CalculatePairwiseDistance`/`CalculateDistanceMatrix` over four methods **Hamming** (raw diff count) / **p-distance** (`differences/comparableSites`, uncorrected) / **Jukesâ€“Cantor JC69** (`-3/4آ·ln(1âˆ’4p/3)`, equal-base/equal-rate) / **Kimura-2-parameter K2P** (`-1/2آ·ln((1âˆ’2Sâˆ’V)آ·âˆڑ(1âˆ’2V))`, S=transition/V=transversion); matrix symmetric / zero-diagonal / non-negative / *nأ—n*, correction ordering **JC69â‰¥p & K2Pâ‰¥p**, triangle inequality expected-not-guaranteed; **pairwise deletion** (gaps + ambiguous IUPAC N/R/Y skipped, only A,C,G,T compared), case-insensitive; **saturation** JC69â†’+âˆ‍ at pâ‰¥3/4 / K2Pâ†’+âˆ‍ at Vâ‰¥1/2, all-gap/emptyâ†’0 (`0/nâ†’0`), unequal-lengthâ†’ArgumentException, nullâ†’ArgumentNullException; oracles `ACGTACGT`/`TCGTACGT`â†’Hamming 1/p 0.125/JC69â‰ˆ0.137, pure-transition `GCGT` K2Pâ‰ˆ0.34657 vs pure-transversion `CCGT`â‰ˆ0.31713, mixedâ‰ˆ0.30679, gapâ†’7 comparable sites; the **upstream substrate** the family sits on â€” [[phylogenetic-bootstrap-support]] resamples + re-runs it per replicate, [[tree-comparison-metrics]] compares the trees it feeds; distinct from the column-selecting [[phylogenetic-marker-selection]] and the distance-matrix-free [[tumor-phylogeny-clonal-tree-reconstruction]]; two API-contract assumptions (empty/all-gapâ†’0, pairwise deletion); no contradictions; record [[phylo-dist-001-evidence]].
- [[tree-statistics]] â€” a phylogenetics `PHYLO-*` unit (PHYLO-STATS-001): **whole-tree descriptive statistics** read off a single rooted binary `PhyloNode` â€” `GetLeaves` (terminal nodes, no children; count via `.Count()` = Biopython `count_terminals`), `CalculateTreeLength` (**total tree length = خ£ all branch lengths**; undefined/default 0 branch â†’ 0; the minimum-evolution quantity, Rzhetsky & Nei 1992; Biopython `total_branch_length`/DendroPy `Tree.length()`), `GetTreeDepth` (**tree height = edges on the longest root-to-leaf path**, counts edges not nodes; single-node 0; empty tree âˆ’1); oracles balanced `((A:1,B:1):1,(C:1,D:1):1)`â†’4/6/2, caterpillarâ†’4/5/3, single leafâ†’1/branch-len/0, null rootâ†’âˆ…/0/âˆ’1; the **descriptive-summary** sibling of the **compare/query** [[tree-comparison-metrics]] (its خ£-all-branches length is the whole-tree analogue of patristic distance's per-path sum), over the same `PhyloNode` [[phylogenetic-bootstrap-support]] resamples and [[evolutionary-distance-matrix]] feeds via UPGMA/NJ; one assumption (null `PhyloNode`â†”empty-tree convention); no deviations, no contradictions; record [[phylo-stats-001-evidence]].
- [[distance-based-tree-construction]] â€” the phylogenetics `PHYLO-*` **tree-building core** (PHYLO-TREE-001): the step that **consumes an [[evolutionary-distance-matrix]] and emits a `PhyloNode` tree** via two agglomerative methods on `PhylogeneticAnalyzer` (`BuildTree` from sequences / `BuildTreeFromMatrix` from a pre-computed matrix; returns `PhylogeneticTree` Root/Taxa/DistanceMatrix/Method). **UPGMA** (Sokal & Michener 1958) â€” rooted **ultrametric**, molecular-clock, nearest-pair merge, arithmetic-mean distance update, **height = d/2**, incremental branch lengths, O(nآ³)/O(nآ²). **Neighbor-Joining** (Saitou & Nei 1987) â€” **unrooted** (midpoint-rooted final join preserving patristic distances), clock-free, join the **minimum-Q** pair `Q(i,j)=(nâˆ’2)آ·d(i,j)âˆ’خ£d(i,k)âˆ’خ£d(j,k)`, branch lengths `خ´(f,u)=d(f,g)/2+(خ£d(f,k)âˆ’خ£d(g,k))/(2(nâˆ’2))`, **correct topology for additive matrices**, **negative branches preserved (no clamping)**, O(nآ³); invariants INV-01..05 (all taxa leaves, binary, n leaves / nâˆ’1 internal, UPGMAâ‰¥0) + UPGMA ultrametric/rooted/height=d/2 + NJ additive-correct/may-be-negative/no-clock; oracles UPGMA 5S-rRNA â†’(a,b)@17â†’((a,b),e)@22â†’(c,d)@28â†’final@33 (root 16.5, all tips 16.5), NJ 5-taxon â†’Qâ‚پ(a,b)=âˆ’50, خ´(a,u)=2â€¦خ´(e,w)=1; the **hinge** of the family â€” downstream of [[evolutionary-distance-matrix]], wrapped per-replicate by [[phylogenetic-bootstrap-support]], its output compared/queried by [[tree-comparison-metrics]] and summarized by [[tree-statistics]], serialized by Newick ([[phylo-newick-001-evidence]]); distinct from [[tumor-phylogeny-clonal-tree-reconstruction]] (no distance matrix) and [[phylogenetic-marker-selection]] (selects columns, builds no tree); no deviations, no contradictions; record [[phylo-tree-001-evidence]].
- [[bed-format-parsing]] â€” FileIO file-parsing `PARSE-*` family anchor (first PARSE-* unit, PARSE-BED-001): UCSC **BED** interval parsing keyed on the **0-based half-open** coordinate model (`chromStart` 0-based / `chromEnd` 1-based-exclusive, length `chromEndâˆ’chromStart`, `chromStart==chromEnd` = zero-length insertion; contrast 1-based GFF/GTF/VCF), the **BED3â†’BED12** column ladder (`chrom`/`chromStart`/`chromEnd` + optional `name`/`score`/`strand`/`thick*`/`itemRgb`/`block*`), and the UCSC validation rules (`chromStart â‰¤ chromEnd` else null, score clamp [0,1000], strand âˆˆ +/âˆ’/., first-line column-count lock, BED12 first-blockStart-0 / blockCount = array lengths / no-overlap / last-block-reaches-end); the malformed-input target of [[fuzzing]]; deviations None (rules verbatim from UCSC FAQ + Wikipedia); record [[parse-bed-001-evidence]].
- [[phred-quality-encoding]] â€” the FASTQ quality-score encoding concept (shared by FileIO parsing + Assembly trimming): Phred score `Q=âˆ’10آ·logâ‚پâ‚€(p)` / `p=10^(âˆ’Q/10)`, the +10-Q=10أ—-fewer-errors ladder (Q20/Q30 QC thresholds), the two live ASCII offsets **Phred+33** (Sanger/Illumina 1.8+, ASCII 33â€“126, Q0â€“93) vs **Phred+64** (Illumina 1.3â€“1.7, ASCII 64â€“126, Q0â€“62) with boundary chars (`!`=Q0/`I`=Q40/`~`=Q93 vs `@`=Q0/`h`=Q40/`~`=Q62), deterministic per-record offset auto-detection (`<'@'`â†’+33, high-bandâ†’+64, ambiguous `@`â€“`I`â†’default +33), why a mis-detected offset silently corrupts all downstream Q-stats/trim/filter, and **cross-variant conversion** as a pure آ±31 re-offset (score invariant; Phred+64â†’Phred+33 always safe, Phred+33â†’Phred+64 overflows for Q>62); anchored on the primary FASTQ spec **Cock et al. 2010**; traced by [[parse-fastq-001-evidence]] and the dedicated Phred-handling unit [[quality-phred-001-evidence]], reused by [[quality-trimming-running-sum]].
- [[fastq-quality-statistics]] â€” the FASTQ **quality-statistics** surface (QUALITY-STATS-001), **distinct from and downstream of** [[phred-quality-encoding]] (which the encoding concept explicitly flags as a separate surface): summary/QC scalars over the **decoded** per-base Phred scores â€” **mean** (arithmetic mean of scores, *not* error-probability-averaged), **median** (odd = middle, **even = mean of the two central order statistics**), **min/max**, **population variance/std dev** (`دƒآ²=(1/N)خ£(Qلµ¢âˆ’خ¼)آ²`, **أ·N not Nâˆ’1** â€” the quality string is the complete population), and the **`% â‰¥ Q20` / `% â‰¥ Q30`** fractions with **inclusive `â‰¥`** thresholds (Illumina: `% â‰¥ Q30` the NGS run-quality benchmark); **encoding-independent** (operates on decoded scores, so Phred+64 with the same scores gives identical stats â€” **consumes** the decode contract of [[quality-phred-001-evidence]] / [[phred-quality-encoding]]); `CalculateQ30Percentage` == `CalculateStatistics(...).PercentAboveQ30`; oracles `5?I`â†’20/30/40 mean 30.0/median 30/var 200/3/دƒâ‰ˆ8.16497/%â‰¥Q20 100/%â‰¥Q30â‰ˆ66.67, even `5II?`â†’median 35.0, single `I`â†’دƒ=0; corner cases even/odd median, single-element دƒ=0, empty/null â†’ zeroed `QualityStatistics` (TotalBases=0); record [[quality-stats-001-evidence]].
- [[insdc-feature-location]] â€” the shared INSDC (DDBJ/ENA/GenBank) feature-table **location-descriptor** grammar underlying both GenBank and EMBL flat files (same location string, different line syntax): 1-based-inclusive coordinates (contrast BED 0-based), descriptors `n..m`/single `n`/between-bases `n^m`/`<`/`>` partials/`complement`/`join`/`order`/`complement(join(â€¦))` with the no-nested-join/order rule, remote refs `accession.version:span`; operator assembly semantics (`join`/`order` concatenate in order, `complement` reverse-complements, `complement(join(a,b))==join(complement(b),complement(a))`), offline-first caller-supplied remote resolver, `<`/`>`-verbatim-slice assumption; oracles `join(1..3,7..9)`/`ACGTACGTAC`â†’`ACGGTA`, `complement(Y.1:1..4)`â†’`GTTT`; traced jointly by [[parse-genbank-001-evidence]] and [[parse-embl-001-evidence]].
- [[ancestry-estimation-admixture]] â€” anchor for the **population-genetics** `POP-*` family (**first POP-\* unit**, POP-ANCESTRY-001): estimate an individual's **ancestry proportions Q** (genome fraction from each of K reference populations) from unlinked SNP genotypes via **supervised/projection ADMIXTURE** â€” reference allele frequencies **F fixed/known**, only Q estimated by EM. Alexander, Novembre & Lange 2009 model: genotype gâˆˆ{0,1,2}=allele-1 copy count, **log-likelihood Eq. 2** `L=خ£لµ¢خ£â±¼{gآ·ln(خ£_k qآ·f)+(2âˆ’g)آ·ln(خ£_k qآ·(1âˆ’f))}` under simplex `خ£_k q_ik=1`; **FRAPPE EM Eq. 4** `q^{n+1}=(1/2J)خ£â±¼[gآ·a_ijk+(2âˆ’g)آ·b_ijk]` (a/b = posteriors an allele-1/allele-2 copy came from k), EM monotone ascent, convergence Eq. 5 خ”L<خµ=10âپ»âپ´, O(IJKآ²); oracles symmetric K=2/J=2 f_A=[0.8,0.2]/f_B=[0.2,0.8] g=[2,0] â†’ one EM iter **(0.8,0.2) exactly** â†’ converges (1.0,0.0), single-SNP g=2â†’(0.9,0.1)/g=1â†’(0.5,0.5) uninformative-het/g=0â†’(0.1,0.9), identical panels uniform fixed point; INV simplex خ£_k q=1 & EM L non-decreasing, missing gâˆ‰{0,1,2} skipped, empty inputsâ†’empty; **label non-identifiability** (K! maxima under population relabeling) **pinned by fixed labelled reference panels** (ADMIXTURE manual آ§2.10/آ§2.14) so Q interpretable relative to supplied labels; scope = estimate-Q-given-fixed-F only (does NOT jointly learn F, run unsupervised block-relaxation, choose K, or model linkage); **distinct from** the tree-building phylogenetics `PHYLO-*` family ([[distance-based-tree-construction]], [[evolutionary-distance-matrix]]) â€” a mixture-weight/EM decomposition of one admixed individual, not a tree; two research-grade assumptions (maxIterations budget + خµ convergence; skip-missing); no contradictions; record [[pop-ancestry-001-evidence]].
- [[genetic-diversity-statistics]] â€” population-genetics `POP-*` family diversity-statistics unit (**second POP-\* unit**, POP-DIV-001, sibling of the anchor [[ancestry-estimation-admixture]]): four classical within-population variation scalars from an aligned sample (n seqs, length L, S segregating sites) â€” **nucleotide diversity د€** = خ£_{i<j} d_ij/(C(n,2)آ·L) (Nei & Li 1979, mean per-site pairwise differences), **Watterson's خ¸_W** = S/a_n with harmonic a_n = خ£_{i=1}^{nâˆ’1} 1/i (per-site S/(a_nآ·L); Watterson 1975), **Tajima's D** = (kج‚ âˆ’ S/a_1)/âˆڑ(e_1آ·S+e_2آ·S(Sâˆ’1)) (Tajima 1989 â€” normalized د€-vs-Watterson difference; **kج‚ = pairwise-difference COUNT not per-site د€**; Dâ‰ˆ0 neutral, D<0 excess rare allelesâ†’sweep/expansion, D>0 deficitâ†’balancing/contraction), and **heterozygosity/gene diversity** H_exp = (1/L)خ£(1âˆ’خ£pآ²) with unbiased haploid H_obs = n/(nâˆ’1)آ·H_exp â‰، د€ (Nei 1978); Wikipedia oracle n=5/L=20/S=4 â†’ kج‚=2.0/د€=0.1/S/a_1â‰ˆ1.92/خ¸_Wâ‰ˆ0.096/**Dâ‰ˆ0.273** (TD-C01/TD-C02); guards n<3â†’D undefinedâ†’0, S=0/monomorphicâ†’all 0, Varâ‰¤0â†’D=0, `CalculateTajimasD(kج‚,S,n)` expects kج‚ not د€; **distinct from** the anchor's ancestry-proportion EM (within-population *variation amount* vs *ancestry decomposition*), summary-only (no variant calling / phasing / recombination / Fu-Li / Fay-Wu); all formulae exact-match, no deviations; record [[pop-div-001-evidence]].
- [[allele-genotype-frequencies]] â€” **foundational** population-genetics `POP-*` primitive (POP-FREQ-001): turn per-locus **genotype counts** into **allele frequencies**, derive **minor allele frequency (MAF)**, and **filter variants by MAF** â€” the numeric substrate under the rest of the POP family (the fixed reference frequencies **F** of [[ancestry-estimation-admixture]] and the per-site `p_i` behind the heterozygosity term of [[genetic-diversity-statistics]] are exactly these quantities). Biallelic allele freq `p = f(AA)+آ½f(AB)` / `q = f(BB)+آ½f(AB)` via counts `total=2آ·(n_AA+n_AB+n_BB)`, `major=2آ·n_AA+n_AB`, `minor=2آ·n_BB+n_AB` (**INV `p+q=1`**, `major+minor=total`; oracle 49/42/9 â†’ 0.70/0.30); VCF/PLINK dosage `alt_freq = خ£g/(2n)`, `MAF = min(alt_freq, 1âˆ’alt_freq)` (**INV `0 â‰¤ MAF â‰¤ 0.5`**, symmetric â€” alt_freq 0.7 â†’ MAF 0.3; monomorphic â†’ 0; 50/50 â†’ 0.5); MAF filter = inclusive `[minMAF,maxMAF]` band with conventional HapMap/common(>0.05)-vs-rare(<0.05) thresholds; edge cases zero samplesâ†’(0,0), empty vectorâ†’MAF 0, **negative count â†’ `ArgumentOutOfRangeException`**; scope = biallelic counting/normalization only (no HWE test, no multiallelic, no phasing/imputation); no deviations/contradictions; record [[pop-freq-001-evidence]].
- [[population-differentiation-fst]] â€” population-genetics `POP-*` differentiation unit (POP-FST-001): measure **how differentiated populations are** â€” fraction of total variation due to between-population structure â€” from per-population allele frequencies (**consumes** [[allele-genotype-frequencies]]; distinct from within-sample [[genetic-diversity-statistics]] and from ancestry decomposition [[ancestry-estimation-admixture]]). **Wright 1965 variance Fst** `Fst = دƒ_Sآ²/(pBar(1âˆ’pBar))`, two-pop size-weighted `pBar=(n1آ·p1+n2آ·p2)/(n1+n2)` / `دƒ_Sآ²=(n1(p1âˆ’pBar)آ²+n2(p2âˆ’pBar)آ²)/(n1+n2)`, multi-locus **ratio-of-sums** `خ£دƒ_Sآ²/خ£het` â€” the **population parameter from known allele freqs**, explicitly **NOT** the Weir & Cockerham 1984 خ¸ estimator (no bias correction); **F-statistics** heterozygosity partition `Fis=1âˆ’Hi/Hs`/`Fit=1âˆ’Hi/Ht`/`Fst=1âˆ’Hs/Ht` with **exact** `(1âˆ’Fit)=(1âˆ’Fis)(1âˆ’Fst)`; INV Fstâˆˆ[0,1] (0=panmixia/1=fixed differences), Fisâˆˆ[âˆ’1,1] (negative under excess heterozygotes), pairwise matrix symmetric + zero diagonal, **not a metric** (fails triangle inequality); oracles fixed p1=1/p2=0â†’**1.0 exactly**, pop1=(.9,.8)/pop2=(.1,.2)â†’1/2, Cavalli-Sforza/Elhaik ref values, Hartl-Clark bands (0.05/0.15/0.25); edge cases denominator 0 (empty/both-fixed-same/monomorphic)â†’**return 0**; scope = Wright Fst + heterozygosity F-statistics only (no significance test, no bootstrap CI); no deviations/contradictions; record [[pop-fst-001-evidence]].
- [[hardy-weinberg-equilibrium-test]] â€” population-genetics `POP-*` unit (POP-HW-001): the **Hardy-Weinberg equilibrium chi-square test** â€” does a biallelic locus's observed genotype counts match the `pآ²/2pq/qآ²` proportions expected under random mating? **Consumes** genotype counts from [[allele-genotype-frequencies]] (POP-FREQ-001, whose scope explicitly leaves the HWE test here) and turns them into a **hypothesis test**. Estimate `p = (2آ·n_AA + n_Aa)/(2n)` / `q = 1âˆ’p`, expected counts `E = {pآ²n, 2pqn, qآ²n}`, **Pearson د‡آ² = خ£ (Oâˆ’E)آ²/E** over the 3 genotype classes, **df = 1** (`#genotypes âˆ’ #alleles = 3 âˆ’ 2`), p-value from chi-square CDF (lower-incomplete-gamma approx), default **خ± = 0.05** critical value **3.841**; returns `InEquilibrium`/`ChiSquare`/`PValue`. Oracles Ford moth (1469,138,5)â†’`pâ‰ˆ0.954`/`د‡آ²â‰ˆ0.83`â†’in-eq, perfect (25,50,25)â†’`د‡آ²=0`, excess-het (10,80,10)â†’`د‡آ²=36 â‰« 3.84`â†’out-of-eq; edge cases **zero samplesâ†’InEquilibrium true, PValue 1** (no evidence against Hâ‚€), monomorphicâ†’`د‡آ²=0`, **expected-0 term skipped** (div-by-zero guard); deviation causes non-random mating/selection/mutation/migration/drift/**genotyping error**; scope = biallelic chi-square only (no Wigginton 2005 **exact test**, no multiallelic); no deviations/contradictions; record [[pop-hw-001-evidence]].
- [[linkage-disequilibrium]] â€” population-genetics `POP-*` unit (POP-LD-001): **non-random association between alleles at two loci** â€” a **pairwise inter-locus** quantity distinct from per-locus counting ([[allele-genotype-frequencies]]), within-sample diversity ([[genetic-diversity-statistics]]), between-population differentiation ([[population-differentiation-fst]]), and the single-locus [[hardy-weinberg-equilibrium-test]]; **consumes** allele/haplotype frequencies from [[allele-genotype-frequencies]]. `D = p_AB âˆ’ p_Aآ·p_B` (Robbins 1918), normalized `D' = |D|/D_max` clamped [0,1] (Lewontin 1964, sign-branched `D_max`) and `rآ² = Dآ²/(p_Aآ·q_Aآ·p_Bآ·q_B)` (Hill & Robertson 1968); implemented **phase-free** via the diploid-frequency result `R_AB=r_AB` (Wright 1933) â€” `rآ²` = squared Pearson correlation of 0/1/2 genotype dosage vectors `Covآ²/(Varآ·Var)`, `D` recovered from `Cov_diploid=2D â‡’ D=Cov/2`; `FindHaplotypeBlocks` = simplified adjacent-pair Gabriel 2002 (consecutive `rآ² â‰¥ threshold`, default **0.7**, â‰¥2 variants); INV `0â‰¤rآ²â‰¤1`/`0â‰¤|D'|â‰¤1`, emptyâ†’`rآ²=0,D'=0`, monomorphic/zero-varianceâ†’`rآ²=0` (guarded div), distance+IDs preserved, blocks Startâ‰¤End/â‰¥2/non-overlapping/position-ordered; perfect correlation **and** perfect anti-correlation both â†’`rآ²=1`/`D'=1` (sign-blind); scope = two-biallelic-loci rآ²/D' + adjacent-pair blocks only (no full LD matrix, no phasing/EM, no LD-decay fit, no exact Gabriel CI); no deviations/contradictions; record [[pop-ld-001-evidence]].
- [[runs-of-homozygosity-inbreeding]] â€” population-genetics `POP-*` unit (POP-ROH-001): detect **long uninterrupted homozygous stretches** (**runs of homozygosity**, `FindROH`) in one individual and summarize their burden as the genomic inbreeding coefficient **F_ROH** â€” a **per-individual segment-detection** problem distinct from per-locus counting ([[allele-genotype-frequencies]]), within-sample diversity ([[genetic-diversity-statistics]]), between-population differentiation ([[population-differentiation-fst]]), two-locus [[linkage-disequilibrium]], and single-locus [[hardy-weinberg-equilibrium-test]]. **Window-free consecutive-runs** scan (Marras 2015 / detectRUNS): walk position-sorted 0/1/2 genotypes (1 = heterozygous = "opposite"), grow a run, **terminate** when opposite calls exceed `maxOppRun` (a few tolerated to absorb genotyping error) or an inter-SNP gap exceeds `maxGap` (breaks even an all-homozygous run); retain a stretch only if it passes **both** `minSNP` **and** `minLengthBps` (PLINK `--homozyg-snp 100` **and** `--homozyg-kb 1000`, one alone insufficient). **F_ROH = خ£L_roh / L_auto** (McQuillan 2008 verbatim; `L_auto` = SNP-covered autosome â‰ˆ2,674 Mb; r=0.86 vs pedigree; min-length lever â‰¥0.5/1.5/5 Mb, 1.5 Mb best); oracle خ£L_roh=20 Mb/L_auto=100 Mb â†’ **0.20**, whole-genome â†’ 1.0; INV each run once/Startâ‰¤End/SnpCount, one tolerated het keeps one run / het beyond splits, gap>maxGap breaks, below minSNP-or-minLength discarded, unsorted ordered internally, genotype 2 = homozygous, leading hets skipped, F_ROHâˆˆ[0,1]; two API-encoding assumptions (0/1/2 encoding; **missing-genotype handling out of scope** â€” no missing sentinel, non-`1` treated homozygous); scope = consecutive-runs scan + F_ROH only (no PLINK sliding-window scoring, no missing bounding, no LOD/model-based callers, no cohort ROH-island mapping); no deviations/contradictions; record [[pop-roh-001-evidence]].
- [[selection-scan-ihs-ehh]] â€” population-genetics `POP-*` unit (POP-SELECT-001): detect **recent positive selection** from **haplotype structure** â€” a selective sweep leaves an unusually long, low-diversity haplotype around the selected allele. A **haplotype-length/decay** statistic distinct from per-locus counting ([[allele-genotype-frequencies]]), within-sample diversity ([[genetic-diversity-statistics]]), between-population differentiation ([[population-differentiation-fst]]), single-locus [[hardy-weinberg-equilibrium-test]], pairwise [[linkage-disequilibrium]], and autozygosity [[runs-of-homozygosity-inbreeding]]; **consumes** derived/ancestral allele freqs from [[allele-genotype-frequencies]]. Pipeline **EHHâ†’iHHâ†’iHSâ†’scan**: `EHH_c=خ£C(n_h,2)/C(n_c,2)` (Sabeti 2002 / selscan Eq.3, decays 1â†’0 with distance), `iHH` = trapezoidal area under EHH both directions truncated at **EHH<0.05**, **unstandardized iHS = ln(iHH_A/iHH_D)** (Voight 2006, ancestral numerator), standardized to std-normal in derived-allele-freq bins, `ScanForSelection` = proportion `|iHS|>2` in ~50-SNP windows; **sign convention critical** â€” Voight (A/D) is the opposite of selscan (D/A), large negative iHS â‡’ long *derived* haplotype, balanced decay â‡’ iHSâ‰ˆ0; oracles rehh F1205400â†’**âˆ’1.978569274**, constructed panel iHH_A=10/iHH_D=40â†’ln(0.25)=**âˆ’1.386294361**; INV EHHâˆˆ[0,1] (1 single chromosome / 0 all-distinct), single-element binâ†’std iHS 0, Nâˆ’1 SD + 20 default 0.05 bins (overridable) affect magnitude only, throws on monomorphic core / null / empty / inconsistent length / invalid core allele / OOR coreIndex; scope = single-core iHS/EHH scan (no XP-EHH, no Fst-outlier or Tajima's-D scan, no genetic-map interpolation, no >200 kb gap masking); no deviations/contradictions; record [[pop-select-001-evidence]].
- [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]] â€” PCR primer-design `PRIMER-*` / MolTools family anchor (PRIMER-TM-001): the **self-/hetero-dimer melting temperature (Tm)** of two primers via the Primer3 `ntthal` **thermodynamic alignment** over the SantaLucia & Hicks 2004 unified **DNA nearest-neighbour** model â€” the **DNA** counterpart of the **RNA** Turner-2004 folding [[rna-base-pairing]] / [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]], distinct by modelling an intermolecular duplex at finite strand concentration. Duplex خ”Hآ°/خ”Sآ° = خ£ 10 Watson-Crick NN stacks + duplex-initiation + per-end terminal-Aآ·T-penalty + self-complementary symmetry; **bimolecular Tm** `خ”Hآ°آ·1000/(خ”Sآ°+Rآ·ln(C_T/x))âˆ’273.15` with **symmetry factor x=1 (reverse-complement palindrome) / x=4 (otherwise)**; **[Naâپ؛] entropy salt correction** `0.368آ·(N/2)آ·ln[Naâپ؛]` (Tm monotone in salt); the dimer DP finds the possibly-**non-contiguous** most-stable structure (internal mismatch/loop, single/multi-base bulge, `tstack2` terminal overhang), reproducing primer3-py 2.3.0 `calc_homodimer`/`calc_heterodimer` to machine precision (GCGCGCGC self x=1 Tm 40.0906 آ°C, TGCATGCATG/CATGCATGCA x=4 Tm 25.6596 آ°C, GCGCATGCGC 2أ—2 loop Tm 43.1572 آ°C); **no stable dimer** (poly-A) â†’ `structure_found=False` â†’ null/NaN, invalid input (null / <2 bases / non-ACGT) â†’ null/NaN; deviations none remaining after the 2026-06-25 full-ntthal-DP port. Also covers the **intramolecular hairpin self-folding** extension (same engine): stem NN stacks (`NnUnifiedParams`) + **Table 4 hairpin-loop خ”Gآ°37** (loop خ”Hآ°=0, خ”Sآ°=âˆ’خ”Gآ°37آ·1000/310.15) + Jacobson-Stockmayer large-loop, **unimolecular hairpin Tm Eq. 11 with NO concentration term** (Vallone & Benight concentration-independent), bimolecular init & terminal-Aآ·T penalty excluded, **bundled** special tri/tetraloop hairpin bonus tables (16 triloop / 76 tetraloop rows, applied in `calc_hairpin`, key incl. closing pair; oracle tetraloop GGGGCGAAAGCCCC Tm 85.0335 آ°C) plus the legacy opt-in caller increment (oracle GGGCTTTTGCCC Tm 68.6404 آ°C, poly-A â†’ null/NaN); Also covers the **per-oligo (single-strand) design Tm** path (Eq. 3 applied to a primer vs its own complement; opt-in NN Tm, legacy Wallace/Marmur-Doty unchanged default) with the **Owczarzy 2004** monovalent-quadratic and **Owczarzy 2008** divalent-Mgآ²âپ؛/dNTP 1/Tm salt corrections (Biopython `salt_correction` methods 5â€“7) and the internal-mismatch/dangling-end tables (`NnInternalMismatch`/`NnDanglingEnd`); records [[primer-tm-001-dimer-evidence]], [[primer-tm-001-hairpin-evidence]], [[primer-tm-001-nn-evidence]], [[primer-tm-001-special-loop-evidence]].
- [[primer3-weighted-penalty-objective]] â€” PCR primer-design `PRIMER-*` / MolTools family (PRIMER-TM-001, **base** unit): the **Primer3 weighted per-primer penalty / objective function** `p_obj_fn` â€” the *only* score Primer3 sorts candidate primers by (**lower is better**), a **selection/scoring** algorithm distinct from the thermodynamic sibling [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]] (Tm enters only as one input *term*). Weighted sum of **sign-gated one-sided deviations** from each parameter optimum: Tm `temp_gtآ·(Tmâˆ’opt_tm)`/`temp_ltآ·(opt_tmâˆ’Tm)`, GC% (percent 0â€“100) `gc_content_gt/lt`, size `length_gt/lt`, plus non-thermodynamic `compl_anyآ·self_any + compl_endآ·self_end + num_nsآ·#N`; left/right primers identical (`p_args`). Defaults `opt_tm=60`/`opt_size=20`, weights `temp_*=length_*=1` and `gc/self/num_ns=0` (GC optimum undefined in header) â‡’ **default objective collapses to `|Tmâˆ’60|+|lenâˆ’20|`**; sign-gated (term=0 exactly at optimum), weight-zero short-circuit, penalty â‰¥ 0 with **0 iff all-optimal**; `self_any`/`self_end` are caller-supplied Primer3 `dpal` local-alignment scores (arithmetic exact, value external, vanish under default 0 weights); oracles (60,20)â†’0.0/(63,20)â†’3.0/(57,18)â†’5.0/combinedâ†’8.0; record [[primer-tm-001-evidence]].
- [[taqman-probe-design-rules]] â€” **PROBE** family anchor (PROBE-DESIGN-001): the **TaqMan (5'-nuclease hydrolysis-probe) design rules** â€” an opt-in extension over the unchanged generic hybridization-probe designer, a distinct MolTools reagent-design algorithm alongside the primer units [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]] / [[primer3-weighted-penalty-objective]]. The probe-specific hard constraints (no analogue in primer selection): **no G at the 5' end** (a 5'-G quenches the reporter dye *even after cleavage*, so it cannot be rescued â€” hard rule; `SelectTaqManStrand` moves the design to the complement/antisense strand when a compliant sense probe is impossible), **more Cs than Gs**, **no run of â‰¥4 consecutive Gs** (flagged separately from the generic homopolymer cap), **G+C 30â€“80%**, **length 18â€“22 nt** (default, `minLength`/`maxLength` parameterised â€” ABI/PREMIER 18â€“22 vs IDT/Thermo up to 30), and the **probe Tm â‰¥ primer Tm + 10 آ°C** gate (so the probe binds before Taq reaches it) with the primer Tm caller-supplied and the probe Tm via the PRIMER-TM-001-validated salt-adjusted `81.5+16.6آ·logâ‚پâ‚€[Naâپ؛]+41آ·GCâˆ’600/N` formula (not a TaqMan-specific nearest-neighbour calc); a `NoGuanineAt5Prime`/`PassesAll`-style checker; oracles CCATCACCCTACATCACC passes-all (primerTm â‰¤ 39.35), 5'-G/GGGG-run/more-G-than-C/len<18/GC-100% each fail, sense GTTAGGGTTAGGGTTAGG â†’ RC CCTAACCCTAACCCTAAC strand selection; two parameterisation assumptions (18â€“22 default window, repository salt-adjusted Tm engine), no source contradictions; record [[probe-design-001-evidence]].
- [[probe-offtarget-specificity-scan]] â€” **PROBE** family (PROBE-VALID-001): the **hybridization-probe off-target specificity scan** â€” align a candidate probe against a pooled reference with a **gapped Smithâ€“Waterman local alignment** and report every site whose identity clears a threshold. The **specificity-checking sibling** of [[taqman-probe-design-rules]] (composition rules), a genuinely distinct algorithm. Core improvement over the earlier **ungapped Hamming scan**: SW's gap-length maxima + **zero floor** (Smith & Waterman 1981) make it *local* and **indel-aware**, so an off-target reachable only through an insertion/deletion (which frame-shifts every downstream base and hides from a fixed window) is found â€” the **gapped-vs-ungapped BLAST** improvement (Altschul 1990â†’1997), realized as an *exact* full SW scan (not seed-and-extend). Zero-floor traceback **trims a mismatched tail** so identity is over the matched core. Off-target call at **â‰¥0.75 identity** (Kane et al. 2000 microarray cross-hyb threshold; `minIdentity` caller-configurable). On/off labelling (assumption): the first perfect ungapped full-coverage exact match = intended on-target, all else off-target. Opt-in **Karlinâ€“Altschul** significance (`ComputeLambdaNucleotide`/`ComputeKarlinAltschul`): `E=Kآ·mآ·nآ·e^(âˆ’خ»S)`, خ» = root of `خ£ p_i p_j e^(خ» s_ij)=1`, bit `S'=(خ»Sâˆ’ln K)/ln 2`, `E=mآ·nآ·2^(âˆ’S')`, preconditions expected-score<0 + a positive score, K caller-supplied; +1/âˆ’3 uniform-0.25 â†’ خ»=1.3740631 (â‰ˆ blastn 1.37), example bit 59.9627 / E 1.7802eâˆ’14. Oracles: exact + indel `ACGTAC-GTACGT` 12/12=1.0 (gapped finds, ungapped misses), indel+mismatch trimmed to 10/12=0.8333 (in @0.75, out @0.90); BLAST DNA scoring +2/âˆ’3 gap âˆ’2. No source contradictions; record [[probe-valid-001-evidence]].
- [[restriction-enzyme-filtering]] â€” **RESTR** family anchor (RESTR-FILTER-001): filtering/selecting a restriction-enzyme **library** by properties of the cut (not searching a sequence for cut sites) â€” a MolTools reagent-selection algorithm alongside [[codon-optimization]] and the primer/probe units. Two filter axes: (1) **end type** â€” every Type II end is either **blunt** (center cut, both strands terminate in a base pair) or **sticky** (staggered cut, 5'/3' overhang), a **total, disjoint partition** (`GetBluntCutters()` âˆھ `GetStickyCutters()` = full library, no third category, blunt-blunt always compatible); (2) **recognition-site length** â€” `GetEnzymesByCutLength(min, max)` over the **inclusive** `[min,max]` interval, undivided Type II sites canonically **4â€“8 nt**. Blunt: SmaI/EcoRV/AluI/HaeIII; sticky: EcoRI(5')/KpnI(3')/PstI(3')/NotI/TaqI. Invariants: partition totality+disjointness; inclusive bounds (API-shape assumption); single-length overload == range at `min==max`; `min>max`/negative/zeroâ†’empty; the **interrupted palindrome** SfiI (`GGCCNNNN^NGGCC`, 13 nt) is sticky but correctly **excluded** by `[4,8]` (undivided sites only). Sources Wikipedia sticky/blunt + restriction enzyme + cutting-site list + NEB/REBASE + PMC; record [[restr-filter-001-evidence]].
